<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the person who applied for or was granted leave</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the company</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>any other party to the proceedings or application.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

An order under this section may require indemnification for costs.

4  After Chapter 2K

Insert: 

Chapter 2L&#151;Debentures
 Part 2L.1&#151;Requirement for trust deed and trustee

260FA  Requirement for trust deed and trustee

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>Before a body:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>makes an offer of debentures in this jurisdiction that needs disclosure to

investors under Chapter 6D, or does not need disclosure to investors under

Chapter 6D because of subsection 708(14) (disclosure document exclusion for

debenture roll overs); or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>makes an offer of debentures in this jurisdiction or elsewhere as

consideration for the acquisition of securities under an off-market takeover

bid; or</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>issues debentures in this jurisdiction or elsewhere under a compromise or

arrangement under Part 5.1 approved at a meeting held as a result of an order

under subsection 411(1) or (1A);

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

regardless of where any resulting issue, sale or transfer occurs, the body must enter into a trust deed that complies with section 260FB and appoint a trustee that complies with section 260FC.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	For rules about when an offer of debentures will need

disclosure to investors under Chapter 6D, see sections 706, 707 and 708.

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>The body may revoke the trust deed after it has repaid all amounts payable

under the debentures in accordance with the debentures' terms and the trust

deed.</dd> <dt>(3)</dt><dd>The body must comply with this Chapter. </dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Sections 168 and 601CZB require a register of debenture

holders to be set up and kept.

 </dl></dl>

260FB  Trust deed

<dl compact="">

		The trust deed must provide that the following are held in trust by the

trustee for the benefit of the debenture holders:

 </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the right to enforce the borrower's duty to repay </dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>any charge or security for repayment </dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the right to enforce any other duties that the borrower and any guarantor

have under:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>the terms of the debentures; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>the provisions of the trust deed or this Chapter.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	For information about the duties that the borrower and any

guarantor body have under this Chapter, see sections 260GB to 260HE.

 </dl></dl>

260FC  Who can be a trustee

_Who can be trustee_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>The trustee must be:

</dd> </dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the Public Trustee of any State or Territory; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>a body corporate authorised by a law of any State or Territory to take in

its own name a grant of probate of the will, or letters of administration of

the estate, of a deceased person; or</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>a body corporate registered under the _Life Insurance Act 1995_; or</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>an Australian ADI; or</dd>

<dt>(e)</dt><dd>a body corporate, all of whose shares are held beneficially by a body

corporate or bodies corporate of the kind referred to in paragraph (b), (c) or

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>if that body or those bodies:

</dd></dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>are liable for all of the liabilities incurred, or to be incurred, by the

trustee as trustee; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>have subscribed for and beneficially hold shares in the trustee and there

is an uncalled liability of at least $500,000 in respect of those shares that

can only be called up if the trustee becomes an externally-administered body

corporate (see section 254N); or

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(f)</dt><dd>a body corporate approved by ASIC (see section 260MB).

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Section 260GD provides that if the borrower becomes aware

that the trustee cannot be a trustee, the trustee must be replaced.

 </dl></dl>

_Circumstances in which a person cannot be trustee_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>A person may only be appointed or act as trustee (except to the extent

provided for by section 260FD) if the appointment or acting will not result in

a conflict of interest or duty. This subsection is not intended to affect any

rule of law or equity.

</dd> </dl>

260FD  Existing trustee continues to act until new trustee takes office

<dl compact="">

		An existing trustee continues to act as the trustee until a new trustee is

appointed and has taken office as trustee, despite any rule of law or equity to

the contrary.

 </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	This section applies even if the existing trustee resigns.

 </dl></dl>

260FE  Replacement of trustee

_Related party of existing trustee may be appointed as a new trustee_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>In addition to any other powers of appointment under the terms of the

debentures or provisions of the trust deed, the borrower may appoint a body

corporate that is related to the existing trustee as trustee in place of the

existing trustee if:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the body corporate can be a trustee under section 260FC; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the existing trustee consents in writing to the appointment _._

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

The appointment has effect despite any terms of the debentures or provisions of the trust deed.

_Appointment by Court_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>The Court may:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>appoint a person who may be a trustee under section 260FC as trustee on

the application of the borrower, a debenture holder or ASIC if:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>a trustee has not been validly appointed; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>the trustee has ceased to exist; or

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>terminate the existing trustee's appointment and appoint a person who may

be a trustee under section 260FC as trustee in the existing trustee's place on

the application of the borrower, the existing trustee, a debenture holder or

ASIC if:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>the existing trustee cannot be trustee under section 260FC; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>the existing trustee fails, or refuses, to act.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

Part 2L.2&#151;Duties of borrower

260GA  Duties of borrower

<dl compact="">

		A borrower that is required to enter into a trust deed under section 260FA

has the duties imposed by this Part.

 </dl>

260GB  General duties

<dl compact="">

		The borrower must:

 </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>carry on and conduct its business in a proper and efficient manner; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>provide a copy of the trust deed to:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>a debenture holder; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>the trustee;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		if they request a copy; and

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>make all of its financial and other records available for inspection by:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>the trustee; or </dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>an officer or employee of the trustee authorised by the trustee to carry

out the inspection; or</dd>

<dt>(iii)</dt><dd>a registered company auditor appointed by the trustee to carry out the

inspection;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		and give them any information, explanations or other assistance that they

require about matters relating to those records.

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	The borrower also has a duty to call a meeting of debenture

holders in certain circumstances (see section 260KA).

 </dl></dl>

260GC  Duty to notify ASIC of name of trustee

<dl compact="">

		The borrower must lodge with ASIC a notice of the name of a trustee within 14

days after they are appointed. The notice must be in the prescribed form.

 </dl>

260GD  Duty to replace trustee

<dl compact="">

		The borrower must take all reasonable steps to replace the trustee under

section 260FE as soon as practicable after the borrower becomes aware that the

trustee:

 </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>has ceased to exist; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>has not been validly appointed; or</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>cannot be a trustee under section 260FC; or</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>has failed or refused to act as trustee.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

260GE  Duty to inform trustee about charges

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact="">

		If the borrower creates a charge, it must:

 </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>give the trustee written details of the charge within 21 days after it is

created; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>if the total amount to be advanced on the security of the charge is

indeterminate and the advances are not merged in a current account with

bankers, trade creditors or anyone else&#151;give the trustee written details of

the amount of each advance within 7 days after it is made.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	If the advances are merged in a current account the

borrower must give the trustee the details in the quarterly report (see

subsection 260GF(4)).

 </dl></dl>

260GF  Duty to give trustee and ASIC quarterly reports

_Quarterly reports_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>Within 1 month after the end of each quarter, the borrower must:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>give the trustee a quarterly report that sets out the information required

by subsections (4), (5) and (6); and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>lodge a copy of the report with ASIC (see section 351).

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

_First quarter_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>The first quarter is the period of 3 months ending on a day fixed by the

borrower, by written notice to the trustee. The day must be less than 6 months

after the first issue of a debenture under the trust deed.

</dd> </dl>

_Subsequent quarters_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>Each of the subsequent quarters are periods of 3 months. The trustee may

allow a particular quarter to be a period of less than 3 months if the trustee

is satisfied that special circumstances justify doing so.

</dd> </dl>

_Content of quarterly report_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>The report for a quarter must include details of:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>any failure by the borrower and each guarantor to comply with the terms of

the debentures or the provisions of the trust deed or this Chapter during the

quarter; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>any event that has happened during the quarter that has caused, or could

cause, 1 or more of the following:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>any amount deposited or lent under the debentures to become immediately

payable</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>the debentures to become immediately enforceable</dd>

<dt>(iii)</dt><dd>any other right or remedy under the terms of the debenture or provisions

of the trust deed to become immediately enforceable; and

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>any circumstances that have occurred during the quarter that materially

prejudice:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>the borrower, any of its subsidiaries, or any of the guarantors; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>any security or charge included in or created by the debentures or the

trust deed; and

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>any substantial change in the nature of the business of the borrower, any

of its subsidiaries, or any of the guarantors that has occurred during the

quarter; and</dd>

<dt>(e)</dt><dd>any of the following events that happened in the quarter:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>the appointment of a guarantor</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>the cessation of liability of a guarantor body for the payment of the

whole or part of the money for which it was liable under the guarantee</dd>

<dt>(iii)</dt><dd>a change of name of a guarantor (if this happens, the report must also

disclose the guarantor's new name); and

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(f)</dt><dd>the net amount outstanding on any advances at the end of the quarter if

the borrower has created a charge where:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>the total amount to be advanced on the security of the charge is

indeterminate; and </dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>the advances are merged in a current account with bankers, trade

creditors or anyone else; and

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(g)</dt><dd>any other matters that may materially prejudice any security or the

interests of the debenture holders.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Paragraph (f)&#151;the borrower has a duty to inform the

trustee about charges as they are created (see section 260GE).

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(5)</dt><dd>If the borrower has deposited money with, or lent money to, a related body

corporate during the quarter, the report must also include details of:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the total of the money deposited with, or lent to, the related body

corporate during the quarter (see subsection (7)); and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the total amount of money owing to the borrower at the end of the quarter

in respect of the deposits or loans to the related body corporate.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

Disregard any amount that the borrower deposits with an ADI in the normal course of the borrower's business.

<dl compact="">

<dt>(6)</dt><dd>If the borrower has assumed a liability of a related body corporate during

the quarter, the report must also include details of the extent of the

liability assumed during the quarter and the extent of the liability as at the

end of the quarter.</dd> <dt>(7)</dt><dd>For the purposes of subsections (5) and (6), the report: </dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>must distinguish between deposits, loans and assumptions of liability that

are secured and those that are unsecured; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>may exclude any deposit, loan or assumption of liability on behalf of the

related body corporate if it has:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>guaranteed the repayment of the debentures of the borrower; and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>secured the guarantee by a charge over all of its property in favour of

the trustee.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

_Formalities_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(8)</dt><dd>The report must:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>be made in accordance with a resolution of the directors; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>specify the date on which the report is made.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

260GG  Exceptions

<dl compact="">

		Sections 260GE and 260GF do not apply in respect of the borrower while:

 </dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>it is under external administration; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>a receiver, or a receiver and manager, of property of the borrower has

been appointed and has not ceased to act under that appointment.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

260GH   How debentures may be described

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>The borrower may describe or refer to the debentures in:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>any disclosure in relation to the offer of the debentures; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>any other document constituting or relating to the offer of the

debentures; or</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the debentures themselves;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

only in accordance with the following table:

<table><tr align="left">
  <th colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>How debentures may be described</div>

  </th>
</tr>
<tr align="left">
  <th colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>Item</div>

  </th>
  <th colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>Description</div>

  </th>
  <th colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>When description may be used</div>

  </th>
</tr>
<tr align="left">
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>1</div>

  </td>
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>mortgage debenture</div>

  </td>
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>only if the circumstances set out in subsection (2) are satisfied</div>

  </td>
</tr>
<tr align="left">
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>2</div>

  </td>
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>debenture</div>

  </td>
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>only if the circumstances set out in subsection (2) or (3) are satisfied</div>

  </td>
</tr>
<tr align="left">
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>3</div>

  </td>
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>unsecured note or unsecured deposit note</div>

  </td>
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>in any other case</div>

  </td>
</tr></table>_When debentures can be called mortgage debentures or debentures_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>The borrower may describe or refer to the debentures as:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>mortgage debentures; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>debentures;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

if:

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the repayment of all money that has been, or may be, deposited or lent

under the debentures is secured by a first mortgage given to the trustee over

land vested in the borrower or in any of the guarantors; and</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>the mortgage has been registered, or is a registrable mortgage that has

been lodged for registration, in accordance with the law relating to the

registration of mortgages of land in the place where the land is situated;

and</dd>

<dt>(e)</dt><dd>the total amount of that money and of all other liabilities (if any)

secured by the mortgage of that land ranking equally  with the liability

to repay that money does not exceed 60% of the value of the borrower's or

guarantor's interest in that land as shown in the valuation included in the

disclosure document for the debentures.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

_When debentures can be called debentures_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>The borrower may describe or refer to the debentures as debentures if:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the repayment of all money that has been, or may be, deposited or lent

under the debentures has been secured by a charge in favour of the trustee over

the whole or any part of the tangible property of the borrower or of any of the

guarantors; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the tangible property that constitutes the security for the charge is

sufficient and is reasonably likely to be sufficient to meet the liability for

the repayment of all such money and all other liabilities that:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>have been or may be incurred; and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>rank in priority to, or equally  with, that liability.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

260GI  Offences for failure to comply with statutory duties

<dl compact="">

		The borrower commits an offence if it intentionally or recklessly contravenes

section 260GB, 260GC, 260GD, 260GE, 260GF or 260KA.

 </dl>

Part 2L.3&#151;Duties of guarantor

260HA  Duties of guarantor

<dl compact="">

		If a borrower is required to enter into a trust deed under section 260FA in

relation to debentures, a guarantor in respect of the debentures has the duties

imposed by this Part.

 </dl>

260HB  General duties

<dl compact="">

		The guarantor must:

 </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>carry on and conduct its business in a proper and efficient manner; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>make all of its financial and other records available for inspection by:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>the trustee; or </dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>an officer or employee of the trustee authorised by the trustee to carry

out the inspection; or</dd>

<dt>(iii)</dt><dd>a registered company auditor appointed by the trustee to carry out the

inspection;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		and give them any information, explanations or other assistance that they

require about matters relating to those records.

</dl></dl></dl>

260HC  Duty to inform trustee about charges

<dl compact="">

		If the guarantor creates a charge, it must:

 </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>give the trustee written details of the charge within 21 days after it is

created; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>if the total amount to be advanced on the security of the charge is

indeterminate, give the trustee written details of:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>the amount of each advance made within 7 days after it is made; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>where the advances are merged in a current account with bankers, trade

creditors or anyone else&#151;the net amount outstanding on the advances at the end

of every 3 months.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

260HD  Exceptions

<dl compact="">

		Section 260HC does not apply in respect of the guarantor while:

 </dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>it is under external administration; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>a receiver, or a receiver and manager, of property of the guarantor has

been appointed and has not ceased to act under that appointment.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

260HE  Offences for failure to comply with statutory duties

<dl compact="">

		The guarantor commits an offence if it intentionally or recklessly

contravenes paragraph 260HB(b) or section 260HC.

 </dl>

Part 2L.4&#151;Trustee

260JA  Trustee's duties

<dl compact="">

		The trustee of a trust deed entered into under section 260FA must:

 </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>exercise reasonable diligence to ascertain whether the property of the

borrower and of each guarantor that is or should be available (whether by way

of security or otherwise) will be sufficient to repay the amount deposited or

lent when it becomes due; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>exercise reasonable diligence to ascertain whether the borrower or any

guarantor has committed any breach of:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>the terms of the debentures; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>the provisions of the trust deed or this Chapter; and

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>do everything in its power to ensure that the borrower or a guarantor

remedies any breach known to the trustee of:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>any term of the debentures; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>any provision of the trust deed or this Chapter;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		unless the trustee is satisfied that the breach will not materially prejudice

the debenture holders' interests or any security for the debentures; and

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>ensure that the borrower and each guarantor complies with Part 2K to the

extent that it applies to the debentures; and</dd>

<dt>(e)</dt><dd>notify ASIC as soon as practicable if:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>the borrower has not complied with section 260GE, 260GF or subsection

318(1) or (4); or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>a guarantor has not complied with section 260HC; and

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(f)</dt><dd>notify ASIC and the borrower as soon as practicable if the trustee

discovers that it cannot be a trustee under section 260FC; and</dd>

<dt>(g)</dt><dd>give the debenture holders a statement explaining the effect of any

proposal that the borrower submits to the debenture holders before any meeting

that:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>the Court calls in relation to a scheme under subsection 411(1) or (1A);

or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>the trustee calls under subsection 260KB(1); and

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(h)</dt><dd>comply with any directions given to it at a debenture holders' meeting

referred to in section 260KA, 260KB or 260KC unless:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>the trustee is of the opinion that the direction is inconsistent with the

terms of the debentures or the provisions of the trust deed or this Law or is

otherwise objectionable; and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>has either obtained, or is in the process of obtaining, an order from the

Court under section 260NA setting aside or varying the direction; and

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>apply to the Court for an order under section 260NB if the borrower

requests it to do so.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note 1:	Paragraph (g)&#151;Section 411 relates to compromises and

arrangements. Note 2:	Section 260JC deals with indemnification in respect of a trustee's liability to the debenture holders.  </dl></dl>

260JB  Exemptions and indemnifications of trustee from liability

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>A term of a debenture, provision of a trust deed or a term of a contract

with holders of debentures secured by a trust deed, is void in so far as the

term or provision would have the effect of:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>exempting a trustee from liability for breach of section 260JA for failure

to show the degree of care and diligence required of it as trustee; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>indemnifying the trustee against that liability;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

unless the term or provision:

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>releases the trustee from liability for something done or omitted to be

done before the release is given; or</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>enables a meeting of debenture holders to approve the release of the

trustee from liability for something done or omitted to be done before the

release is given.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>For the purposes of paragraph (1)(d):

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>a release is approved if the debenture holders who vote for the resolution

hold 75% of the nominal value of the debentures held by all the debenture

holders who attend the meeting and vote on the resolution; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>a debenture holder attends the meeting and votes on the resolution if:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>they attend the meeting in person and vote on the resolution; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>if proxies are permitted&#151;they are represented at the meeting by a proxy

and the proxy votes on the resolution.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

260JC  Indemnity

<dl compact="">

		The trustee is not liable for anything done or omitted to be done in

accordance with a direction given to it by the debenture holders at any meeting

called under section 260KA, 260KB or 260KC.

 </dl>

Part 2L.5&#151;Meetings of debenture holders

260KA  Borrower's duty to call meeting

_Duty to call meeting_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>The borrower must call a meeting of debenture holders if:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>debenture holders who together hold 10% or more of the nominal value of

the issued debentures to which the trust relates direct the borrower to do so;

and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the direction is given to the borrower in writing at its registered

office; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the purpose of the meeting is to:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>consider the financial statements that were laid before the last AGM of

the borrower; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>give the trustee directions in relation to the exercise of any of its

powers.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	The trustee usually must comply with any directions given

to it by the debenture holders at the meeting (see paragraph 260JA(h)).

 </dl></dl>

_Duty to give notification of meeting_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>If the borrower is required to call a meeting, it must give notice of the

time and place of the meeting to:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the trustee; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the borrower's auditor; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>each of the debenture holders whose names are entered on the register of

debenture holders.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

Notice to joint holders of a debenture must be given to the joint holder named first in the register of debenture holders.

<dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>The borrower may give the notice to a debenture holder:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>personally; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>by sending it by post to the address for the debenture holder in the

register of debenture holders; or</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>by sending it to the fax number or electronic address (if any) nominated

by the debenture holder; or</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>by any other means that the trust deed or the terms of the debentures

permit.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	A defect in the notice may not invalidate a meeting (see

section 1322).

 </dl></dl>

_When notice by post or fax is given_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>A notice of meeting sent to a debenture holder is taken to be given:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>3 days after it is posted, if it is posted; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>on the business day after it is sent, if it is sent by fax or other

electronic means;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

unless the trust deed or the terms of the debentures provide otherwise.

260KB  Trustee's power to call meeting

_Trustee may call meeting in event of breach_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>If the borrower or a guarantor fails to remedy any breach of the terms of

the debentures or provisions of the trust deed or this Chapter when required by

the trustee, the trustee may:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>call a meeting of debenture holders; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>inform the debenture holders of the failure at the meeting; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>submit proposals for protection of the debenture holders' interests to the

meeting; and</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>ask for directions from the debenture holders in relation to the matter.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

_Trustee may appoint person to chair meeting_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>The trustee may appoint a person to chair a meeting of debenture holders

called under subsection (1). If the trustee does not exercise this power, the

debenture holders present at the meeting may appoint a person to chair the

meeting.

</dd> </dl>

260KC  Court may order meeting

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>Without limiting section 260NA or 260NB, the Court may make an order under

either of those sections for a meeting of all or any of the debenture holders

to be held to give directions to the trustee. The order may direct the trustee

to:

</dd> </dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>place before the debenture holders any information concerning their

interests; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>place before the debenture holders any proposals to protect their

interests that the Court directs or the trustee considers appropriate; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>obtain the debenture holders' directions concerning the protection of

their interests.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>The meeting is to be held and conducted in the manner the Court directs.

The trustee may appoint a person to chair the meeting. If the trustee does not

exercise this power, the debenture holders present at the meeting may appoint a

person to chair the meeting.

</dd> </dl>

Part 2L.6&#151;Civil liability

260L  Civil liability for contravening this Chapter

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>A person who suffers loss or damage because a person contravenes a

provision of this Chapter may recover the amount of the loss or damage from:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the person who contravened the provision; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>a person involved in the contravention.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

This is so even if the person did not commit, and was not involved in, the contravention.

<dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>An action under subsection (1) may begin at any time within 6 years after

the day on which the cause of action arose.</dd> <dt>(3)</dt><dd>This Part does not affect any liability that a person has under any other law. </dd> </dl>

Part 2L.7&#151;ASIC powers

260MA  ASIC's power to exempt and modify

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>ASIC may:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>exempt a person from a provision of this Chapter; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>declare that this Chapter applies to a person as if specified provisions

were omitted, modified or varied as specified in the declaration.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>The exemption or declaration may do all or any of the following:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>apply to all or specified provisions of this Chapter</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>apply to all persons, specified persons, or a specified class of persons</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>relate to all debentures, specified debentures or a specified class of

debentures</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>relate to any other matter generally or as specified.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>An exemption may apply unconditionally or subject to specified conditions.

A person to whom a condition specified in an exemption applies must comply with

the condition. The Court may order the person to comply with the condition  in a specified way. Only ASIC may apply to the Court for the

order.</dd> <dt>(4)</dt><dd>The exemption or declaration must be in writing and ASIC must publish notice of it in the _Gazette_.</dd> <dt>(5)</dt><dd>For the purposes of this section, the _provisions of this Chapter_ include: </dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>regulations made for the purposes of this Chapter; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>definitions in this Law or the regulations as they apply to references in:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>this Chapter; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>regulations made for the purposes of this Chapter; and

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>Division 12 of Part 11.2.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

260MB  ASIC may approve body corporate to be trustee

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>ASIC may approve a body corporate in writing to be a trustee for the

purposes of paragraph 260FC(1)(f). The approval may allow the body corporate to

act as trustee:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>in any circumstances; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>in relation to a particular borrower or particular class of borrower; or</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>in relation to a particular trust deed;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

and may be given subject to conditions.

<dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>ASIC must publish notice of the approval in the _Gazette_.

</dd> </dl>

Part 2L.8&#151;Court

260NA  General Court power to give directions and determine questions

<dl compact="">

		If the trustee applies to the Court for any direction in relation to the

performance of the trustee's functions or to determine any question in relation

to the interests of the debenture holders, the Court may give any direction and

make any declaration or determination in relation to the matter that the Court

considers appropriate. The Court may also make ancillary or consequential

orders.

 </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Under this section, the Court may order a meeting of

debenture holders to be held, see section 260KC.

 </dl></dl>

260NB  Specific Court powers

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>If the trustee or ASIC applies to the Court, the Court may make any or all

of the following orders:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>an order staying an action or other civil proceedings before a court by or

against the borrower or a guarantor body</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>an order restraining the borrower from paying any money to the debenture

holders or any holders of any other class of debentures</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>an order that any security for the debentures be enforceable immediately

or at the time the Court directs (even if the debentures are irredeemable or

redeemable only on the happening of a contingency)</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>an order appointing a receiver of any property constituting security for

the debentures</dd>

<dt>(e)</dt><dd>an order restricting advertising by the borrower for deposits or loans </dd>

<dt>(f)</dt><dd>an order restricting borrowing by the borrower</dd>

<dt>(g)</dt><dd>any other order that the Court considers appropriate to protect the

interests of existing or prospective debenture holders.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>In deciding whether to make an order under subsection (1), the Court must

have regard to:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the ability of the borrower and each guarantor to repay the amount

deposited or lent as and when it becomes due; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>any contravention of section 260MA by the borrower; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the interests of the borrower's members and creditors; and</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>the interests of the members of each of the guarantors.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	The Court may order a meeting of debenture holders to be

held (see section 260KC).

 </dl></dl>

Part 2L.9&#151;Location of other debenture provisions

260P  Signpost to other debenture provisions

<dl compact="">

		There are other rules relating to debentures in paragraph 124(1)(b) and

section 563AAA.

 </dl>

5  Chapter 6

Repeal the Chapter, substitute: 

Chapter 6&#151;Takeovers

602  Purposes of Chapter

<dl compact="">

		The purposes of this Chapter are to ensure that:

 </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the acquisition of control over:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>the voting shares in a listed company, or an unlisted company with more

than 50 members; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>the voting shares in a listed body; or</dd>

<dt>(iii)</dt><dd>the voting interests in a listed managed investment scheme;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		takes place in an efficient, competitive and informed market; and

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the holders of the shares or interests, and the directors of the company

or body or the responsible entity for the scheme:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>know the identity of any person who proposes to acquire a substantial

interest in the company, body or scheme; and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>have a reasonable time to consider the proposal; and</dd>

<dt>(iii)</dt><dd>are given enough information to enable them to assess the merits of the

proposal; and

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>as far as practicable, the holders of the relevant class of voting shares

or interests all have a reasonable and equal opportunity to participate in any

benefits accruing to the holders through any proposal under which a person

would acquire a substantial interest in the company, body or scheme; and</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>an appropriate procedure is followed as a preliminary to compulsory

acquisition of voting shares or interests or any other kind of securities under

Part 6A.1.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note 1:	To achieve the objectives referred to in paragraphs (a),

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>and (c), the prohibition in section 606 and the exceptions to it refer to

interests in "voting shares". To achieve the objective in paragraph (d), the

provisions that deal with the takeover procedure refer more broadly to

interests in "securities".</dd> Note 2:	Subsection 92(3) defines _securities_ for the purposes of this Chapter.  </dl></dl>

603  Chapter extends to some listed bodies that are not companies

<dl compact="">

		This Chapter applies to the acquisition of relevant interests in the

securities of listed bodies that are not companies but are incorporated or

formed in this jurisdiction in the same way as it applies to the acquisition of

relevant interests in the securities of companies.

 </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Section 9 defines _company_,

_jurisdiction_ and _listed_.

 </dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

604  Chapter extends to listed managed investment schemes

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>This Chapter applies to the acquisition of relevant interests in the

interests in a listed managed investment scheme registered in this jurisdiction

as if:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the scheme were a listed company; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>interests in the scheme were shares in the company; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>voting interests in the scheme were voting shares in the company; and</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>a meeting of the members of the scheme were a general meeting of the

company; and</dd>

<dt>(e)</dt><dd>the obligations and powers that are imposed or conferred on the company

were imposed or conferred on the responsible entity; and</dd>

<dt>(f)</dt><dd>the directors of the responsible entity were the directors of the company;

and</dd>

<dt>(g)</dt><dd>the appointment of a responsible entity for the scheme were the election

of a director of the company; and</dd>

<dt>(h)</dt><dd>the scheme's constitution were the company's constitution.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note 1:	Paragraph (g): See subsection 610(2). Note 2:	Section 9 defines _voting interest_ in a managed investment scheme.  </dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>The regulations may modify the operation of this Chapter as it applies in

relation to the acquisition of interests in listed managed investment schemes.

</dd> </dl>

605  Classes of securities

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>Takeover bids are made for securities within a particular class.

Similarly, compulsory acquisition and buy-out rights operate on securities

within a particular class.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>For the purposes of this Chapter and Chapters 6A and 6C, securities are not to be taken to be different classes merely because: </dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>some of the securities are fully-paid and others are partly-paid; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>different amounts are paid up or remain unpaid on the securities.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

Part 6.1&#151;Prohibited acquisitions of relevant interests in voting shares

606  Prohibition on certain acquisitions of relevant interests in voting shares

_Acquisition of relevant interests in voting shares through transaction entered into by or on behalf of person acquiring relevant interest_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>A person must not acquire a relevant interest in issued voting shares in a

company if:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the company is:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>a listed company; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>an unlisted company with more than 50 members; and

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the person acquiring the interest does so through a transaction in

relation to securities entered into by or on behalf of the person; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>because of the transaction, that person's or someone else's voting power

in the company increases:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>from 20% or below to more than 20%; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>from a starting point that is above 20% and below 90%.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

However, the person may acquire the relevant interest under one of the exceptions set out in section 611 without contravening this subsection.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note 1:	Section 9 defines _company_ as meaning a

company incorporated, or taken to have been incorporated, in this

jurisdiction. Note 2:	Section 607 deals with the effect of a contravention of this section on transactions. Sections 608 and 609 deal with the meaning of _relevant_ _interest_. Section 610 deals with the calculation of a person's voting power in a company. Note 3:	If the acquisition of relevant interests in an unlisted company with 50 or fewer members leads to the acquisition of a relevant interest in another company that is an unlisted company with more than 50 members, or a listed company, the acquisition is caught by this section because of its effect on that other company.  </dl></dl>

_Acquisition of legal or equitable interest giving rise to relevant interest for someone else_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>A person must not acquire a legal or equitable interest in securities of a

body corporate if, because of the acquisition:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>another person acquires a relevant interest in issued voting shares in a

company that is:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>a listed company; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>an unlisted company with more than 50 members; and

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>someone's voting power in the company increases:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>from 20% or below to more than 20%; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>from a starting point that is above 20% and below 90%.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

However, if the acquisition of the relevant interest is covered by one of the exceptions set out in section 611, the person may acquire the legal or equitable interest without contravening this subsection.

_50 member threshold_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>In determining whether the company has more than 50 members for the

purposes of subsection (1) or (2), count joint holders of a particular parcel

of shares as 1 person.

</dd> </dl>

_Offers and invitations_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>A person must not:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>make an offer, or cause an offer to be made on their behalf, if the person

would contravene subsection (1) or (2) if the offer were accepted; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>issue an invitation, or cause an invitation to be issued on their behalf,

if the person would contravene subsection (1) or (2) if:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>an offer were made in response to the invitation; and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>the offer were accepted.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

_Defences_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(5)</dt><dd>It is a defence to the prosecution of a person for contravening subsection

(1), (2) or (4) if the person proves that they contravened the subsection:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>because of inadvertence or mistake; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>because the person was not aware of a relevant fact or occurrence.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

In determining whether the defence is available, disregard the person's ignorance of, or a mistake on the person's part concerning, a matter of law.

_Extended meaning of acquiring relevant interestsconversions and increases in voting rights_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(6)</dt><dd>A person is taken for the purposes of subsection (1) or (2) to acquire a

relevant interest in voting shares in a company if:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>securities in which the person already had a relevant interest become

voting shares in the company; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>there is an increase in the number of votes that may be cast on a poll

attached to voting shares that the person already had a relevant interest in.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

The acquisition occurs when the securities become voting shares or the number of votes increases.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Some examples of cases to which this subsection applies are:

 </dl></dl>

*	A person exercises a right to convert a non-voting preference share into an ordinary share that carries votes.
 *	A person pays up partly-paid shares with limited votes and this leads to an increase in the number of votes attached to the shares.

607  Effect on transactions

<dl compact="">

		A transaction is not invalid merely because it involves a contravention of

section 606.

 </dl>

608  Relevant interests in securities

_Basic rulerelevant interest is holding, or controlling voting or disposal of, securities_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>A person has a relevant interest in securities if they:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>are the holder of the securities; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>have power to exercise, or control the exercise of, a right to vote

attached to the securities; or</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>have power to dispose of, or control the exercise of a power to dispose

of, the securities.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

It does not matter how remote the relevant interest is or how it arises. If 2 or more people can jointly exercise one of these powers, each of them is taken to have that power. 

_Extension to control exercisable through a trust, agreement or practice_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>In this section, power or control includes:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>power or control that is indirect; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>power or control that is, or can be, exercised as a result of, by means of

or by the revocation or breach of:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>a trust; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>an agreement; or</dd>

<dt>(iii)</dt><dd>a practice; or</dd>

<dt>(iv)</dt><dd>any combination of them;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		whether or not they are enforceable; and

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>power or control that is, or can be made, subject to restraint or

restriction.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

It does not matter whether the power or control is express or implied, formal or informal, exercisable alone or jointly with someone else. It does not matter that the power or control cannot be related to a particular security.

_Extension to relevant interests held through bodies corporate_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>A person has the relevant interests in any securities that any of the

following has:

</dd> </dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>a body corporate, or managed investment scheme, in which the person's

voting power is above 20%</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>a body corporate, or managed investment scheme, that the person controls.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

Paragraph (a) does not apply to a relevant interest that the body corporate or scheme itself has in the securities merely because of the operation of that paragraph in relation to another body corporate or managed investment scheme.

<dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>For the purposes of paragraph (3)(b), a person controls a body corporate

if the person has the capacity to determine the outcome of decisions about the

body corporate's financial and operating policies.</dd> <dt>(5)</dt><dd>In determining whether a person has this capacity: </dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the practical influence the person can exert (rather than the rights they

can enforce) is the issue to be addressed; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>any practice or pattern of behaviour affecting the body corporate's

financial or operating policies is to be taken into account (even if it

involves a breach of an agreement or a breach of trust).

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(6)</dt><dd>The person does not control the body corporate merely because the person

and an entity that is not an associate jointly have the capacity to determine

the outcome of decisions about the body corporate's financial and operating

policies.</dd> <dt>(7)</dt><dd>A person is not to be taken to control a body corporate merely because of a capacity they have if they are under a legal obligation to exercise that capacity for the benefit of: </dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>if the person is an individual&#151;someone else; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>if the person is a body corporate&#151;someone other than its members.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

_Extension to control in anticipation of performance of agreements etc._

<dl compact="">

<dt>(8)</dt><dd>If at a particular time all the following conditions are satisfied:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>a person has a relevant interest in issued securities</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the person (whether before or after acquiring the relevant interest):

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>has entered or enters into an agreement with another person with respect

to the securities; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>has given or gives another person an enforceable right, or has been or is

given an enforceable right by another person, in relation to the securities

(whether the right is enforceable presently or in the future and whether or not

on the fulfilment of a condition); or</dd>

<dt>(iii)</dt><dd>has granted or grants an option to, or has been or is granted an option

by, another person with respect to the securities

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the other person would have a relevant interest in the securities if the

agreement were performed, the right enforced or the option exercised;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

the other person is taken to already have a relevant interest in the securities.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Subsections 609(6) and (7) deal with specific situations in

which the agreement will not give rise to a relevant interest.

 </dl></dl>

_Body corporate may have relevant interest in its own securities_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(9)</dt><dd>This section may result in a body corporate having a relevant interest in

its own securities.

</dd> </dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

609  Situations not giving rise to relevant interests

_Money lending and financial accommodation_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>A person does not have a relevant interest in securities merely because of

a mortgage, charge or other security taken for the purpose of a transaction

entered into by the person if:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the mortgage, charge or security is taken or acquired in the ordinary

course of the person's business of providing financial services and on ordinary

commercial terms; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the person whose property is subject to the mortgage, charge or security

is not an associate of the person.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Sections 11 to 17 define _associate_.

 </dl></dl>

_Nominees and other trustees_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>A person who would otherwise have a relevant interest in securities as a

bare trustee does not have a relevant interest in the securities if a

beneficiary under the trust has a relevant interest in the securities because

of a presently enforceable and unconditional right of the kind referred to in

subsection 608(8).

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	This subsection will often apply to a person who holds

securities as a nominee.

 </dl></dl>

_Holding of securities by securities dealer_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>A securities dealer does not have a relevant interest in securities merely

because they hold securities on behalf of someone else in the ordinary course

of their securities business.

</dd> </dl>

_Shares covered by buy-backs_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>A person does not have a relevant interest in a company's shares if the

relevant interest would arise merely because the company has entered into an

agreement to buy back the shares.

</dd> </dl>

_Proxies_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(5)</dt><dd>A person does not have a relevant interest in securities merely because

the person has been appointed to vote as a proxy or representative at a meeting

of members, or of a class of members, of the company, body or managed

investment scheme if:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the appointment is for one meeting only; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>neither the person nor any associate gives valuable consideration for the

appointment.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

_Exchange traded options and futures contracts_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(6)</dt><dd>A person does not have a relevant interest in securities merely because of:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>an exchange traded option over the securities; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>a right to acquire the securities given by a futures contract.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

This subsection stops applying to the relevant interest when the obligation to make or take delivery of the securities arises.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Without this subsection, subsection 608(8) would create a

relevant interest from the option or contract.

 </dl></dl>

_Conditional agreements_

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(7)</dt><dd>A person does not have a relevant interest in securities merely because of

an agreement if the agreement:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>is conditional on:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>a resolution under item 7 in the table in section 611 being passed; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>ASIC exempting the acquisition under the agreement from the provisions of

this Chapter under section 655A; and

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>does not confer any control over, or power to substantially influence, the

exercise of a voting right attached to the securities; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>does not restrict disposal of the securities for more than 3 months from

the date when the agreement is entered into.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

The person acquires a relevant interest in the securities when the condition referred to in paragraph (a) is satisfied.

_Pre-emptive rights_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(8)</dt><dd>A member of a company, body or managed investment scheme does not have a

relevant interest in securities of the company, body or scheme merely because

the company's, body's or scheme's constitution gives members pre-emptive rights

on the transfer of the securities if all members have pre-emptive rights on the

same terms.

</dd> </dl>

_Director of body corporate holding securities_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(9)</dt><dd>A person does not have a relevant interest in securities merely because:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the person is a director of a body corporate; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the body corporate has a relevant interest in those securities.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

_Prescribed exclusions_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(10)</dt><dd>A person does not have a relevant interest in securities in the

circumstances specified in the regulations. The regulations may provide that

interests in securities are not relevant interests subject to specified

conditions.

</dd> </dl>

610  Voting power in a body corporate

_Person&apos;s voting power in a body corporate_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>A person's _voting power_ in a body corporate is:

</dd> </dl>

<sub> ![A graphic exists here.](http://www.comlaw.gov.au/Details/C2004C01070/Html/AA356F7CD35B5DE2CA256F7100539BBD/$FILE/1203.gif)![A graphic exists here.](http://www.comlaw.gov.au/Details/C2004C01070/Html/AA356F7CD35B5DE2CA256F7100539BBD/$FILE/1204.gif)</sub>

where:

<def><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

_person&apos;s and associates&apos; votes_ is the total number of votes

attached to all the voting shares in the body corporate (if any) that the

person or an associate has a relevant interest in. _total votes in body corporate_ is the total number of votes attached to all voting shares in the body corporate.  </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Even if a person's relevant interest in voting shares is

based on control over disposal of the shares (rather than control over voting

rights attached to the shares), their voting power in the body corporate is

calculated on the basis of the number of votes attached to those shares.

 </dl></dl>

_Counting votes_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>For the purposes of this section, the number of votes attached to a voting

share in a body corporate is the maximum number of votes that can be cast in

respect of the share on a poll:

</dd> </dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>if the election of directors is determined by the casting of votes

attached to voting shares&#151;on the election of a director of the body corporate;

or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>if the election of directors is not determined by the casting of votes

attached to voting shares&#151;on the adoption of a constitution for the body

corporate or the amendment of the body corporate's constitution.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	The Corporations and Securities Panel may decide that the

setting or varying of voting rights in a way that affects control of a body

corporate is unacceptable circumstances under section 657A.

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>If:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>a transaction in relation to, or an acquisition of an interest in,

securities occurs; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>before the transaction or acquisition, a person did not have a relevant

interest in particular voting shares but an associate of the person did have a

relevant interest in those shares; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>because of the transaction or acquisition, the person acquires a relevant

interest in those shares;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

then, for the purposes of applying section 606 to the transaction or acquisition, the person's voting power is taken to have increased because of the transaction or acquisition from what it would have been before the transaction or acquisition if the votes attached to those shares were disregarded to what it was after the transaction or acquisition (taking the votes attached to those shares into account).

<dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>Disregard the operation of section 613 in working out a person's voting

power in a body corporate.

</dd> </dl>

Part 6.2&#151;Exceptions to the prohibition

611  Exceptions to the prohibition

<dl compact="">

		The following table sets out:

 </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>acquisitions of relevant interests in a company's voting shares  that are exempt from the prohibition in subsection 606(1); and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>acquisitions of relevant interests in a company's voting shares  resulting from acquisitions of legal or equitable interests in securities

of a body corporate that are exempt from the prohibition in subsection 606(2).

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Some of the items in the table cover only activities in

relation to the company itself (items 7, 8, 12 and 13) while the other items

cover acquisitions in that company that may occur through activities in

relation to other companies.

</tr></table>612 
<center>Back to Top</center>
  Effect of non-compliance with takeover rules for exceptions 1 to 4

<dl compact="">

		The exceptions in items 1 to 4 of the table in section 611 do not apply to a

takeover bid if the bid is carried out in contravention of:

 </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>section 618 (full or proportionate bid); or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>section 619 (offers to be the same); or</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>subsection 621(3) (minimum price); or</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>subsection 624(1) (minimum offer period); or</dd>

<dt>(e)</dt><dd>sections 625 to 630 (conditional offers); or</dd>

<dt>(f)</dt><dd>items 2, 3 and 6 in the table in subsection 633(1) (procedural steps for

off-market bid); or </dd>

<dt>(g)</dt><dd>items 3, 4 and 6 in the table in section 635 (procedural steps for market

bid).

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

613  Bidder not to exercise voting rights if failure to send bids for off-market acquisition&#151;exception 2 or 3

<dl compact="">

		If the exception in item 2 or 3 of the table in section 611 applies to an

acquisition on-market during a takeover bid, the bidder is not entitled to

exercise the voting rights attached to the shares if:

 </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the bid is an off-market bid; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the bidder fails to send offers under the bid within 28 days after giving

the bidder's statement to the target. 

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

615  Treatment of foreign holders under equal access issue&#151;exception 10

<dl compact="">

		The exception in item 10 of the table in section 611 applies even though the

conditions set out in the item are not satisfied in respect of foreign holders

of the company's securities if, under the terms of the offers:

 </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the company must appoint a nominee for foreign holders of the company's

securities who is approved by ASIC; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the company must transfer to the nominee:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>the securities that would otherwise be issued to the foreign holders who

accept the offer; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>the right to acquire those securities; and

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the nominee must sell the securities, or those rights, and distribute to

each of those foreign holders their proportion of the proceeds of the sale net

of expenses.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

Part 6.3&#151;The different types of takeover bid

616  Off-market bids and market bids

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>There are 2 kinds of takeover bid:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>an off-market bid (for quoted or unquoted securities); or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>a market bid (only available for quoted securities).

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Although the prohibition in section 606 is against

acquiring relevant interests in voting shares, a takeover bid may be made for

any securities (for example, as a preliminary to compulsorily acquiring

securities in that class under Part 6A.1).

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>The following table shows where to find the provisions dealing with the

main features of the offers that may be made under off-market bids and market

bids and the procedures to be followed:

</dd> </dl>
