<center>Back to Top</center>

Part 6.4&#151;Formulating the takeover offer
 Division 1&#151;General
 617  Securities covered by the bid

_Off-market bid_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>An off-market bid must relate to securities:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>in a class of securities (the _bid class_); and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>that exist or will exist as at the date set by the bidder under subsection

633(2).

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Subsection 92(3) defines _securities_ for the

purposes of this Chapter.

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>If other securities exist or will exist at that date that:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>will convert, or may be converted, to securities in the bid class; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>confer rights to be issued securities in the bid class;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

the bid may extend to securities that come to be in the bid class during the offer period due to a conversion or exercise of the rights.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	The bidder's statement must say if the bid is extended in

this way (see paragraph 636(1)(j)).

 </dl></dl>

_Market bid_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>A market bid must relate to securities:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>in a class of quoted securities (the _bid class_); and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>that exist or  will exist  at any time during the offer period.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

618  Offers must be for all or a proportion of securities in the bid class

_Off-market bid_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>An offer for securities under an off-market bid must be an offer to buy:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>all the securities in the bid class; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>a specified proportion of the securities in the bid class.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

The proportion specified under paragraph (b) must be the same for all holders of securities in the bid class.

_Off-market bidnon-marketable parcels_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>If accepting an offer under an off-market bid for quoted securities would

leave a person with a parcel of the securities that is less than a marketable

parcel (within the meaning of the rules of the relevant securities exchange),

the offer extends to that parcel.

</dd> </dl>

_Market bid_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>An offer for securities under a market bid must be an offer to buy all the

securities in the bid class.

</dd> </dl>

619  General terms of the offer

_Off-market bid_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>All the offers made under an off-market bid must be the same.

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	The offers may include alternative forms of consideration

(see section 621).

 </dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>In applying subsection (1), disregard the following:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>any differences in the offers attributable to the fact that the number of

securities that may be acquired under each offer is limited by the number of

securities held by the holder</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>any differences in the offers attributable to the fact that the offers

relate to securities having different accrued dividend or distribution

entitlements</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>any differences in the offers attributable to the fact that the offers

relate to securities on which different amounts are paid up or remain unpaid</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>any differences in the offers attributable to the fact that the bidder may

issue or transfer only whole numbers of securities as consideration for the

acquisition</dd>

<dt>(e)</dt><dd>any additional cash amount offered to holders instead of the fraction of a

security that they would otherwise be offered.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

_Foreign holders_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>If the consideration for the bid includes an offer of securities, the

securities do not need to be offered to foreign holders of the target's

securities if under the terms of the bid:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the bidder must appoint a nominee for foreign holders of the target's

securities who is approved by ASIC; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the bidder must transfer to the nominee:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>the securities that would otherwise be transferred to the foreign holders

who accept the bid for that consideration; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>the right to acquire those securities; and

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the nominee must sell the securities, or those rights, and distribute to

each of those foreign holders their proportion of the proceeds of the sale net

of expenses.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

620  Off-market bid (offer formalities)

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>Each offer under an off-market bid must:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>be in writing; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>have the same date; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>provide that, unless withdrawn, it will remain open until the end of the

offer period (see section 624); and</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>state how, and when, the bidder is to satisfy their obligations.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>Each offer must provide that the bidder is to pay or provide the

consideration for the offer:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>if the bidder is given the necessary transfer documents with the

acceptance&#151;by the end of whichever of the following periods ends earlier:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>1 month after the offer is accepted or, if the offer is subject to a

defeating condition, within 1 month after the takeover contract becomes

unconditional</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>21 days after the end of the offer period; or

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>if the bidder is given the necessary transfer documents after the

acceptance and before the end of the bid period&#151;within 1 month after the

bidder is given the necessary transfer documents; or</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>if the bidder is given the necessary transfer documents after the

acceptance and after the end of the bid period&#151;within 21 days after the bidder

is given the necessary transfer documents.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Subsection 630(1) requires an offer that is subject to a

defeating condition to specify a date for declaring whether the condition has

been fulfilled or not.

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>The offer may provide that the bidder may avoid the takeover contract if

the bidder is not given the necessary transfer documents within 1 month after

the end of the offer period.

</dd> </dl>

Division 2&#151;Consideration for the offer
 621  Consideration offered

_Off-market bidgeneral_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>A bidder making an off-market bid for securities may offer any form of

consideration for the securities, including:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>a cash sum; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>securities (including shares, debentures, interests in a managed

investment scheme or options); or</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>a combination of a cash sum and securities.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Sections 650B and 651A deal with variations of the

consideration offered under the bid.

 </dl></dl>

_Market bidcash only_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>As the offers under a market bid for securities are made through the stock

market of a securities exchange, the bidder must offer to acquire the

securities for a cash sum only for each security.

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Section 649B deals with variations of the consideration

offered under the bid.

 </dl></dl>

_All bidsminimum consideration if bidder purchased securities in the 4 months before the bid_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>The consideration offered for securities in the bid class under a takeover

bid must equal or exceed the maximum consideration that the bidder or an

associate provided, or agreed to provide, for a security in the bid class under

any purchase or agreement during the 4 months before the date of the bid.</dd> <dt>(4)</dt><dd>For the purposes of subsection (3), the consideration offered or provided for a security is: </dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>if the consideration offered or provided is a cash sum only&#151;the amount of

that cash sum; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>if the consideration offered or provided does not include a cash sum&#151;the

value of that consideration; or</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>if the consideration offered or provided is a cash sum and other

consideration&#151;the sum of the amount of the cash sum and the value of the other

consideration.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

The value of consideration that is not a cash sum is to be ascertained as at the time the relevant offer, purchase or agreement is made.

<dl compact="">

<dt>(5)</dt><dd>If:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>a person agrees to buy a security in a company; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the agreement provides that the price payable for the security is a price

specified in the agreement but may be varied in accordance with the terms of

the agreement;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

any variation in price under the agreement is to be disregarded in working out, for the purposes of subsection (3), the price agreed to be paid for the 
<center>Back to Top</center>
 security under the agreement.

622  Escalation agreements

_Benefits linked to bids and proposed bids not allowed_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>A person who makes or proposes to make a takeover bid for securities, or

their associate, contravenes this section if:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>a person acquires a relevant interest in securities in the bid class

within the 6 months before the bid is made or proposed; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>at any time whatever, the bidder, proposed bidder or associate gives or

agrees to give a benefit to, or receives or agrees to receive a benefit from:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>a person who had a relevant interest in any of the paragraph (a)

securities immediately before the acquisition; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>an associate of a person who had a relevant interest in any of those

securities at that time; and

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the benefit is attributable to the acquisition or matters that include the

acquisition; and</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>the amount or value of the benefit is, or is to be, determined by

reference to or to matters that include either of the following:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>the amount or value of the consideration for the securities under the bid

or proposed bid</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>the amount or value of the consideration for which the bidder or proposed

bidder acquires, offers or proposes to offer to acquire, securities in the bid

class during the offer period (whether or not under the bid) or under Chapter

6A.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

_Contravening agreements void_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>An agreement is void to the extent that it purports to provide for:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>a person to give a benefit to a person; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>a person to receive a benefit from a person;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

in contravention of subsection (1).

623  Collateral benefits not allowed

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>A bidder, or an associate, must not, during the offer period for a

takeover bid, give, offer to give or agree to give a benefit to a person if:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the benefit is likely to induce the person  or an associate to:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>accept an offer under the bid; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>dispose of securities in the bid class; and

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the benefit is not offered to all holders of securities in the bid class

under the bid.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>For the purpose of this section, a person does not receive a benefit that

is not offered under a takeover bid merely because the person sells bid class

securities on-market and the takeover bid is an off-market bid or a conditional

bid.</dd> <dt>(3)</dt><dd>This section does not prohibit: </dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the variation of a takeover offer as provided by sections 649A to 650D;

or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>an acquisition of securities through an on-market transaction; or</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>simultaneous takeover bids for different classes of securities in the

target.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

Division 3&#151;The offer period
 624  Offer period

_Offer period set in offer_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>The offers under a takeover bid must remain open for the period stated in

the offer. The period must:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>start on the date the first offer under the bid is made; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>last for at least 1 month, and not more than 12 months.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

However, the offer may be withdrawn during that period under section 652B.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Sections 649C (market bids) and 650C (off-market bids) deal

with variation of the offer period.

 </dl></dl>

_Automatic extension of offer period if bidder reaches 50% or consideration increased in last week_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>If, within the last 7 days of the offer period:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>for an off-market bid&#151;the offers under the bid are varied to improve the

consideration offered; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>in any case&#151;the bidder's voting power in the target increases to more

than 50%;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

the offer period is extended so that it ends 14 days after the event referred to in paragraph (a) or (b). The bidder must give the target and everyone who has not accepted an offer under the bid written notice that the extension has occurred within 3 days after that event.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	The consideration for a market bid cannot be increased in

the last 5 trading days of the offer period (see section 649B).

 </dl></dl>

Division 4&#151;Conditional offers
 625  Conditional offers&#151;general

_Market bids_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>Offers under a market bid must be unconditional.

</dd> </dl>

_Off-market bids may generally be conditional_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>Offers under an off-market bid may be subject to conditions that are not

prohibited by sections 626 to 629.</dd> <dt>(3)</dt><dd>If: </dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the consideration offered is or includes securities; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the offer or the bidder's statement states or implies that the securities

are to be quoted on a stock market of a securities exchange (whether in

Australia or elsewhere);

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

the following rules apply:

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the offer is subject to a condition that:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>an application for admission to quotation will be made within 7 days after

the start of the bid period; and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>permission for admission to quotation will be granted no later than 7

days after the end of the bid period

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>the offer may not be freed from this condition.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Section 1325A provides that a Court may make a remedial

order if the condition is not satisfied.

 </dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

626  Maximum acceptance conditions in off-market bids

_Maximum acceptance conditions not allowed_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>Offers under an off-market bid must not be subject to a maximum acceptance

condition. A maximum acceptance condition is one that provides that the offers

will terminate, or the maximum consideration offered under the bid will be

reduced, if one or more of the following occur:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the number of securities for which the bidder receives acceptances reaches

or exceeds a particular number; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the bidder's voting power in the company reaches or exceeds a particular

percentage; or</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the percentage of securities the bidder has relevant interests in reaches

or exceeds a particular percentage of securities in that class.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>For the purposes of subsection (1), it does not matter:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>how the condition is expressed; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>how a particular number or percentage was, or is to be, determined; or</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>whether or not a particular number or percentage is specified in the

condition and, if it is so specified, how it is expressed.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>For the purposes of subsection (1), an offer under an off-market bid

terminates if:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the offer lapses, is withdrawn or otherwise ceases to have effect; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>a binding takeover contract will not result from an acceptance of the

offer; or</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>an obligation of the bidder will not arise under the takeover contract;

or</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>the takeover contract is rescinded; or</dd>

<dt>(e)</dt><dd>the bidder is entitled to rescind the takeover contract; or</dd>

<dt>(f)</dt><dd>the bidder is relieved of an obligation arising under the takeover

contract.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

627  Discriminatory conditions not allowed for off-market bids

<dl compact="">

		Offers under an off-market bid must not be subject to a condition that allows

the bidder to acquire, or may result in the bidder acquiring, securities from

some but not all of the people who accept the offers. It does not matter how

the condition is expressed.

 </dl>

628  Conditions requiring payments to officers of target not allowed in off-market bids

<dl compact="">

		An offer to a person under an off-market bid must not be made subject to a

condition that requires the person to approve or consent to a payment or other

benefit to an officer of the target or a related body corporate:

 </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>as compensation for loss of; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>as consideration in connection with retirement from;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

any office or employment in connection with the management of the target or of a related body corporate. A purported requirement of this kind is void.

629  Conditions turning on bidder's or associate's opinion not allowed in off-market bids

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>Offers under an off-market bid must not be subject to a defeating

condition if the fulfilment of the condition depends on:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the bidder's, or an associate's, opinion, belief or other state of mind;

or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the happening of an event that is within the sole control of, or is a

direct result of action by, any of the following:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>the bidder (acting alone or together with an associate or associates)</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>an associate (acting alone or together with the bidder or another

associate or associates of the bidder).

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

A purported condition of this kind is void.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Section 9 defines _defeating condition_.

Sections 630, 650F and 650G deal with defeating conditions.

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>For the purposes of paragraph (1)(b):

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the target; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>a subsidiary of the target;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

are taken not to be associates of the bidder if they would otherwise be an associate merely because they are a related body corporate.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Paragraph 11(b) makes related bodies corporate associates

of each other.

 </dl></dl>

630  Defeating conditions

_Off-market bid may include defeating conditions_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>Offers under an off-market bid may be made subject to a defeating

condition only if the offers specify a date (not more than 14 days and not less

than 7 days before the end of the offer period) for giving a notice on the

status of the condition.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>If the offer period is extended by a period: </dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the date for giving the notice is taken to be postponed for the same

period; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>as soon as practicable after the extension, the bidder must give a notice

that states:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>the new date for giving the notice of the status of the condition; and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>whether the offers have been freed from the condition and whether, so far

as the bidder knows, the condition has been fulfilled on the date the notice

under this subsection is given.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

_Bidder to give notice of status of defeating condition near end of offer period_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>On the date determined under subsection (1) or (2), the bidder must give a

notice that states:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>whether the offers are free of the condition; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>whether, so far as the bidder knows, the condition was fulfilled on the

date the notice is given; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the bidder's voting power in the target.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

The bidder must comply with this subsection whether or not the bidder has given a notice under subsection (4) or 650F(1).

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	The offers may be freed of the condition by a declaration

by the bidder under subsection 650F(1).

 </dl></dl>

_Bidder to give notice if defeating condition fulfilled_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>If the condition is fulfilled (so that the offers become free of the

condition) during the bid period but before the date for publishing the notice

on the status of the condition, the bidder must publish as soon as practicable

a notice that states that the condition has been fulfilled.</dd> <dt>(5)</dt><dd>A notice under this section is given by: </dd> </dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>giving the notice to the target; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>for quoted bid class securities&#151;giving the notice to the relevant

securities exchange; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>for unquoted bid class securities&#151;lodging the notice with ASIC.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

Part 6.5&#151;The takeover procedure
 Division 1&#151;The overall procedure
 631  Proposing or announcing a bid

_Bid must proceed within 2 months after proposal_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>If a person publicly proposes to make a takeover bid for securities in a

company, either alone or with other persons, the person contravenes this

subsection unless they make offers for the securities under a takeover bid

within 2 months after the proposal. The terms and conditions of the bid must be

the same as or not substantially less favourable than those in the public

proposal.

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	The Court has power under section 1325B to order a person

to proceed with a bid.

 </dl></dl>

_Proposals if takeover bid not intended_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>A person must not publicly propose, either alone or with other persons, to

make a takeover bid if:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the person knows the proposed bid will not be made, or is reckless as to

whether the proposed bid is made; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the person is reckless as to whether they will be able to perform their

obligations relating to the takeover bid if a substantial proportion of the

offers under the bid are accepted.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>Section 1314 (continuing offences) and subsection 1324(2) (injunctions) do

not apply in relation to a failure to make a takeover bid in accordance with a

public proposal under subsection (1).

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	For liability and defences for contraventions of this

section, see sections 670E and 670F.

 </dl></dl>

633  Detailed steps in an off-market bid

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>The following table provides for the steps that a bidder must take to make

an effective off-market bid and the steps that a target must take when an

off-market bid is made.

</dd> </dl>

<table><tr align="left">
  <th colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>Steps in off-market bid</div>

  </th>
  <th colspan="1" align="right">
    <div>\[operative table]</div>

  </th>
</tr>
<tr align="left">
  <th colspan="1" align="left">

  </th>
  <th colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>Steps</div>

  </th>
  <th colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>Timing and relevant provisions</div>

  </th>
</tr>
<tr align="left">
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>1</div>

  </td>
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>The bidder must prepare:</div>
    <div>* a bidder's statement; and 
* if the bidder's statement does not set out all the terms of the offer&#151;an offer document that sets out the other terms of the offer.</div>

  </td>
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div><i>See section 636 for content of statement.</i></div>

  </td>
</tr>
<tr align="left">
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>2</div>

  </td>
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>The bidder must lodge a copy of the bidder's statement and offer document with ASIC.</div>

  </td>
  <td colspan="1" align="left">

  </td>
</tr>
<tr align="left">
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>3</div>

  </td>
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>The bidder must send a copy of the bidder's statement and offer document to the target.</div>

  </td>
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>To be done on the day the bidder's statement is lodged or within 21 days afterwards</div>

  </td>
</tr>
<tr align="left">
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>4</div>

  </td>
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>The bidder must lodge with ASIC a notice stating that the bidder's statement and offer document have been sent to the target.</div>

  </td>
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>To be done on the day the bidder's statement is sent to the target</div>

  </td>
</tr>
<tr align="left">
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>5</div>

  </td>
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>The bidder must send a copy of the bidder's statement and offer document to each securities exchange that has a stock market on which the target's securities are quoted.</div>

  </td>
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>To be done on the day the bidder's statement is sent to the target 
 <i>See also subsection (5).</i></div>

  </td>
</tr>
<tr align="left">
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>6</div>

  </td>
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>The bidder must send the bidder's statement and offers to each person (other than the bidder) who holds:</div>
    <div>* securities in the bid class; or 
* if the bid extends to securities that come to be in the bid class due to the conversion of or exercise of rights attached to other securities (see subsection 617(2))&#151;the other securities;</div>
    <div>as at the date set by the bidder under subsection (2). 
The offers must be made on the terms set out in the bidder's statement and the offer document lodged with ASIC under item 2.</div>

  </td>
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>To be done:</div>
    <div>* within a 3 day period; and 
* within 14-28 days after the bidder's statement is sent to the target</div>
    <div>The directors of the target may agree that the offers and accompanying documents be sent earlier. 
 <i>See also subsections (5) and (6).</i> 
 <i>Item 2 of the table in section 611 covers offers made by the bidder on-market during the period between the lodgment of the bidder's statement and the making of the offers under the bid.</i> 
 <i>Sections 648B and 648C provide for the manner in which documents may be sent to holders.</i></div>

  </td>
</tr>
<tr align="left">
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>7</div>

  </td>
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>The bidder must send a notice to the target that the bidder's statement and offers have been sent as required by item 6\. 
The notice must state the date of the offers.</div>

  </td>
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>To be done on the day all offers have been sent as required by item 6 
 <i>See subsection 620(1) on date of offer.</i></div>

  </td>
</tr>
<tr align="left">
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>8</div>

  </td>
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>The bidder must send a notice that offers have been sent as required by item 6 to each securities exchange that has a stock market on which the target's securities are quoted.</div>

  </td>
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>To be done on the day all offers have been sent as required by item 6</div>

  </td>
</tr>
<tr align="left">
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>9</div>

  </td>
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>The bidder must lodge with ASIC a notice that offers have been sent as required by item 6.</div>

  </td>
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>To be done on the day all offers have been sent as required by item 6</div>

  </td>
</tr>
<tr align="left">
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>10</div>

  </td>
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>The target must prepare a target's statement.</div>

  </td>
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div><i>See section 638 for content of statement.</i></div>

  </td>
</tr>
<tr align="left">
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>11</div>

  </td>
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>The target must send the target's statement (and any accompanying report) to the bidder.</div>

  </td>
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>To be done no later than 15 days after the target receives a notice that all offers have been sent as required by item 6</div>

  </td>
</tr>
<tr align="left">
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>12</div>

  </td>
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>The target must send a copy of the target's statement (and any accompanying report) to each person who holds:</div>
    <div>* securities in the bid class; or 
* if the bid extends to securities that come to be in the bid class due to the conversion of or exercise of rights attached to other securities (see subsection 617(2))&#151;the other securities;</div>
    <div>as at the date set by the bidder under subsection (2).</div>

  </td>
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>To be done:</div>
    <div>* no earlier than the day on which the target sends the target's statement to the bidder; and 
* no later than 15 days after the target receives a notice that all offers have been sent as required by item 6</div>
    <div><i>Sections 648B and 648C provide for the manner in which documents may be sent to holders.</i></div>

  </td>
</tr>
<tr align="left">
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>13</div>

  </td>
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>The target must lodge a copy of the target's statement (and any accompanying report) with ASIC.</div>

  </td>
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>To be done on the day the target's statement is sent to the bidder 
 <i>See also subsection (7).</i></div>

  </td>
</tr>
<tr align="left">
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>14</div>

  </td>
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>The target must send a copy of the target's statement (and any accompanying report) to each securities exchange that has a stock market on which the target's securities are quoted.</div>

  </td>
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>To be done on the day the target's statement is sent to the bidder 
 <i>See also subsection (7).</i></div>

  </td>
</tr></table>_Date Back to Top for determining holders of securities_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>The people to whom information is to be sent under items 6 and 12 of the

table in subsection (1) are the holders of the securities referred to in those

items as at the date set by the bidder in:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the bidder's statement; or</dd>

(b)	a separate written notice given to the target on or before the date

set by the bidder.

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	The bidder may set the date when the bidder asks the target

for a list of members under section 641.

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>The date set by the bidder must be:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>on or after the date on which the bidder gives the bidder's statement, or

the separate written notice, to the target; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>on or before the date on which the first offers under the bid are made to

holders of the securities.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>As soon as practicable after setting the day, the bidder must give notice

of it by:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>if the securities in the bid class are quoted&#151;giving the notice to the

relevant securities exchange; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>otherwise&#151;lodging the notice with ASIC.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

_Information to be sent with bidder&apos;s statement_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(5)</dt><dd>A bidder's statement required to be sent under item 5 or 6 in the table in

subsection (1) must be sent together with any other information sent by the

bidder to the target with the statement.

</dd> </dl>

_Information to be sent with notices that offers have been sent_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(6)</dt><dd>If the bidder sends the people to whom the bidder's statement is sent

under item 6 of the table in subsection (1) additional information together

with the bidder's statement and the offer, the bidder must also include that

information in any notice under item 7, 8 or 9 of the table.

</dd> </dl>

_Information to be sent with target&apos;s statement_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(7)</dt><dd>If the target sends the people to whom the target's statement is sent

under item 12 of the table in subsection (1) additional information together

with the target's statement, the target must also include that information in

any notice under item 13 or 14 of the table.

</dd> </dl>

    <div>

  Detailed steps in a market bid

		The following table provides for the steps that a bidder must take to make an

effective market bid and the steps that a target must take when a market bid is

made.

 </dl>

 <i>Item 2 of the table in section 611 covers offers made by the bidder on market during the 14 day period between the announcement and the making of the offers under the bid</i></div>
