<center>Back to Top</center>
 2&#151;The bidder's statement
 636  Bidder's statement content

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>A bidder's statement must include the following:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the identity of the bidder</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the date of the statement</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>if the target is a company or body&#151;details of the bidder's intentions

regarding:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>the continuation of the business of the target; and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>any major changes to be made to the business of the target, including any

redeployment of the fixed assets of the target; and</dd>

<dt>(iii)</dt><dd>the future employment of the present employees of the target

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>if the target is a managed investment scheme&#151;details of the bidder's

intentions regarding:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>the continued operation of the scheme; and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>any major changes to be made to the operation of the scheme, including

any redeployment of scheme property; and</dd>

<dt>(iii)</dt><dd>any plans to remove the current responsible entity and appoint a new

responsible entity

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(e)</dt><dd>for an off-market bid&#151;a statement that the bidder's statement has been

lodged with ASIC but that ASIC takes no responsibility for the content of the

statement</dd>

<dt>(f)</dt><dd>in relation to the cash consideration (if any) offered under the

bid&#151;details of:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>the cash amounts (if any) held by the bidder for payment of the

consideration; and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>the identity of any other person who is to provide, directly or

indirectly, cash consideration from that person's own funds; and</dd>

<dt>(iii)</dt><dd>any arrangements under which cash will be provided by a person referred

to in subparagraph (ii)

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(g)</dt><dd>if any securities are offered as consideration under the bid and the

bidder is:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>the body that has issued or will issue the securities; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>a person who controls that body;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		all material that would be required for a prospectus for an offer of those

securities by the bidder under section 710 to 713

<dt>(h)</dt><dd>if the bidder or an associate provided, or agreed to provide,

consideration for a security in the bid class under a purchase or agreement

during the 4 months before the date of the bid&#151;the following information about

the consideration:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>to the extent to which the consideration is a cash sum&#151;the amount per

security of the cash sum</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>to the extent to which the consideration is quoted securities&#151;the market

price per security of those securities</dd>

<dt>(iii)</dt><dd>to the extent to which the consideration is neither a cash sum nor a

quoted security&#151;the value per security of that consideration

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>if, during the period of 4 months before the date of the bid, the bidder

or an associate gave, or offered to give or agreed to give a benefit to another

person and the benefit was likely to induce the other person, or an

associate, to:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>accept an offer under the bid; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>dispose of securities in the bid class;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		and the benefit is not offered to all holders of securities in the bid class

under the bid&#151;details of the benefit

<dt>(j)</dt><dd>if the bid is to extend to securities that come to be in the bid class

during the offer period due to the conversion of or exercise of rights attached

to other securities (see subsection 617(2))&#151;a statement to that effect</dd>

<dt>(k)</dt><dd>for an off-market bid&#151;the following details in relation to each class of

securities in the target:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>the total number of securities in the class</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>the number of securities in the class that the bidder had a relevant

interest in immediately before the first offer is sent (expressed as a number

of securities or as a percentage of the total number of securities in the class)

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(l)</dt><dd>for an off-market bid&#151;the bidder's voting power in the company</dd>

<dt>(m)</dt><dd>any other information that:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>is material to the making of the decision by a holder of bid class

securities whether to accept an offer under the bid; and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>is known to the bidder; and</dd>

<dt>(iii)</dt><dd>does not relate to the value of securities offered as consideration

under the bid.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

The information that the bidder must disclose under subparagraph (k)(i) and paragraph (l) must be only as up-to-date as it is reasonable to expect in the circumstances. The bidder does not have to disclose information under paragraph (m) if it would be unreasonable to require the bidder to do so because the information had previously been disclosed to the holders of bid class securities.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Paragraph (b)&#151;See subsection 637(2) for the date of the

statement.

 </dl></dl>

_Expert&apos;s report on non-cash consideration provided for bid class securities in last 4 months_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>If the bidder's statement includes details of the value per share of

consideration under subparagraph (1)(h)(iii), the statement must include, or be

accompanied by, a report by an expert that states whether, in the expert's

opinion, the value stated is fair and reasonable and gives the reasons for

forming that opinion.

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Subsections 648A(2) and (3) provide for the independence of

the expert and disclosure of any association between the bidder and the expert

or the target and the expert. A contravention of one of those subsections

results in the bidder's statement not complying with this subsection.

 </dl></dl>

_Consent of person to whom statement attributed_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>The bidder's statement may only include, or be accompanied by, a statement

by a person, or a statement said in the bidder's statement to be based on a

statement by a person, if:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the person has consented to the statement being included in the bidder's

statement, or accompanying it, in the form and context in which it is included;

and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the bidder's statement states that the person has given this consent;

and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the person has not withdrawn this consent before the bidder's statement is

lodged with ASIC.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>The bidder must keep the consent.

</dd> </dl>

637  Bidder's statement formalities

<dl compact="">

		_Approval_ <dt>(1)</dt><dd>The copy of the bidder's statement that is lodged with ASIC must be approved by: </dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>for a bidder that is a body corporate:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>if the consideration offered under the bid is a cash sum only&#151;a

resolution passed by the directors of the bidder; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>otherwise&#151;a unanimous resolution passed by all the directors of the

bidder; or

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>for a bidder who is an individual&#151;the bidder.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>The bidder's statement must be dated. The date is the date on which it is

lodged with ASIC.

</dd> </dl>

Division 3&#151;The target's response
 638  Target's statement content

_General requirement_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>A target's statement must include all the information that holders of bid

class securities and their professional advisers would reasonably require to

make an informed assessment whether to accept the offer under the bid. The

statement must contain this information:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>only to the extent to which it is reasonable for investors and their

professional advisers to expect to find the information in the statement; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>only if the information is known to any of the directors of the target.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>In deciding what information should be included under subsection (1), have

regard to:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the nature of the bid class securities; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>if the bid class securities are interests in a managed investment

scheme&#151;the nature of the scheme; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the matters that the holders of bid class securities may reasonably be

expected to know; and</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>the fact that certain matters may reasonably be expected to be known to

their professional advisers; and</dd>

<dt>(e)</dt><dd>the time available to the target to prepare the statement.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

_Director&apos;s recommendations_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>A target's statement must contain a statement by each director of the

target:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>recommending that offers under the bid be accepted or not accepted, and

giving reasons for the recommendation; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>giving reasons why a recommendation is not made.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>The statement under subsection (3) must be made by:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>if the target is under administration&#151;the liquidator or administrator;

or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>if the target has executed a deed of company arrangement that has not yet

terminated&#151;the deed's administrator.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

_Consent of person to whom statement attributed_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(5)</dt><dd>The target's statement may only include, or be accompanied by, a statement

by a person, or a statement said in the target's statement to be based on a

statement by a person, if:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the person has consented to the statement being included in the target's

statement, or accompanying it, in the form and context in which it is included;

and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the target's statement states that the person has given this consent;

and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the person has not withdrawn this consent before the target's statement is

lodged with ASIC.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(6)</dt><dd>The target must keep the consent.

</dd> </dl>

639  Target's statement formalities

<dl compact="">

		_Approval_ <dt>(1)</dt><dd>The copy of the target's statement that is lodged with ASIC must be approved by: </dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>if paragraphs (b) and (c) do not apply&#151;a resolution passed by the

directors of the target; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>for a target that is under administration&#151;the liquidator or

administrator; or</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>for a target that has executed a deed of company arrangement that has not

yet terminated&#151;the deed's administrator.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

_Date_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>The target's statement must be dated. The date is the date on which it is

lodged with ASIC.

</dd> </dl>

640  Expert's report to accompany target's statement if bidder connected with target

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>If:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the bidder's voting power in the target is 30% or more; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>for a bidder who is, or includes, an individual&#151;the bidder is a director

of the target; or</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>for a bidder who is, or includes, a body corporate&#151;a director of the

bidder is a director of the target;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

a target's statement given in accordance with section 638 must include, or be accompanied by, a report by an expert that states whether, in the expert's opinion, the takeover offers are fair and reasonable and gives the reasons for forming that opinion.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Subsections 648A(2) and (3) provide for the independence of

the expert and disclosure of any association between the target and the expert

or the bidder and the expert. A contravention of one of those subsections

results in the target's statement not complying with this subsection.

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>In determining whether the bidder's voting power in the target is 30% or

more, calculate the bidder's voting power at the time the bidder's statement is

sent to the target.

</dd> </dl>

641  Target must inform bidder about securities holdings

_Requirement to inform bidder and information that must be given_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>If the bidder has given a bidder's statement to the target and requested

the target to give the bidder information in accordance with this section, the

target must inform the bidder of:

</dd> </dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the name and address of each person who, at a time specified by the bidder

under subsection (2), held securities:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>in the bid class; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>convertible into securities in the bid class; and

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the type, and number of each type, of those securities held by the person

at the specified time.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

However, the target does not need to give information to the bidder about a person or their holding of securities unless the target knows the person's name.

_Time at which target&apos;s information must be correct_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>The bidder's request must specify a day as at which the information must

be correct. The day must be one that occurs after the day on which the bidder

makes the request unless the target agrees to it being the day on which the

bidder makes the request.

</dd> </dl>

_Form in which target must provide information_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>The target must give the information to the bidder:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>in the form that the bidder requests; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>if the target is unable to comply with the request&#151;in writing.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

(4)	If the target must give the information to the bidder in electronic

form, the information must be readable but the information need not be

formatted for the bidder's preferred operating system.

 </dl>

_Fee for provision of information_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(5)</dt><dd>The target may require the bidder to pay an amount, not exceeding the

prescribed amount, for the provision of the information to the bidder.

</dd> </dl>

_Time by which target must provide information_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(6)</dt><dd>The target must give the information to the bidder no later than the

latest of the following times:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the end of the second day after the day on which the bidder requested the

information; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the end of the next day after the day as at which the information must be

correct; or</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the time when the target receives the amount mentioned in subsection (5).

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

642  Expenses of directors of target companies

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>If the target is a company or body, the directors of the target have a

right to recover from the target any expenses they reasonably incur in the

interest of members of the target and in relation to the takeover bid. The

directors have this right regardless of anything contained in the target's

constitution (if any).</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>If the target is a managed investment scheme, the responsible entity for the scheme has a right to recover from scheme property any expenses it reasonably incurs in the interest of members of the scheme and in relation to the takeover bid. The responsible entity has this right regardless of anything contained in the scheme's constitution. </dd> </dl>

Division 4&#151;Updating and correcting the bidder's statement and target's statement
 643  Supplementary bidder's statement

<dl compact="">

		If a bidder becomes aware of:

 </dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>a misleading or deceptive statement in the bidder's statement; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>an omission from the bidder's statement of information required by section

636; or</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>a new circumstance that:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>has arisen since the bidder's statement was lodged; and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>would have been required by section 636 to be included in the bidder's

statement if it had arisen before the bidder's statement was lodged;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

that is material from the point of view of a holder of bid class securities, the bidder must prepare a supplementary bidder's statement that remedies this defect.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note 1:	The bidder must then send and lodge the supplementary

bidder's statement in accordance with section 647\. Note 2:	Section 670A makes it an offence to give a bidder's statement after the bidder has become aware of a misleading or deceptive statement, omission or new circumstance that is material from the point of view of a holder of securities to whom the statement is given (unless the deficiency is corrected). Note 3:	The power to issue a supplementary bidder's statement is not limited to the situations dealt with in this section. Note 4:	This section applies to a bidder's statement that has already been previously supplemented.  </dl></dl>

644  Supplementary target's statement

<dl compact="">

		If a target becomes aware of:

 </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>a misleading or deceptive statement in the target's statement; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>an omission from the target's statement of information required by section

638; or</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>a new circumstance that:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>has arisen since the target's statement was lodged; and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>would have been required by section 638 to be included in the target's

statement if it had arisen before the target's statement was lodged;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

that is material from the point of view of a holder of bid class securities, the target must prepare a supplementary target's statement that remedies this defect.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note 1:	The target must then send and lodge the supplementary

target's statement in accordance with section 647\. Note 2:	Section 670A makes it an offence to give a target's statement after the target has become aware of a misleading or deceptive statement, omission or new circumstance that is material  from the point of view of a holder of securities to whom the statement is given (unless the deficiency is corrected). Note 3:	The power to issue a supplementary target's statement is not limited to the situations dealt with in this section. Note 4:	This section applies to a target's statement that has already been previously supplemented.  </dl></dl>

645  Form of supplementary statement

_Identity as a supplementary statement_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>At the beginning of a supplementary bidder's or target's statement there

must be:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>a statement that it is a supplementary statement; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>an identification of the statement it supplements; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>an identification of any previous supplementary statements lodged with

ASIC in relation to the bid; and</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>a statement that it is to be read together with the statement it

supplements and any previous supplementary statements.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

_Approval of supplementary bidder&apos;s statement_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>The copy of the supplementary bidder's statement that is lodged with ASIC

must be approved by:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>for a bidder that is a body corporate:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>if the consideration offered under the bid is a cash sum only&#151;a

resolution passed by the directors of the bidder; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>otherwise&#151;a unanimous resolution passed by all the directors of the

bidder; or

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>for a bidder who is an individual&#151;the bidder.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

_Approval of supplementary target&apos;s statement_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>The copy of a supplementary target's statement that is lodged with ASIC

must be approved by:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>if paragraphs (b) and (c) do not apply&#151;a resolution passed by the

directors of the target; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>for a target that is under administration&#151;the liquidator or

administrator; or</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>for a target that has executed a deed of company arrangement that has not

yet terminated&#151;the deed's administrator.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

_Date_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>A supplementary statement must be dated. The date is the date on which it

is lodged with ASIC.

</dd> </dl>

646  Consequences of lodging a supplementary statement

<dl compact="">

		If a supplementary statement is lodged with ASIC, for the purposes of the

application of this Chapter and Chapter 6B to events that occur after the

lodgment, the bidder's or target's statement is taken to be the original

statement together with the supplementary statement.

 </dl>

647  To whom supplementary statement must be sent

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>A supplementary bidder's statement must be sent to the target as soon as

practicable.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>A supplementary target's statement must be sent to the bidder as soon as practicable.</dd> <dt>(3)</dt><dd>Either kind of supplementary statement must as soon as practicable be: </dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>lodged with ASIC; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>if the bid class securities are quoted and the target is listed&#151;sent to

each relevant securities exchange that has a stock market on which the target's

securities are quoted; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>if the bid is an off-market bid and the bid class securities are not

quoted&#151;sent to all holders of bid class securities who have not accepted an

offer under the bid.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Sections 648B and 648C provide for the manner in which

documents may be sent to holders.

 </dl></dl>

Division 5&#151;General rules on takeover procedure 

<division>Subdivision A&#151;Experts' reports</division>

648A  Experts' reports

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>If the bidder or target obtains 2 or more reports each of which could be

used for the purposes of subparagraph 636(1)(h)(iii) or subsection 640(1), the

bidder's or target's statement must be accompanied by a copy of each report.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>The expert must be someone other than an associate of the bidder or target.</dd> <dt>(3)</dt><dd>The report must set out details of: </dd> </dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>any relationship between the expert and:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>the bidder or an associate of the bidder; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>the target or an associate of the target;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		including any circumstances in which the expert gives them advice, or acts on

their behalf, in the proper performance of the functions attaching to the

expert's professional capacity or business relationship with them; and

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>any financial or other interest of the expert that could reasonably be

regarded as being capable of affecting the expert's ability to give an unbiased

opinion in relation to the matter being reported on; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>any fee, payment or other benefit (whether direct or indirect) that the

expert has received or will or may receive in connection with making the report.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	If the statement includes, or is accompanied by, the

report, it must state that the expert has consented to this being done (see

subsections 636(3) and 638(5)).

 </dl></dl>

Subdivision B&#151;Sending documents to holders of securities
 648B  Address at which bidder may send documents to holders of securities

<dl compact="">

		The bidder may send a document to a holder of securities for the purposes of

this Chapter at the address shown for the holder in the information given to

the bidder by the target under section 641\. This section does not limit the

address to which the document may be sent to the holder.

 </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Section 109X makes general provision for service of

documents.

 </dl></dl>

648C  Manner of sending documents to holders of securities

<dl compact="">

		If a document must be sent to the holder of securities under this Chapter,

the document must be sent:

 </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>if the document is to be sent to the holder in an external territory or

outside Australia&#151;by pre-paid airmail post or by courier; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>if the document is to be sent to the holder in Australia&#151;by pre-paid

ordinary post or by courier.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

Subdivision C&#151;Effect of proportional takeover approval provisions
 648D  Constitution may contain proportional takeover approval provisions

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>Subject to this Subdivision, the constitution of a company may contain

provisions to the effect that, if offers are made under a proportional takeover

bid for securities of the company:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the registration of a transfer giving effect to a takeover contract for

the bid is prohibited unless and until a resolution (an _approving resolution_) to approve the bid is passed in accordance with the

provisions; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>a person (other than the bidder or an associate of the bidder) who, as at

the end of the day on which the first offer under the bid was made, held bid

class securities is entitled to vote on an approving resolution; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>an approving resolution is to be voted on in whichever of the following

ways is specified in the provisions:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>at a meeting, convened and conducted by the company, of the persons

entitled to vote on the resolution;</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>by means of a postal ballot conducted by the company in accordance with a

procedure set out in the provisions;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		or, if the provisions so provide, in whichever of those ways is determined by

the directors of the company; and

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>an approving resolution that has been voted on is taken to have been

passed if the proportion that the number of votes in favour of the resolution

bears to the total number of votes on the resolution is greater than the

proportion specified in the provisions, and otherwise is taken to have been

rejected.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

The proportion specified under paragraph (d) must not exceed 50%.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Section 9 defines _proportional takeover bid_.

See paragraph 618(1)(b).

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>To be effective, an approving resolution in relation to a proportional

takeover bid must be passed before the _approving resolution deadline_. The deadline is the 14th day before the last day of the bid

period.

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	In certain circumstances, an approving resolution will be

taken to have been passed (see subsection 648E(3)).

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>Except to the extent to which a company's constitution provides otherwise:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the provisions that apply to a general meeting of the company apply, with

such modifications as the circumstances require, to a meeting convened under

the company's proportional takeover approval provisions; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>those provisions apply as if the meeting convened under the proportional

takeover provisions were a general meeting of the company.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

The provisions referred to in paragraph (a) may be the provisions of a law, provisions of the company's constitution or any other provisions.

648E  Resolution to be put if proportional bid made

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>If:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>a company's constitution contains proportional takeover approval

provisions; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>offers are made under a proportional bid for a class of the company's

securities;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

then:

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the company's directors must ensure that a resolution to approve the bid

is voted on in accordance with those provisions before the approving resolution

deadline; and</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>if the directors fail to ensure that a resolution of that kind is voted on

before the deadline, each of the directors contravenes this subsection.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Subsection 648D(2) sets the approving resolution deadline.

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>If a resolution to approve the bid is voted on in accordance with the

proportional takeover approval provisions before the approving resolution

deadline, the company must, on or before the deadline, give:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the bidder; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>if the company is listed&#151;each relevant securities exchange;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

a written notice stating that a resolution to approve the bid has been voted on and whether the resolution was passed or rejected.

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>If no resolution to approve the bid has been voted on in accordance with

the proportional takeover approval provisions as at the end of the day before

the approving resolution deadline, a resolution to approve the bid is taken,

for the purposes of those provisions, to have been passed in accordance with

those provisions.

</dd> </dl>

648F  Effect of rejection of approval resolution

<dl compact="">

		If a resolution to approve the bid is voted on, in accordance with the

proportional takeover approval provisions, before the approving resolution

deadline and is rejected:

 </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>despite section 652A:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>all offers under the bid that have not been accepted as at the end of

deadline; and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>all offers under the bid that have been accepted, and from whose

acceptance binding contracts have not resulted, as at the end of the deadline;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		are taken to be withdrawn at the end of the deadline; and

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>as soon as practicable after the deadline, the bidder must return to each

person who has accepted an offer referred to in subparagraph (a)(ii) any

documents that the person sent the bidder with the acceptance of the offer;

and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the bidder:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>is entitled to rescind; and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>must rescind as soon as practicable after the deadline;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		each binding takeover contract for the bid; and

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>a person who has accepted an offer made under the bid is entitled to

rescind their takeover contract.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

648G  Including proportional takeover provisions in constitution

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>A company's proportional takeover approval provisions, unless sooner

omitted from the constitution of the company, cease to apply at the end of:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>unless paragraph (b) or (c) applies&#151;3 years;</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>if the constitution provides that the provisions apply for a specified

period of less than 3 years and the provisions have not been renewed&#151;the

specified period; or</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>if the provisions have been renewed on at least one occasion and the

resolution, or the most recent resolution, renewing the provisions states that

the provisions are renewed for a specified period of less than 3 years&#151;the

specified period.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>The period referred to in subsection (1) starts:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>if the provisions were contained in the company's constitution when it was

incorporated or formed and have not been renewed&#151;at that time; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>if the provisions were inserted in the company's constitution and have not

been renewed&#151;when the provisions were inserted; or</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>if the provisions have been renewed on at least one occasion&#151;when the

provisions were renewed, or last renewed.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>When the provisions cease to apply, the company's constitution is, by

force of this subsection, altered by omitting the provisions.</dd> <dt>(4)</dt><dd>A company may renew its proportional takeover approval provisions. The provisions are to be renewed in the same manner as that in which the company could alter its constitution to insert proportional takeover approval provisions.</dd> <dt>(5)</dt><dd>With every notice that: </dd> </dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>specifies the intention to propose:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>a resolution to alter a company's constitution by inserting proportional

takeover approval provisions; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>a resolution to renew a company's proportional takeover approval

provisions; and

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>is sent to a person who is entitled to vote on the proposed resolution;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

the company must send a statement that:

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>explains the effect of the proposed provisions, or of the provisions

proposed to be renewed; and</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>explains the reasons for proposing the resolution and sets out the factual

matters and principles underlying those reasons; and</dd>

<dt>(e)</dt><dd>states whether, as at the day on which the statement is prepared, any of

the directors of the company is aware of a proposal by a person to acquire, or

to increase the extent of, a substantial interest in the company and, if so,

explains the extent (if any) to which the proposal has influenced the decision

to propose the resolution; and</dd>

<dt>(f)</dt><dd>for a proposed resolution to renew proportional takeover approval

provisions&#151;reviews both the advantages, and disadvantages, of the provisions

proposed to be renewed for:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>the directors; and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>the company's members;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		during the period during which the provisions have been in effect; and

<dt>(g)</dt><dd>discusses both the potential advantages, and the potential disadvantages,

of the proposed provisions, or of the provisions proposed to be renewed, for:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>the directors; and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>the company's members.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(6)</dt><dd>If, on a particular day, a company purports to:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>alter its constitution by inserting proportional takeover approval

provisions; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>renew its proportional takeover approval provisions;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

then:

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>holders who together hold not less than 10% (by number) of the issued

securities in a class of securities in the company to which the provisions

apply may, within 21 days after that day, apply to the Court to have the

purported alteration or renewal set aside to the extent to which it relates to

that class; and</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>unless and until an application made under paragraph (c) is finally

determined by the making of an order setting aside the purported alteration or

renewal to that extent, the company is taken for all purposes (other than the

purposes of an application of that kind):

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>to have validly altered its constitution by inserting the provisions

referred to in paragraph (a) applying to that class; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>to have validly renewed the provisions referred to in paragraph (b)

applying to that class.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(7)</dt><dd>An application under paragraph (6)(c) may be made, on behalf of the

holders entitled to make the application, by a holder or holders appointed by

them in writing.</dd> <dt>(8)</dt><dd>On an application under paragraph (6)(c), the Court may make an order setting aside the purported alteration or renewal to the extent to which it applies to that class if it is satisfied that it is appropriate in all the circumstances to do so. Otherwise the Court must dismiss the application.</dd> <dt>(9)</dt><dd>Within 14 days after the day on which the Court makes an order of the kind referred to in subsection (8) in relation to a company, the company must lodge a copy of the order with ASIC. </dd> </dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

648H  Effect of Subdivision

<dl compact="">

		This Subdivision applies notwithstanding anything contained in:

 </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the business rules or listing rules of a securities exchange; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the constitution of a company; or</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>any agreement.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

Part 6.6&#151;Variation of offers
 Division 1&#151;Market bids
 649A  General

<dl compact="">

		A bidder may only vary the offers under a market bid in accordance with

section 649B or 649C.

 </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	ASIC may allow other variations under section 655A.

 </dl></dl>

649B  Market bids&#151;raising bid price

<dl compact="">

		The bidder may increase the current market bid price. They may not do so,

however, during the last 5 trading days of the relevant securities exchange in

the offer period.

 </dl>

649C  Market bids&#151;extending the offer period

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>The bidder may extend the offer period. The extension must be announced to

the relevant securities exchange at least 5 trading days of the exchange before

the end of the offer period. However, the announcement may be made up to the

end of the offer period if during those 5 trading days:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>another person lodges with ASIC a bidder's statement for a takeover bid

for securities in the bid class; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>another person announces a takeover bid for securities in the bid class;

or</dd>

(c)	another person makes offers under a takeover bid for securities in

the bid class; or

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>the consideration for offers under another takeover bid for securities in

the bid class is improved.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

The offer period is extended by having the extension announced to the relevant securities exchange.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Section 624 provides for an automatic extension of the bid

period in certain circumstances.

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>On the day on which the announcement is made, the bidder must:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>give the target and the relevant securities exchange a notice setting out

the terms of the announcement; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>lodge a notice setting out the terms of the announcement with ASIC.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

Division 2&#151;Off-market bids (express variation by bidder)
 650A  General

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>A bidder may only vary the offers under an off-market bid in accordance

with section 650B, 650C or 650D.

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	ASIC may allow other variations under section 655A.

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>If the bidder varies the offer under an off-market bid in accordance with

section 650B, 650C or 650D, the bidder must vary all unaccepted offers under

the bid in the same way.

</dd> </dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Subsections 650B(2) and (3) deal with the effect of a

variation on takeover contracts that have already resulted from acceptances of

offers under the bid when the variation is made.

 </dl></dl>

650B  Off-market bids&#151;consideration offered

_Improving the consideration offered_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>The bidder may vary the offers made under the bid to improve the

consideration offered:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>by increasing a cash sum offered; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>by increasing the number of securities offered; or</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>by increasing the rate of interest payable under debentures offered; or</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>by increasing the amount or value of debentures offered; or</dd>

<dt>(e)</dt><dd>by increasing the number of unissued securities that may be acquired under

options offered; or</dd>

<dt>(f)</dt><dd>by offering a cash sum in addition to securities; or</dd>

<dt>(g)</dt><dd>if the securities being acquired include shares to which rights to accrued

dividends are attached&#151;by giving the holders the right to:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>retain the whole or a part of the dividend; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>be paid an amount equal to the amount of the dividend;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		in addition to the consideration already offered; or

<dt>(h)</dt><dd>offering an additional alternative form of consideration.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	If the bidder increases the consideration during the last 7

days of the offer period, subsection 624(2) extends the offer period by a

further 14 days.

 </dl></dl>

_Effect of increase in consideration on offers already accepted_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>Improving the consideration has the effects set out in the following table

on the rights of a person who has already accepted an offer when the variation

is made.

</dd> </dl>

<table><tr align="left">
  <th colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>Effect of improving consideration</div>

  </th>
  <th colspan="1" align="right">
    <div>\[operative]</div>

  </th>
</tr>
<tr align="left">
  <th colspan="1" align="left">

  </th>
  <th colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>Improvement</div>

  </th>
  <th colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>Effect on person who has already accepted bid offer</div>

  </th>
</tr>
<tr align="left">
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>1</div>

  </td>
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>improvement of the only form of consideration being offered</div>

  </td>
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>entitled to the improved consideration</div>

  </td>
</tr>
<tr align="left">
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>2</div>

  </td>
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>2 or more forms of consideration offered and all forms improved by the same factor or percentage</div>

  </td>
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>entitled to the improvement in the form of consideration accepted</div>

  </td>
</tr>

  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>3</div>

  </td>
  <td colspan="1" align="left">

  </td>

  <td colspan="1" align="left">

  </td>

  </td>
</tr>
<tr align="left">
  <td colspan="1" align="left">

  </td>
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>any other improvement</div>

  </td>
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>entitled to make a fresh election as to the form of consideration to be taken</div>

  </td>
</tr></table>

<center>Back to Top</center>

The person is entitled to receive the improved consideration immediately, or immediately after the exercise of the election.

_Fresh election as to the form of consideration_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>If a person who has already accepted an offer has the right to make a

fresh election as to the form of consideration to be taken, the bidder must

send the person as soon as practicable after the variation a written notice

informing them about their right to make the election.

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note 1:	Section 651B says how the election is to be exercised. Note 2:	Sections 648B and 648C provide for the manner in which documents may be sent to holders.  </dl></dl>

650C  Off-market bids&#151;extension of offer period

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>A bidder making an off-market bid may extend the offer period at any time

before the end of the offer period.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>If the bid is subject to a defeating condition, the bidder may extend the offer period after the publication of the notice under subsection 630(3) only if one of the following happens after the publication: </dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>another person lodges with ASIC a bidder's statement for a takeover bid

for securities in the bid class</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>another person announces a takeover bid for securities in the bid class</dd>

(c)	another person makes offers under a takeover bid for securities in

the bid class

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>the consideration for offers under another takeover bid for securities in

the bid class is improved.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Section 624 says how long the total offer period can be.

 </dl></dl>

650D  Off-market bids&#151;method of making variation

_Variation to be made by notice to the target and holders_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>To vary offers under an off-market bid, the bidder must:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>prepare a notice that:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>sets out the terms of the proposed variation; and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>if the bid is subject to a defeating condition and the proposed variation

postpones for more than 1 month the time by which the bidder must satisfy their

obligations under the bid&#151;informs people about the right to withdraw

acceptances under section 650E; and

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>lodge the notice with ASIC; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>after the notice is lodged, give the notice to:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>the target; and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>everyone to whom offers were made under the bid.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Sections 648B and 648C provide for the manner in which

documents may be sent to holders.

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>A person must be sent a copy of the notice under subparagraph (1)(c)(ii)

even if they have already accepted the offer. However, they need not be sent a

copy if:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the variation merely extends the offer period; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the bid is not subject to a defeating condition at the time the notice is

given to the target. 

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>A notice under subsection (1) must be signed by:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>if the bidder is, or includes, an individual&#151;the individual; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>if the bidder is, or includes, a body corporate with 2 or more

directors&#151;not fewer than 2 of the directors who are authorised to sign the

notice by a resolution passed at a directors' meeting; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>if the bidder is, or includes, a body corporate that has only one

director&#151;that director.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>A copy of a notice given to a person under subparagraph (1)(c)(ii) must

include a statement that:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>a copy of the notice was lodged with ASIC on a specified date; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>ASIC takes no responsibility for the contents of the notice.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

650E  Right to withdraw acceptance

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>A person who accepts an offer made under an off-market bid may withdraw

their acceptance of the offer if:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the bid is subject to a defeating condition; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the bidder varies the offers under the bid in a way that postpones for

more than 1 month the time when the bidder has to meet their obligations under

the bid; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the person is entitled to be given a notice of the variation under

subsection 650D(1).

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>To withdraw their acceptance, the person must:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>give the bidder notice within 1 month beginning on the day after the day

on which the copy of the notice of the variation was received; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>return any consideration received by the person for accepting the offer.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>A notice under paragraph (2)(a):

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>if it relates to securities that are entered on an SCH subregister&#151;must

be in an electronic form approved by the SCH business rules for the purposes of

this Part; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>if it relates to shares that are not entered on an SCH subregister&#151;must

be in writing. 

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>To return consideration that includes securities, the person must:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>if the securities are entered on an SCH subregister&#151;take the action that

the SCH business rules require in relation to the return of the securities;

or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>otherwise&#151;give the bidder any transfer documents needed to effect the

return of securities.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(5)</dt><dd>If the person withdraws their acceptance, the bidder must:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>take any action that the SCH business rules require in relation to any of

the securities to which the acceptance relates that are entered on an SCH

subregister; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>return any documents that the person sent the bidder with the acceptance

of the offer;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

within 14 days after:

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

.	(c)	if the person does the things referred to in subsection (2) on the same

day&#151;that day; or

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>if the person does those things on different days&#151;the last of those days.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(6)</dt><dd>If under this section a person returns to a company any certificates

(together with any necessary transfer documents) in respect of the securities

issued by the company, the company must cancel those securities as soon as

possible. Any reduction in share capital is authorised by this subsection.

</dd> </dl>

650F  Freeing off-market bids from defeating conditions

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>If the offers under an off-market bid are subject to a defeating

condition, the bidder may free the offers, and the takeover contracts, from the

condition only by giving the target a notice declaring the offers to be free

from the condition in accordance with this section:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>if the condition is that the bidder may withdraw unaccepted offers if an

event or circumstance referred to in subsection 652C(1) or (2) occurs in

relation to the target&#151;not later than 3 business days after the end of the

offer period; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>in any other case&#151;not less than 7 days before the end of the offer period.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>The notice must:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>state that the offers are free from the condition; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>specify the bidder's voting power in the company.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>The notice must be:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>if the securities in the bid class are quoted&#151;given to the relevant

securities exchange; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>if those securities are not quoted&#151;lodged with ASIC.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

650G  Contracts and acceptances void if defeating condition not fulfilled

<dl compact="">

		All takeover contracts, and all acceptances that have not resulted in binding

takeover contracts, for an off-market bid are void if:

 </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>offers made under the bid have at any time been subject to a defeating

condition; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the bidder has not declared the offers to be free from the condition

within the period before the date applicable under subsection 630(1) or (2);

and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the condition has not been fulfilled at the end of the offer period.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

A transfer of securities based on an acceptance or contract that is void under this section must not be registered.

Division 3&#151;Off-market bids (automatic variations)
 651A  Off-market bid&#151;effect on bid consideration of purchases made outside bid

_Effect of purchases outside bid on offers made under the bid_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>The offers made under an off-market bid, and the takeover contracts, are

varied under this section if:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the bidder purchases securities in the bid class outside the bid during

the bid period; and:</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the consideration for that purchase consists solely of a cash sum; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>either:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>the consideration, or 1 of the forms of consideration, payable under the

bid consists of a cash sum only and the consideration referred to in paragraph

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>is higher than the cash sum payable for the securities under the bid; or</dd></dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>a cash sum only is not the consideration, or 1 of the forms of

consideration, payable under the bid.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note 1:	Section 9 defines _takeover contract_. Note 2:	The effect of section 623 is that the purchase outside the bid has to be made through an on-market transaction (see subsection 623(1) and paragraph 623(3)(b)).  </dl></dl>

_Effect on unaccepted cash offers_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>If:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>one of the forms of consideration offered to a person under an off-market

bid is a cash sum only; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the person has not accepted the offer before the purchase outside the bid

occurs;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

the cash sum is taken to be increased to the highest outside purchase price before the offer is accepted.

_Effect on cash offers already accepted_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>The consideration payable for each security covered by a takeover contract

arising from the acceptance of an offer for a cash sum only is increased to the

highest outside purchase price. If the person who accepted the offer has

already received the whole or any part of the consideration under the contract,

they are entitled to receive the increase in consideration immediately.

</dd> </dl>

_Effect on non-cash offers accepted at any time during bid period_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>If:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>a person accepts an offer under a bid at any time during the bid period;

and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the consideration paid or provided, or to be paid or provided, under the

takeover contract arising from the acceptance of the offer does not consist of

a cash sum only;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

then:

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the person may elect to take as consideration for each security covered by

the takeover contract a cash sum equal to the highest outside purchase price

instead of the consideration they originally accepted; and</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>the bidder must give the person a written notice of their right to make

the election within 14 days after the end of the offer period.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Section 651B says how the election is to be exercised.

 </dl></dl>

651B  How to make an election for new forms of consideration

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>An election under section 650B or 651A to take a new form of consideration

must be made:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>by written notice to the bidder; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>within 1 month after the person receives the notice from the bidder of

their right to make the election.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>The person becomes entitled to the new form of consideration if they:

</dd> </dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>make the election; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>return to the bidder:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>any consideration they have already received; and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>any necessary transfer documents.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

651C  Returning securities as part of election

<dl compact="">

		If under section 651B a person returns to a company any certificates

(together with any necessary transfer documents) in respect of the securities

issued by a company, the company must cancel those securities as soon as

possible.

 </dl>

Part 6.7&#151;Withdrawal and suspension of offers

652A  Withdrawal of unaccepted offers under takeover bid

<dl compact="">

		Unaccepted offers under a takeover bid may only be withdrawn under section

652B or 652C.

 </dl>

652B  Withdrawal of takeover offers with ASIC consent

<dl compact="">

		Unaccepted offers under a takeover bid may be withdrawn with the written

consent of ASIC. ASIC may consent subject to conditions.

 </dl>

652C  Withdrawal of market bids

_Bidder entitled to withdraw if certain events happen during the offer period_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>The bidder may withdraw unaccepted offers made under a market bid if 1 of

the following happens during the bid period, but only if the bidder's voting

power in the target is at or below 50% when the event happens:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the target converts all or any of its shares into a larger or smaller

number of shares (see section 254H)</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the target or a subsidiary resolves to reduce its share capital in any

way</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the target or a subsidiary:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>enters into a buy-back agreement; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>resolves to approve the terms of a buy-back agreement under subsection

257C(1) or 257D(1) 

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>the target or a subsidiary issues shares, or grants an option over its

shares, or agrees to make such an issue or grant such an option </dd>

<dt>(e)</dt><dd>the target or a subsidiary issues, or agrees to issue, convertible notes</dd>

<dt>(f)</dt><dd>the target or a subsidiary disposes, or agrees to dispose, of the whole,

or a substantial part, of its business or property </dd>

<dt>(g)</dt><dd>the target or a subsidiary charges, or agrees to charge, the whole, or a

substantial part, of its business or property </dd>

<dt>(h)</dt><dd>the target or a subsidiary resolves to be wound up.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>The bidder may also withdraw unaccepted offers made under a market bid if

1 of the following happens during the bid period:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>a liquidator or provisional liquidator of the target or of a subsidiary is

appointed </dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>a court makes an order for the winding up of the target or of a subsidiary

</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>an administrator of the target, or of a subsidiary, is appointed under

section 436A, 436B or 436C </dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>the target or a subsidiary executes a deed of company arrangement</dd>

<dt>(e)</dt><dd>a receiver, or a receiver and manager, is appointed in relation to the

whole, or a substantial part, of the property of the target or of a subsidiary.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

This is so regardless of the bidder's voting power at the time.

<dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>Notice of the withdrawal must be given to each relevant securities

exchange.

</dd> </dl>

Part 6.8&#151;Acceptances

653A  Acceptance of offers made under off-market bid

<dl compact="">

		If:

 </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>an offer is made under an off-market bid for quoted securities; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the SCH business rules require that an acceptance of the offer, so far as

it relates to those securities, must be made in a particular way;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

an acceptance of the offer for those securities is effective only if it is made in that way.

653B  Acceptances by transferees and nominees of offers made under off-market bid

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>If an off-market bid is made for securities:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>a person who:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>is able during the offer period to give good title to a parcel of those

securities; and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>has not already accepted an offer under the bid for those securities;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		may accept as if an offer on terms identical with the other offers made under

the bid had been made to that person in relation to those securities; and

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>a person who holds 1 or more parcels of those securities as trustee or

nominee for, or otherwise on account of, another person may accept as if a

separate offer had been made in relation to:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>each of those parcels; and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>any parcel they hold in their own right.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

If a person accepts an offer under a proportional takeover bid for securities, no-one else may accept an offer under the bid in respect of those securities.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Section 9 defines _proportional takeover bid_.

See paragraph 618(1)(b).

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>For the purposes of this section:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>a person is taken to hold securities if the person is, or is entitled to

be registered as, the holder of the securities; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>a person is taken to hold the securities on trust for, as nominee for or

on account of another person if they:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>are entitled to be registered as the holder of particular securities;

and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>hold their interest in the securities on trust for, as nominee for or on

account of that other person; and

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>in determining under subsection (1) whether a person has accepted an offer

for particular securities under a takeover bid, a person who accepts an offer

under a proportional takeover bid is taken to have accepted the offer for all

the securities in the bid class that they hold at the time they accept the

offer.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>If under paragraph (1)(b) a person may accept as if a separate offer is

taken to be made to a person for a parcel of securities within a holding, an

acceptance of that offer is ineffective unless:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the person gives the bidder a notice stating that the securities consist

of a separate parcel; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the acceptance specifies the number of securities in the parcel.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>A notice under subsection (3) must be made:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>if it relates to securities that are entered on an SCH subregister&#151;in an

electronic form approved by the SCH business rules for the purposes of this

Part; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>if it relates to shares that are not entered on an SCH subregister&#151;in

writing. 

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(5)</dt><dd>A person contravenes this subsection if:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>they purport to accept an offer under this section; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the acceptance is not made in accordance with this section.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

The acceptance is, however, as valid as it would have been if it had been made in accordance with this section.

<dl compact="">

<dt>(6)</dt><dd>A person may, at the one time, accept for 2 or more parcels under this

section as if there had been a single offer for a separate parcel consisting of

those parcels.

</dd> </dl>

Part 6.9&#151;Other activities during the bid period
 654A  Bidder not to dispose of securities during the bid period

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>The bidder must not dispose of any securities in the bid class during the

bid period.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>Subsection (1) does not apply to a disposal of securities by the bidder if: </dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>someone else who is not an associate of the bidder makes an offer, or

improves the consideration offered, under a takeover bid for securities in the

bid class after the bidder's statement is given to the target; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the bidder disposes of the securities after the offer is made or the

consideration is improved.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

654B  Disclosures about substantial shareholdings in listed companies

<dl compact="">

		During the bid period, substantial shareholding notices that need to be

lodged under section 671B must be lodged by 9.30 am the next business day

(rather than the usual 2 days).

 </dl>

654C  Disclosures about substantial shareholdings in unlisted companies

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>A bidder making a bid for securities of an unlisted company must give the

target a notice stating the bidder's voting power in the target if, at a

particular time during the bid period, the bidder's voting power in the target

rises from below a percentage in the following list to that percentage or

higher:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>25%</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>50%</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>75%</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>90%.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>The notice must be given as soon as practicable, and in any event within 2

business days, after the rise in voting power occurred.</dd> <dt>(3)</dt><dd>The target must: </dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>make the notice available at its registered office for inspection without

charge by any holder of bid class securities  during the bid period;

and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>lodge the notice with ASIC.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

Part 6.10&#151;Review and intervention
 Division 1&#151;ASIC's power to exempt and modify
 655A  ASIC's power to exempt and modify

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>ASIC may:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>exempt a person from a provision of this Chapter; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>declare that this Chapter applies to a person as if specified provisions

were omitted, modified or varied as specified in the declaration.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Under section 656A, the Panel has power to review the

exercise by ASIC of its powers under this section.

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>In deciding whether to give the exemption or declaration, ASIC must

consider the purposes of this Chapter set out in section 602.</dd> <dt>(3)</dt><dd>The exemption or declaration may: </dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>apply to all or specified provisions of this Chapter; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>apply to all persons, specified persons, or a specified class of persons;

and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>relate to all securities, specified securities or a specified class of

securities; and</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>relate to any other matter generally or as specified.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>An exemption may apply unconditionally or subject to specified conditions.

A person to whom a condition specified in an exemption applies must comply with

the condition. The Court may order the person to comply with the condition in a

specified way _._ Only ASIC may apply to the Court for the order.</dd> <dt>(5)</dt><dd>The exemption or declaration must be in writing and ASIC must publish notice of it in the _Gazette_.</dd> <dt>(6)</dt><dd>For the purposes of this section, the _provisions of this Chapter_ include: </dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>regulations made for the purposes of this Chapter; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>definitions in this Law or the regulations as they apply to references in:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>this Chapter; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>regulations made for the purposes of this Chapter; and

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>Division 12 of Part 11.2.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

655B  Notice of decision and review rights

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>Subject to subsection (3), ASIC must take such steps as are reasonable in

the circumstances to give to each person whose interests are affected by a

decision under a section 655A notice, in writing or otherwise:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>of the making of the decision; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>of the person's right to have the decision reviewed by the Panel under

section 656A.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>Subsection (1) does not require ASIC to give notice to a person affected

by the decision or to the persons in a class of persons affected by the

decision, if ASIC determines that giving notice to the person or persons is not

warranted, having regard to:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the cost of giving notice to the person or persons; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the way in which the interests of the person or persons are affected by

the decision.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>A failure to comply with this section does not affect the validity of the

decision.

</dd> </dl>

Division 2&#151;The Corporations and Securities Panel
 Subdivision A&#151;Review of ASIC's exercise of its exemption or modification powers
 656A  Review of exercise of exemption or modification powers

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>The Panel may review:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>a decision of ASIC under section 655A; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>a decision of ASIC under section 673 in relation to securities of the

target of a takeover bid during the bid period.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

For these purposes, _decision_ has the same meaning as in the _Administrative Appeals Tribunal Act 1975_.

<dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>An application to the Panel for review of the decision may be made by any

person whose interests are affected by the decision.</dd> <dt>(3)</dt><dd>For the purpose of reviewing the decision, the Panel may exercise all the powers and discretions conferred on ASIC by this Chapter or Chapter 6C. The Panel must make a decision: </dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>affirming the decision; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>varying the decision; or</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>setting aside the decision and:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>making a decision in substitution for the decision under review; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>remitting the matter for reconsideration by ASIC in accordance with any

directions or recommendations of the Panel.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>The decision must be in writing and published in the _Gazette._</dd> <dt>(5)</dt><dd>If the Panel varies an ASIC decision, or makes a decision in substitution for an ASIC decision: </dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the ASIC decision as varied, or the substituted decision, is taken for all

purposes (other than the purposes of applications to the Panel for review in

accordance with this section) to be a decision of ASIC under section 655A;

and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>when the Panel's determination on the review comes into operation, the

ASIC decision as varied, or the substituted decision, has effect, or is taken

to have had effect, on and from the day on which the ASIC decision has or had

effect.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

Paragraph (b) applies unless the Panel otherwise orders.

656B  Operation and implementation of a decision that is subject to review

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>Subject to this section, applying to the Panel under section 656A for

review of an ASIC decision does not:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>affect the operation of the decision; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>prevent the taking of action to implement the decision.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>On application by a party to the proceedings before the Panel, the Panel

may:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>make an order staying, or otherwise affecting the operation or

implementation of, the whole or a part of the decision if the Panel considers

that:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>it is desirable to make the order after taking into account the interests

of any person who may be affected by the review; and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>the order is appropriate for the purpose of securing the effectiveness of

the hearing and determination of the application for review; or

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>make an order varying or revoking an order made under paragraph (a)

(including an order that has previously been varied on one or more occasions

under this paragraph).

</dd>
