</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>Subject to subsection (4), the Panel must not:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>make an order under paragraph (2)(a) unless ASIC has been given a

reasonable opportunity to make a submission to the Panel in relation to the

matter; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>make an order under paragraph (2)(b) unless:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>ASIC; and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>the person who requested the making of the order under paragraph (2)(a);

and</dd>

<dt>(iii)</dt><dd>if the order under paragraph (2)(a) has previously been varied by an

order or orders under paragraph (2)(b)&#151;the person or persons who applied for

the last-mentioned order or orders;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		have been given a reasonable opportunity to make submissions to the Panel in

relation to the matter.

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>Subsection (3) does not prohibit the Panel from making an order without

giving to a person referred to in that subsection a reasonable opportunity to

make a submission to the Panel in relation to a matter if the Panel is

satisfied that, by reason of the urgency of the case or otherwise, it is not

practicable to give that person such an opportunity. If an order is so made

without giving such an opportunity to ASIC, the order does not come into

operation until a notice setting out the terms of the order is served on

ASIC.</dd> <dt>(5)</dt><dd>An order in force under paragraph (2)(a) (including an order that has previously been varied on one or more occasions under paragraph (2)(b)): </dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>is subject to the conditions that are specified in the order; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>has effect until:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>if a period for the operation of the order is specified in the order&#151;the

end of that period or, if the application for review is decided by the Panel

before the end of that period, the decision of the Panel on the application for

review comes into operation; or </dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>if a period for the operation of the order is not specified in the

order&#151;the decision of the Panel on the application for review comes into

operation.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

Subdivision B&#151;Unacceptable circumstances
 657A  Declaration of unacceptable circumstances

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>The Panel may declare circumstances in relation to the affairs of a

company to be unacceptable circumstances. Without limiting this, the Panel may

declare circumstances to be unacceptable circumstances whether or not the

circumstances constitute a contravention of a provision of this Law.

</dd> </dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Sections 659B and 659C deal with court proceedings during

and after a takeover bid.

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>The Panel may only declare circumstances to be unacceptable circumstances

if it appears to the Panel that the circumstances:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>are unacceptable having regard to the effect of the circumstances on:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>the control, or potential control, of the company or another company; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>the acquisition, or proposed acquisition, by a person of a substantial

interest in the company or another company; or

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>are unacceptable because they constitute, or give rise to, a contravention

of a provision of this Chapter or of Chapter 6A, 6B or 6C.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

The Panel may only make a declaration under this subsection, or only decline to make a declaration under this subsection, if it considers that doing so is not against the public interest after taking into account any policy considerations that the Panel considers relevant.

<dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>In exercising its powers under this section, the Panel:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>must have regard to:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>the purposes of this Chapter set out in section 602; and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>the other provisions of this Chapter; and</dd>

<dt>(iii)</dt><dd>the rules made under section 658C; and</dd>

<dt>(iv)</dt><dd>the matters specified in regulations made for the purposes of paragraph

195(3)(c) of the _Australian Securities and Investments Commission Act 1989_; and

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>may have regard to any other matters it considers relevant.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

In having regard to the purpose set out in paragraph 602(1)(c) in relation to an acquisition, or proposed acquisition, of a substantial interest in a company, body or scheme, the Panel must take into account the actions of the directors of the company or body or the responsible entity for a scheme (including actions that caused the acquisition or proposed acquisition not to proceed or contributed to it not proceeding).

<dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>The Panel must give an opportunity to make submissions in relation to the

matter to:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>each person to whom a proposed declaration relates; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>each party to the proceedings; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>ASIC.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(5)</dt><dd>The declaration must be in writing and published in the _Gazette._</dd> <dt>(6)</dt><dd>As soon as practicable, the Panel must give each person to whom the declaration relates: </dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>a copy of the declaration; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>a written statement of the Panel's reasons for making the declaration.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(7)</dt><dd>This section does not require the Panel to perform a function, or exercise

a power, in a particular way in a particular case.

</dd> </dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

657B  When Panel may make declaration

<dl compact="">

		The Panel can only make a declaration under section 657A within:

 </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>3 months after the circumstances occur; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>1 month after the application under section 657C for the declaration was

made;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

whichever ends last. The Court may extend the period on application by the Panel.

657C  Applying for declarations and orders

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>The Panel may make a declaration under section 657A, or an order under

section 657D or 657E, only on an application made under this section.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>An application for a declaration under section 657A or an order under section 657D or 657E may be made by: </dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the bidder; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the target; or</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>ASIC; or</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>any other person whose interests are affected by the relevant

circumstances.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	The Administrative Appeals Tribunal cannot review ASIC's

decision whether to apply to the Panel (see paragraph 1317C(gc)).

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>An application for a declaration under section 657A can be made only

within:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>2 months after the circumstances have occurred; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>a longer period determined by the Panel.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

657D  Orders that Panel may make following declaration

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>The Panel may make an order under subsection (2) if it has declared

circumstances to be unacceptable under section 657A. It must not make an order

if it is satisfied that the order would unfairly prejudice any person. Before

making the order, the Panel must give:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>each person to whom a proposed order relates; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>each party to the proceedings; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>ASIC;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

an opportunity to make submissions to the Panel about the matter

<dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>The Panel may make any order (including a remedial order but not including

an order directing a person to comply with a requirement of Chapter 6, 6A, 6B

or 6C) that it thinks appropriate to:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>protect the rights or interests of any person affected by the

circumstances; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>ensure that a takeover bid or proposed takeover bid in relation to

securities proceeds (as far as possible) in a way that it would have proceeded

if the circumstances had not occurred; or</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>specify in greater detail the requirements of an order made under this

subsection; or</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>determine who is to bear the costs of the parties to the proceedings

before the Panel;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

regardless of whether it has previously made an order under this subsection or section 657E  in relation to the declaration. The Panel may also make any ancillary or consequential orders that it thinks appropriate.

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Section 9 defines _remedial order_.

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>The Panel may vary, revoke or suspend an order made under this section.

Before doing so, it must give an opportunity to make submissions in relation to

the matter to:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>each person to whom the order is directed; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>each party to the proceedings in which the order was made; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>ASIC.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>If the Panel makes an order under this section, the Panel must give a copy

of the order, and a written statement of its reasons for making the order, to:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>each party to the proceedings before the Panel; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>each person to whom the order is directed if they are not a party to the

proceedings; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>for an order relating to specified securities of a company&#151;the company;

and</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>ASIC.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

The Panel must also publish the order in the _Gazette._ The order takes effect as soon as it is made and not when all the requirements of this subsection are met.

<dl compact="">

<dt>(5)</dt><dd>If the Panel makes an order of the kind referred to in paragraph (j) of

the definition of _remedial order_, the exercise of rights attached

to shares is to be disregarded as provided in the order.</dd> <dt>(6)</dt><dd>If the Panel makes an order of the kind referred to in paragraph (k) of the definition of _remedial order_, then, by force of this subsection, the agreement or offer specified in the order is cancelled, or becomes voidable, as from the making of the order or any later time that is specified in the order. </dd> </dl>

657E  Interim orders

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>The Panel, or the President of the Panel, may make an interim order of a

kind referred to in subsection 657D(2) in relation to circumstances even if:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>there is no declaration under section 657A that the circumstances are

unacceptable; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>no application to the Panel for a declaration of that kind has been made.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

The order must specify the period (not exceeding 2 months) for which it is to have effect.

<dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>The order ceases to have effect:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>at the end of the period specified in the order; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>if, before the end of that period, proceedings for a declaration under

section 657A in relation to the circumstances (and all related proceedings for

an order under section 657D) are determined&#151;when those proceedings are

determined.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

657EA  Internal Panel reviews

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>The following may apply under this section for review by the Panel of a

decision of the Panel made on an application under section 657C:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>a party to the proceedings in which the decision was made; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>ASIC.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

For these purposes, _decision_ has the same meaning as in the _Administrative Appeals Tribunal Act 1975_.

<dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>If the decision is not:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>a decision to make a declaration under section 657A; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>a decision to make an order under section 657D or 657E;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

the person may apply for review only with the consent of the President of the Panel.

<dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>The regulations may provide for the time limits within which an

application may be made for review of a decision.

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Regulations made under the _Australian Securities and Investments Commission Act 1989_ deal with the constitution of the Panel for

the purposes of conducting a review under this section and the procedures to be

followed in conducting the review.

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>After conducting a review under this section, the Panel may:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>vary the decision reviewed; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>set aside the decision reviewed; or</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>set aside the decision reviewed and substitute a new decision.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

In conducting the review, the Panel has the same power to make a declaration under section 657A, or an order under section 657D or 657E, as it has when it is considering an application under section 657C.

657EB  References by Courts

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>A Court hearing proceedings in relation to a decision of the Panel made on

an application under section 657C may refer the decision to the Panel for

review.

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Regulations made under the _Australian Securities and Investments Commission Act 1989_ deal with the constitution of the Panel for

the purposes of conducting a review under this section and the procedures to be

followed in conducting the review.

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>After conducting a review under this section, the Panel may:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>vary the decision reviewed; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>set aside the decision reviewed; or</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>set aside the decision reviewed and substitute a new decision.</dd>

		In conducting the review, the Panel has the same powers to make a declaration

under section 657A, or an order under section 657D or 657E, as it has when it

is considering an application under section 657C.

</dl></dl></dl>

657F  Offence to contravene Panel order

<dl compact="">

		A person who contravenes an order made under section 657D or 657E commits an

offence.

 </dl>

657G  Orders by the Court where contravention or proposed contravention of Panel order

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>If a person contravenes, or proposes to engage in conduct that would

contravene, an order made by the Panel under section 657D or 657E, the Court

may make any orders it considers appropriate to secure compliance with the

Panel's order, including:

</dd> </dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>1 or more remedial orders; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>an order directing a person to do, or to refrain from doing, a specified

act.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Section 9 defines _remedial order_.

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>An application for an order under this section may only be made by:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>ASIC; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the President of the Panel; or</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>a person to whom the Panel's order relates; or</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>a person who was a party to the proceedings in which the Panel's order was

made.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

657H  ASIC may publish report about application to Panel or Court

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>ASIC may publish a report, statement or notice in relation to an

application it has made for:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>a declaration of unacceptable circumstances under section 657A; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>an order under subsection 657D(2); or</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>an order under section 657E; or</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>review under section 657EA of a decision of the Panel; or</dd>

<dt>(e)</dt><dd>an order under section 657G to secure compliance with an order made under

subsection 657D(2) or section 657E.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>The report, statement or notice must:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>state that the application has been made; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>name the company; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>if ASIC considers that the report, statement or notice should name any

other person to whom the declaration would relate or the order would be

directed&#151;name that other person.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>The report, statement or notice may be published in any way that ASIC

thinks appropriate. It need not be in writing.</dd> <dt>(4)</dt><dd>This section does not limit a function or power of ASIC, the Panel or any other person or body. </dd> </dl>

Subdivision C&#151;General provisions
 658A  Power of Panel where a proceeding is frivolous or vexatious 

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>If an application is made to the Panel under this Division, the Panel may,

at any stage of the proceeding, if it is satisfied that the application is

frivolous or vexatious:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>dismiss the application; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>if the Panel considers it appropriate, on the application of a party to

the proceedings, direct that the person who made the application must not,

without leave of the Panel, make a subsequent application to the Panel of a

kind or kinds specified in the direction.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>A direction given by the Panel under paragraph (1)(b) has effect despite

any other provision of this Act or a provision of any other Act.</dd> <dt>(3)</dt><dd>The Panel may revoke or vary the direction. </dd> </dl>

658B  Evidentiary value of findings of fact by Panel

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>A finding of fact recorded in an order by the Panel, or a written

statement of the reasons for an order of the Panel, is proof of the fact in the

absence of evidence to the contrary.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>A certificate signed by the President of the Panel that states a finding of fact made in proceedings before the Panel is proof of the fact in the absence of evidence to the contrary. </dd> </dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

658C  Panel's power to make rules

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>The President of the Panel may, after consultation with members of the

Panel, make rules, not inconsistent with the Law or the Regulations, to clarify

or supplement the operation of the provisions of this Chapter.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>In making rules under this section, the President of the Panel must consider the purposes of this Chapter set out in section 602.</dd> <dt>(3)</dt><dd>A rule under this section must be in writing and the President of the Panel must: </dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>publish notice of it in the _Gazette_; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>give the Minister, and ASIC, a copy of the rule as soon as practicable

after it is published in the _Gazette_.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>Within 28 days after receiving the copy, the Minister may disallow the

whole or a specified part of the rule.</dd> <dt>(5)</dt><dd>If a person contravenes a rule made under this section, the Court may give directions for compliance with the rule to: </dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>that person; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>if that person is a body corporate&#151;the directors of the body corporate.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

The Court must give the person against whom the order is sought, and any person aggrieved by the contravention, an opportunity to be heard before giving directions under this subsection.

<dl compact="">

<dt>(6)</dt><dd>The Court may give a direction under subsection (5) only on application by:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>ASIC; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the President of the Panel; or</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>a person aggrieved by the contravention.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

658D  Inconsistency between Panel and ASIC exemptions or modifications

<dl compact="">

		If there is an inconsistency between a rule made under section 658C and an

exemption or modification given by ASIC under section 655A, the rule made under

section 658C prevails to the extent of the inconsistency.

 </dl>

Division 3&#151;Court powers
 659A  Panel may refer questions of law to the Court

<dl compact="">

		The Panel may, of its own motion, refer a question of law arising in a

proceeding before the Panel to the Court for decision.

 </dl>

659AA  Object of sections 659B and 659C

<dl compact="">

		The object of sections 659B and 659C is to make the Panel the main forum for

resolving disputes about a takeover bid until the bid period has ended.

 </dl>

659B  Court proceedings before end of bid period

_Delay in commencing court proceedings until after end of bid period_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>Only:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>ASIC; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>another public authority of the Commonwealth or a State;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

may commence court proceedings in relation to a takeover bid, or proposed takeover bid, before the end of the bid period.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	This restriction starts to apply as soon as there is a

takeover bid, or a proposed takeover bid; it does not start to apply only when

the bid period commences.

 </dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

_Court power to stay proceedings that have already commenced_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>A court may stay:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>court proceedings in relation to a takeover bid or proposed takeover bid;

or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>court proceedings that would have a significant effect on the progress of

a takeover bid;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

until the end of the bid period.

<dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>In deciding whether to exercise its powers under subsection (2), the court

is to have regard to:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the purposes of this Chapter; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the availability of review by the Panel under Division 2.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>For the purposes of this section:

</dd> </dl>

<def><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

_court proceedings in relation to a takeover bid or proposed takeover bid_:

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>means any proceedings before a court in relation to:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>an action taken or to be taken as part of, or for the purposes of, the bid

or the target's response to the bid; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>a document prepared or to be prepared, or a notice given or to be given,

under this Chapter; and

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>includes:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>proceedings to enforce an obligation imposed by this Chapter; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>proceedings for the review of a decision, or the exercise of a power or

discretion, under this Chapter; or</dd>

<dt>(iii)</dt><dd>proceedings for the review of a decision, or the exercise of a power or

discretion, under Chapter 6C in relation to securities of the target of a

takeover bid during the bid period; and</dd>

<dt>(iv)</dt><dd>proceedings under Part 2F.1A for leave to bring, or to intervene in,

proceedings referred to in paragraph (a) or subparagraph (b)(i), (ii) or (iii).

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

This is not limited to proceedings brought under this Chapter or this Law but includes proceedings under other Commonwealth and State laws (including the general law).

659C  Court proceedings after end of bid period

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>If:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>an application is made to the Panel for a declaration under section 657A

that particular conduct amounts to, or leads to, circumstances that are

unacceptable; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the Panel refuses to make the declaration; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>a Court finds after the end of the bid period that the conduct contravenes

this Law;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

the Court's powers under this Law in relation to the conduct are limited to the following:

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>the Court may:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>determine whether a person is guilty of an offence against this Law

because they engaged in or were involved in the conduct; and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>impose a penalty if the person is found guilty

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(e)</dt><dd>the Court may:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>determine whether a person who engaged in, or was involved in, the conduct

contravened a provision of the Law; and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>order the person to pay an amount of money to another person (whether by

way of damages, account of profits, pecuniary penalty or otherwise)

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(f)</dt><dd>the Court may make an order under section 1318 or 1322 in relation to the

conduct.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

This subsection does not confer power or jurisdiction on a court that it does not have apart from this subsection.

<dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>Without limiting subsection (1), the only kind of remedial order that the

Court may make is one that requires the person to pay money to another person.

</dd> </dl>

Chapter 6A&#151;Compulsory acquisitions and buy-outs

660A  Chapter extends to some listed bodies that are not companies

<dl compact="">

		This Chapter extends to the acquisition of securities of listed bodies that

are not companies but are incorporated or formed in this jurisdiction in the

same way as it applies to the acquisition of securities of companies.

 </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Section 9 defines _company_,

_jurisdiction_ and _listed_.

 </dl></dl>

660B  Chapter extends to listed managed investment schemes

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>This Chapter extends to the acquisition of interests in a listed managed

investment scheme registered in this jurisdiction as if:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the scheme were a company; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>interests in the scheme were shares in the company; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>voting interests in the scheme were voting shares in the company.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>If Part 6A.1 applies to a scheme at the end of the bid period for a

takeover, that Part continues to apply to the scheme in relation to the

takeover bid even if the scheme ceases to be listed.</dd> <dt>(3)</dt><dd>If Part 6A.2 applies to a scheme when a compulsory acquisition notice under section 664C is lodged, that Part (including Division 2 of that Part) continues to apply to apply to the scheme in relation to the notice even if the scheme ceases to be listed.</dd> <dt>(4)</dt><dd>The regulations may modify the operation of this Chapter as it applies in relation to the acquisition of interests in listed managed investment schemes. </dd> </dl>

Part 6A.1&#151;Compulsory acquisitions and buy-outs following takeover bid
 Division 1&#151;Compulsory acquisition of bid class securities
 661A  Compulsory acquisition power following takeover bid

_Threshold for compulsory acquisition power_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>Under this subsection, the bidder under a takeover bid may compulsorily

acquire any securities in the bid class if:

</dd> </dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the bid is:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>an off-market bid to acquire all the securities in the bid class; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>a market bid; and

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>during, or at the end of, the offer period:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>the bidder and their associates have relevant interests in at least 90%

(by number) of the securities in the bid class; and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>the bidder and their associates have acquired at least 75% (by number) of

the securities that the bidder offered to acquire under the bid (whether the

acquisitions happened under the bid or otherwise).

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

This is so even if the bidder subsequently ceases to satisfy subparagraph (b)(i) because of the issue of further securities in the bid class.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Subsection 92(3) defines _securities_ for the

purposes of this Chapter.

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>For the purposes of subsection (1), disregard any relevant interests that

the bidder has merely because of the operation of subsection 608(3) (relevant

interest by 20% interest in body corporate).

</dd> </dl>

_Court may allow compulsory acquisition even if threshold not reached_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>Under this subsection, the bidder under a takeover bid may compulsorily

acquire securities in the bid class with the approval of the Court.

</dd> </dl>

_Securities to be acquired_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>If the bidder compulsorily acquires securities in the bid class under

subsection (1) or (3), the bidder:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>must acquire all the securities in the bid class:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>which were issued or granted before the end of the offer period; and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>in which the bidder does not have a relevant interest; and

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>may elect to acquire all securities in the bid class:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>that were issued or granted after the end of the offer period and before

the notice under section 661B is issued; and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>in which the bidder does not have a relevant interest;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		but only if the bidder and their associates have relevant interests in at

least 90% (by number) of the securities in the bid class when the bidder gives

notice under section 661B; and

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>if securities exist when the bidder gives the notice under section 661B

that:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>will convert, or may be converted, to securities in the bid class; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>confer rights to be issued securities in the bid class that may be

exercised;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		within the period of 6 weeks after the notice is given&#151;may elect to acquire

securities that come to be in the bid class during that period due to a

conversion or exercise of the rights but only if the bidder and their

associates have relevant interests in at least 90% of the securities (by

number) in the bid class when the bidder gives notice under section 661B; and

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>may elect to acquire any securities in the bid class in which the bidder

has a relevant interest (no matter when they were issued or granted).

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(5)</dt><dd>This section has effect despite anything in the constitution of the

company whose securities are to be acquired.

</dd> </dl>

661B  Compulsory acquisition notice

_Compulsory acquisition notice_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>To compulsorily acquire securities under subsection 661A(1) or (3), the

bidder must:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>prepare a notice in the prescribed form that:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>informs the holders of the securities that the bidder is entitled to

acquire their securities under that subsection; and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>informs the holders about the compulsory acquisition procedure under this

Part, including:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

	(A)	their right under section 661D to obtain the names and addresses of everyone else the bidder has given the notice to; and
 	(B)	their right under section 661E to apply to the Court for an order that the securities not be compulsorily acquired; and

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>lodge the notice with ASIC; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>give the notice to each other person who is:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>a holder of securities in the bid class; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>if the bidder elects under paragraph 661A(4)(c) to acquire securities

that come to be in the bid class after the notice is given&#151;a holder of the

convertible securities referred to in that paragraph; and

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>give a copy to each relevant securities exchange on the same day as it is

lodged with ASIC if the target is listed.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

If alternative forms of consideration were offered under the takeover bid, the notice must specify which of those forms of consideration will apply to the acquisition of the holder's securities if the holder does not elect one of the forms under paragraph 661C(2)(a).

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Everyone who holds bid class securities on the day on which

the notice is lodged with ASIC is entitled notice. Under section 661E, anyone

who holds the securities after that day may apply to the Court to stop the

acquisition.

 </dl></dl>

_Time for dispatching notices to holders_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>The bidder must dispatch the notices under paragraph (1)(c):

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>during the offer period, or within 1 month after:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>the end of offer period if the acquisition is under subsection 661A(1);

or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>the court approval if the acquisition is under subsection 661A(3); and

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>on the day the bidder lodges the notice with ASIC or on the next business

day.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

The notices cannot be withdrawn.

_Manner of giving notice to holders_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>The bidder may give the notice to a holder:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>personally; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>by sending it by post to the address for the holder in the register of

members, debenture holders or option holders.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

A notice sent by post is taken to be given 3 days after it is posted.

<dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>The notice may be sent:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>if the notice is to be sent to the holder in an external territory or

outside Australia&#151;by pre-paid airmail post or by courier; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>if the notice is to be sent to the holder in Australia&#151;by pre-paid

ordinary post or by courier.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

This section does not limit the manner in which the notice may be sent to the holder.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Section 109X makes general provision for service of

documents.

 </dl></dl>

661C  Terms on which securities to be acquired

_Same terms as takeover bid_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>The bidder may acquire the securities only on the terms that applied to

the acquisition of securities under the takeover bid immediately before:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the notice under section 661B is given if it is given before the end of

the offer period; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the end of the offer period if it is not.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

_Alternative forms of consideration under takeover bid_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>If alternative forms of consideration were offered under the takeover bid,

the form of consideration that applies to the acquisition of the holder's

securities is:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the form that the holder elects; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the form set out in the compulsory acquisition notice under subsection

661B(1).

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>The holder makes an election under subsection (2) by giving the bidder a

notice of the election by the later of:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>1 month after the compulsory acquisition notice is given under section

661B; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>14 days after the holder is given a statement under section 661D if the

holder asks for it.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>The election must be:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>in an electronic form approved by the SCH business rules for the purposes

of this Part if it relates to shares that are entered on an SCH subregister;

or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>in writing if it relates to shares that are not entered on an SCH

subregister.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

661D  Holder may obtain names and addresses of other holders

<dl compact="">

		Within 1 month after a compulsory acquisition notice in relation to

securities in the bid class is lodged with ASIC under section 661B, the holder

of the securities may ask the bidder in writing for a written statement of the

names and addresses of everyone else the bidder has given the notice to. The

bidder must give the holder the statement within 7 days after the request.

 </dl>

661E  Holder may apply to Court to stop acquisition

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>The holder of securities covered by a compulsory acquisition notice under

section 661B may apply to the Court for an order that the securities not be

compulsorily acquired under subsection 661A(1). The application must be made

before the later of:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the end of 1 month after the holder is given notice under section 661B;

or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the end of 14 days after the holder is given a statement under section

661D if the holder asks for it.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>The Court may order that the securities not be compulsorily acquired under

subsection 661A(1) only if the Court is satisfied that the consideration is not

fair value for the securities.

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	See section 667C on valuation.

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>If the Court makes an order under this section in relation to an

acquisition of securities, the order applies to all holders who have

applications to the Court pending for an order under this section in relation

to the acquisition.

</dd> </dl>

661F  Signpost&#151;completing the acquisition of the securities

<dl compact="">

		See section 666A to find out how to complete the acquisition.

 </dl>

Division 2&#151;Compulsory buy-out of bid class securities
 662A  Bidder must offer to buy out remaining holders of bid class securities

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>If the bidder and their associates have relevant interests in at least 90%

of the securities (by number) in the bid class at the end of the offer period,

the bidder must offer to buy out the remaining holders of bid class securities

in accordance with sections 662B and 662C.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>This section does not apply to securities that are issued: </dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>if the takeover bid was not subject to a defeating condition&#151;after the

end of the offer period; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>if the takeover bid was subject to a defeating condition&#151;after the notice

whether the bid is free from a defeating condition or not is given under

subsection 630(3).

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

662B  Bidder to tell remaining holders of their right to be bought out

_Notice to remaining holders of bid class securities_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>The bidder must:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>prepare a notice in the prescribed form that:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>states that the bidder and their associates have relevant interests in at

least 90% (by number) of the securities in the bid class; and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>informs the holder of bid class securities about their right to be bought

out under this Part; and</dd>

<dt>(iii)</dt><dd>sets out the terms on which the holder may be bought out; and

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>lodge the notice with ASIC; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>give the notice to each other person who:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>is a holder of securities in the bid class on the day on which the notice

is lodged with ASIC; and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>has not been given a compulsory acquisition notice under section 661B

when the notice under subsection (2) is given; and

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>give the notice to each relevant securities exchange on the same day as it

is lodged with ASIC if the target is listed.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

If alternative forms of consideration were offered under the takeover bid, the notice must specify which of those forms will apply to the acquisition of the holder's securities if the holder does not give the bidder an election notice under subsection 662C(1).

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	The notice is be given to everyone who holds bid class

securities on the day on which the notice is lodged with ASIC. Under section

662C, anyone who acquires the securities after that day may require the bidder

to acquire the securities.

 </dl></dl>

_Time for dispatching notice to holders_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>The bidder must dispatch the notices under paragraph (1)(c):

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>during, or within 1 month after the end of, the offer period; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>on the day the bidder lodges the notice with ASIC or on the next business

day.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

The notices cannot be withdrawn.

_Manner of giving notice to holders_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>The bidder may give the notice to a holder:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>personally; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>by sending it by post to the address for the holder in the register of

members, debenture holders or option holders.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

A notice sent by post is taken to be given 3 days after it is posted.

<dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>The notice may be sent:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>if the notice is to be sent to the holder in an external territory or

outside Australia&#151;by pre-paid airmail post or by courier.</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>if the notice is to be sent to the holder in Australia&#151;by pre-paid

ordinary post or by courier.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

This subsection does not limit the manner in which the document may be sent to the holder.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Section 109X makes general provision for service of

documents.

 </dl></dl>

662C  Right of remaining holder of securities in the bid class to be bought out

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>Within 1 month after notice is given in relation to securities under

section 662B, the holder of the securities may give the bidder written notice

requiring the bidder to acquire the securities. If alternative forms of

consideration were offered under the takeover bid, the holder may elect in the

notice which of those forms will apply to the acquisition of the holder's

securities.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>The notice by the holder gives rise to a contract between the holder and the bidder for the sale of the securities on: </dd> </dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the terms that applied to the acquisition of securities under the bid

immediately before the end of the offer period; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>if alternative forms of consideration applied at that time&#151;on the terms

that the bidder will provide:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>the alternative specified by the holder in the notice under subsection

(1); or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>if the holder has not made an election under that subsection&#151;the

alternative set out in the bidder's notice under section 662B; or

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>if the holder and the bidder agree on other terms&#151;those terms.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

Division 3&#151;Compulsory buy-out of convertible securities
 663A  Bidder must offer to buy out holders of convertible securities

<dl compact="">

		If the bidder and their associates have relevant interests in at least 90% of

the securities (by number) in the bid class at the end of the offer period, the

bidder must offer to buy out the holders of securities that are convertible

into bid class securities in accordance with sections 663B and 663C. This

section does not apply to securities if a takeover bid has been made for the

convertible securities and a notice has been given under section 661B or 662B

in relation to the convertible securities.

 </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	For when securities are convertible into bid class

securities, see the definition of _convertible securities_ in

section 9.

 </dl></dl>

663B  Bidder to tell holders of convertible securities of their right to be bought out

_Notice to holders of convertible securities_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>The bidder must:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>prepare a notice in the prescribed form that:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>states that the bidder and their associates have relevant interests in at

least 90% of the securities (by number) in the bid class; and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>informs the holder of convertible securities about their right to be

bought out under this Part; and</dd>

<dt>(iii)</dt><dd>sets out the terms on which the holder may be bought out; and

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>lodge the notice with ASIC; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>give each other person who is a holder of convertible securities:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>the notice; and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>a copy of the expert's report, or of all the experts' reports, under

section 667A; and

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>give a copy of those documents to each relevant securities exchange on the

same day as it is lodged with ASIC if the target is listed.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note 1:	Subparagraph (a)(iii)&#151;Section 667A deals with the

contents of an expert's report. Note 2:	The notice is to be given to everyone who holds convertible securities on the day on which the notice is lodged with ASIC. Under section 663C, anyone who acquires the securities after that day may require the bidder to acquire the securities.  </dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

_Time for dispatching notice to holders_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>The bidder must dispatch the notices and reports under paragraph (1)(c):

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>during, or within 1 month after the end of, the offer period; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>on the day the bidder lodges the notice with ASIC or on the next business

day.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

The notices cannot be withdrawn.

_Manner of giving notice to holders_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>The bidder may give the notice or report to a holder:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>personally; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>by sending it by post to the address for the holder in the register of

members, debenture holders or option holders.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

A notice or report sent by post is taken to be given 3 days after it is posted.

<dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>The notice may be sent:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>if the notice is to be sent to the holder in an external Territory or

outside Australia&#151;by pre-paid airmail post or by courier; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>if the notice is to be sent to the holder in Australia&#151;by pre-paid

ordinary post or by courier.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

This subsection does not limit the manner in which the document may be sent to the holder.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Section 109X makes general provision for service of

documents.

 </dl></dl>

663C  Right of holders of convertible securities to be bought out

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>Within 1 month after notice under section 663B is given in relation to

convertible securities, the holder of the convertible securities may give the

bidder a notice requiring the bidder to acquire the securities.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>The holder's notice gives rise to a contract between the holder and the bidder for the sale of the securities on: </dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the terms agreed to by the bidder and the holder; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the terms determined by the Court on application by the holder.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>If the Court makes a determination under paragraph (2)(b) in relation to

the terms of sale for a holder's securities of a particular class, the

determination applies to all holders of securities in that class who have

applications to the Court pending for a determination under that paragraph in

relation to the terms of sale of their securities.

</dd> </dl>

Part 6A.2&#151;General compulsory acquisitions and buy-outs
 Division 1&#151;Compulsory acquisition of securities by 90% holder
 664A  Threshold for general compulsory acquisition power

_90% holderholder of 90% of securities in particular class_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>A person is a 90% holder in relation to a class of securities of a company

if the person holds, either alone or with a related body corporate, full

beneficial interests in at least 90% of the securities (by number) in that

class.

</dd> </dl>

_90% holderholder with 90% voting power and 90% of whole company or scheme_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>A person is also a 90% holder in relation to a class of securities of a

company if:

</dd> </dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the securities in the class are shares or convertible into shares; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the person's voting power in the company is at least 90%; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the person holds, either alone or with a related body corporate, full

beneficial interests in at least 90% by value of all the securities of the

company that are either shares or convertible into shares.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Subsection 667A(2) provides that the expert's report that

accompanies the compulsory acquisition notice must support the paragraph (c)

condition.

 </dl></dl>

_90% holder may acquire remainder of securities in class_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>Under this section, a 90% holder in relation to a class of securities of a

company may compulsorily acquire all the securities in that class in which

neither the person nor any related bodies corporate has full beneficial

interests if either:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the holders of securities in that class (if any) who have objected to the

acquisition between them hold less than 10% by value of those remaining

securities at the end of the objection period set out in the notice under

paragraph 664C(1)(b); or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the Court approves the acquisition under section 664F.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

If subsection (2) applies to the 90% holder, the holder may compulsorily acquire securities in a class only if the holder gives compulsory acquisition notices in relation to all classes of shares and securities convertible into shares of which they do not already have full beneficial ownership.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Subsection 92(3) defines _securities_ for the

purposes of this Chapter.

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>This section has effect despite anything in the constitution of the

company whose securities are to be acquired.</dd> <dt>(5)</dt><dd>This Part does not apply to shares that give the shareholder, as a shareholder, a right to occupy or use real property that the company owns or holds under lease, whether the right is a lease or licence or a contractual right.</dd> <dt>(6)</dt><dd>The 90% holder's power to compulsorily acquire securities under a notice given under section 664C ends if the 90% holder contravenes section 664D by offering benefits outside the terms proposed in the compulsory acquisition notice under section 664C. </dd> </dl>

664AA  Time limit on exercising compulsory acquisition power

<dl compact="">

		The 90% holder in relation to a class of securities of a company may

compulsorily acquire securities in that class under section 664A only if the

holder lodges the compulsory acquisition notice for the acquisition with ASIC

under paragraph 664C(2)(a) within whichever of the following periods ends last:

 </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the period of 12 months after the commencement of this section; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the period of 6 months after the 90% holder becomes the 90% holder in

relation to that class.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

664B  The terms for compulsory acquisition

<dl compact="">

		The 90% holder may acquire the securities in the class for a cash sum only

and must pay the same amount for each security in the class acquired.

 </dl>

664C  Compulsory acquisition notice

_Compulsory acquisition notice_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>To compulsorily acquire securities under section 664A, the 90% holder must

prepare a notice in the prescribed form that:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>sets out the cash sum for which the 90% holder proposes to acquire the

securities; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>specifies a period of at least 1 month during which the holders may return

the objection forms; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>informs the holders about the compulsory acquisition procedure under this

Part, including:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>their right to obtain the names and addresses of the other holders of

securities in that class from the company register; and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>their right to object to the acquisition by returning the objection form

that accompanies the notice within the period specified in the notice; and

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>gives details of the consideration given for any securities in that class

that the 90% holder or an associate has purchased within the last 12 months;

and</dd>

<dt>(e)</dt><dd>discloses any other information that is:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>known to the 90% holder or any related bodies corporate; and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>material to deciding whether to object to the acquisition; and</dd>

<dt>(iii)</dt><dd>not disclosed in an expert's report under section 667A.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>The 90% holder must then:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>lodge the notice with ASIC; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>give each other person (other than a related body corporate) who is a

holder of securities in the class on the day on which the notice is lodged with

ASIC:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>the notice; and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>a copy of the expert's report, or of all experts' reports, under section

667A; and</dd>

<dt>(iii)</dt><dd>an objection form; and

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>give the company copies of those documents; and</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>give copies of those documents to the relevant securities exchange if the

company is listed.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Everyone who holds the securities on the day on which the

notice is lodged with ASIC is entitled to notice. Under subsection 664E(1),

anyone who acquires the securities during the objection period may object to

the acquisition.

 </dl></dl>

_Time for dispatching notice to holders_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>The 90% holder must dispatch the notices under paragraph (2)(b) on the day

the 90% holder lodges the notice with ASIC or on the next business day.

</dd> </dl>

_Manner of giving notice to holders_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>The 90% holder may give the notice to a holder:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>personally; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>by sending it by post to the address for the holder in the register of

members, debenture holders or option holders.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

A notice sent by post is taken to be given 3 days after it is posted.

<dl compact="">

<dt>(5)</dt><dd>The notice may be sent:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>if the notice is to be sent to the holder in an external territory or

outside Australia&#151;by pre-paid airmail post or by courier; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>if the notice is to be sent to the holder in Australia&#151;by pre-paid

ordinary post or by courier.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

This subsection does not limit the manner in which the document may be sent to the holder.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Section 109X makes general provision for service of

documents.

 </dl></dl>

_Notice not to be withdrawn_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(6)</dt><dd>The 90% holder may not:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>withdraw a notice under this section; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>if the 90% holder has given a notice under this section in relation to

those securities and the objection period for that notice has not ended&#151;give

another notice under this section in relation to securities.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

664D  Benefits outside compulsory acquisition procedure

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>If the 90% holder gives a notice under section 664C to compulsorily

acquire securities, the 90% holder or an associate must not offer, give or

agree to give a benefit to a person during the objection period if:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the benefit is likely to induce the person, or an associate of the person,

to:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>dispose of securities in that class; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>not object to the acquisition of those securities under the notice; and

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the benefit is not provided for in the notice.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>If the 90% holder proposes to give a notice under section 664C to acquire

securities within the next 4 months, the 90% holder or an associate must not

offer, give or agree to give a benefit to a person if:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the benefit is likely to induce the person, or an associate of the person,

to:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>dispose of securities in that class; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>not object to the acquisition of those securities under the notice; and

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the benefit is not proposed to be provided for in the notice.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>If the 90% holder gives a notice under section 664C to compulsorily

acquire securities, the 90% holder or an associate must not give a benefit to a

person:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>within 1 month after the end of the objection period (see subsection

664F(2)); or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>during any proceedings by the Court to determine an application under

subsection 664F(1) by the 90% holder;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

if:

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the benefit is likely to induce the person, or an associate of the person,

to:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>not object, or pursue an objection, to the acquisition of those securities

under the notice; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>dispose of securities in that class; and

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>the benefit is not offered to all holders of securities in that class

under the notice.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>This section does not prohibit simultaneous notices under section 664C to

compulsorily acquire different classes of securities in the company.

</dd> </dl>

664E  Holder's right to object to the acquisition

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>A person who holds securities covered by the compulsory acquisition notice

may object to the acquisition of the securities by signing an objection form

and returning it to the 90% holder. The objection:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>relates to all securities that are covered by the notice and are held by

the person at the end of the objection period; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>cannot be withdrawn.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>The 90% holder must lodge with ASIC a copy of any objection form returned

under subsection (1) as soon as practicable after it is returned.</dd> <dt>(3)</dt><dd>As soon as practicable after the end of the objection period, the 90% holder must: </dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>prepare a list that sets out:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>the names of people who hold securities covered by the compulsory

acquisition notice and have objected to the acquisition; and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>details of the securities they hold; and

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>lodge the list with ASIC; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>give a copy of the list to the company; and</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>if the company is listed&#151;give a copy to the relevant securities exchange.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>If people who hold at least 10% of the securities covered by the

compulsory acquisition notice object to the acquisition before the end of the

objection period, the 90% holder must give everyone to whom the compulsory

acquisition notice was sent under section 664C:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>a notice that the proposed acquisition will not occur; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>a notice that the 90% holder has applied to the Court for approval of the

acquisition under section 664F;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

within 1 month after the end of the objection period.

664F  The Court's power to approve acquisition

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>If people who hold at least 10% of the securities covered by the

compulsory acquisition notice object to the acquisition before the end of the

objection period, the 90% holder may apply to the Court for approval of the

acquisition of the securities covered by the notice.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>The 90% holder must apply within 1 month after the end of the objection period.</dd> <dt>(3)</dt><dd>If the 90% holder establishes that the terms set out in the compulsory acquisition notice give a fair value for the securities, the Court must approve the acquisition of the securities on those terms. Otherwise it must confirm that the acquisition will not take place. </dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	See section 667C on valuation.

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>The 90% holder must bear the costs that a person incurs on legal

proceedings in relation to the application unless the Court is satisfied that

the person acted improperly, vexatiously or otherwise unreasonably. The 90%

holder must bear their own costs.

</dd> </dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

664G  Signpost&#151;completing the acquisition of the securities

<dl compact="">

		See section 666A for how to complete the acquisition.

 </dl>

Division 2&#151;Compulsory buy-out of convertible securities by 100% holder
 665A  100% holder must offer to buy out holders of convertible securities

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>A person is a 100% holder of securities in a class if the person, either

alone or with a related body corporate, holds full beneficial interests in all

the securities in the class.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>A 100% holder in relation to a class of securities (the _main class_) who becomes a 100% holder through compulsory acquisitions under this Part must offer to buy out the holders of securities in another class that are convertible into main class securities in accordance with sections 665B and 665C. This subsection does not apply to securities if a notice is given in relation to the securities under section 661B, 662B or 664C. </dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	For when securities are convertible into main class

securities, see the definition of _convertible securities_ in

section 9.

 </dl></dl>

665B  100% holder to tell holders of convertible securities of their right to be bought out

_Notice to holders of convertible securities_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>The 100% holder must:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>prepare a notice in the prescribed form that:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>states that the person giving the notice has acquired all the securities

in the main class; and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>sets out the information that was included in the compulsory acquisition

notice given in relation to securities in the main class under paragraphs

664C(1)(d) and (e); and</dd>

<dt>(iii)</dt><dd>sets out the cash sum for which they are willing to acquire the

convertible securities; and</dd>

<dt>(iv)</dt><dd>informs the holder of convertible securities about their right to be

bought out under this Part; and

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>lodge the notice with ASIC; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>give each other person who is a holder of convertible securities on the

day on which the notice is lodged with ASIC:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>the notice; and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>a copy of the expert's report, or all experts' reports, under section

667A; and

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>give a copy of the documents to the company that issued the securities;

and</dd>

<dt>(e)</dt><dd>give a copy of the documents to each relevant securities exchange on the

same day as it is lodged with ASIC if the company is listed.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note 1:	Subparagraph (a)(iv)&#151;Section 667A deals with the

contents of an expert's report. Note 2:	The notice is to be given to everyone who holds convertible securities on the day on which the notice is lodged with ASIC. Under section 665C, anyone who holds the securities after that day may require the 100% holder to acquire the securities.  </dl></dl>

_Time for dispatching notice to holders_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>The 100% holder must dispatch the notices and reports under paragraph

(1)(c):

</dd> </dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>within 1 month after they become the 100% holder; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>on the day the 100% holder lodges the notice with ASIC or on the next

business day.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

The notices cannot be withdrawn.

_Manner of giving notice to holders_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>The 100% holder may give the notice or report to a holder:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>personally; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>by sending it by post to the address for the holder in the register of

members, debenture holders or option holders.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

A notice or report sent by post is taken to be given 3 days after it is posted.

<dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>The notice may be sent:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>if the notice is to be sent to the holder in an external Territory or

outside Australia&#151;by pre-paid airmail post or by courier; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>if the notice is to be sent to the holder in Australia&#151;by pre-paid

ordinary post or by courier.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

This subsection does not limit the manner in which the document may be sent to the holder.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Section 109X makes general provision for service of

documents.

 </dl></dl>

665C  Right of holders of convertible securities to be bought out

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>Within 1 month after notice under section 665B is given in relation to

convertible securities, the holder of the convertible securities may give the

100% holder a notice requiring the 100% holder to acquire the securities.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>The notice by the holder of convertible securities gives rise to a contract between the holder and the 100% holder for the sale of the securities on: </dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>terms agreed to by the 100% holder and the holder of the convertible

securities; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the terms determined by the Court on application by the holder of the

convertible securities.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>If the Court makes a determination under paragraph (2)(b) in relation to

the terms of sale for a holder's convertible securities of a particular class,

the determination applies to all holders of convertible securities in that

class who have applications to the Court pending for a determination under that

paragraph in relation to the terms of sale of their convertible securities.

</dd> </dl>

Division 3&#151;Notice that person has become 85% holder of a class of securities
 665D  Notice by 85% holder to company

_85% holderholder of 85% of securities in particular class_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>A person is an 85% holder in relation to a class of securities of a

company if the person holds, either alone or with a related body corporate,

full beneficial interests in at least 85% of the securities (by number) in that

class.

</dd> </dl>

_85% holderholder with 85% voting power and 85% of whole company_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>A person is also an 85% holder in relation to a class of securities of a

company if:

</dd> </dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the securities in the class are shares or convertible into shares; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the person's voting power in the company is at least 85%; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the person holds, either alone or with a related body corporate, full

beneficial interests in at least 85% by value of all the securities of the

company that are either shares or convertible into shares.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

_Person becoming 85% holder to give notice to company_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>A person who becomes an 85% holder in relation to a class of securities of

a company must notify the company in writing that they have become an 85%

holder in relation to that class. The person must give the notice within 14

days after the person becomes aware of the information.

</dd> </dl>

_Person continuing to be 85% holder to give notice to company_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>A person who:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>gives a company a notice under subsection (3) in relation to a class of

securities; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>is an 85% holder in relation to the class on any anniversary of becoming

an 85% holder in relation to the class;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

must notify the company in writing that they continue to be an 85% holder in relation to the class. The person must give the notice within 14 days after the anniversary.

665E  Notice by company to other members

_Company to notify members_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>A company that is given a notice by a person under section 665D in

relation to a class of securities must notify its members in writing that:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the person:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>has become an 85% holder in relation to the class; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>continues to be an 85% holder in relation to the class; and

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the person will be able to acquire the securities in that class under this

Part if the person becomes a 90% holder in relation to that class.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

_Time for notifying members_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>The company must notify its members before, or at the same time as,

whichever of the following it first gives to its members after the company is

given the notice under section 665D:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>a notice under another provision of this Law</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>a report under a provision of this Law.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

_Information about 85% holder to be prominent if included in other material given to members_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>If a company notifies its members under this section by including the

information referred to in paragraphs (1)(a) and (b) in:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>a notice given to members under another provision of this Law; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>a report given to members under a provision of this Law;</dd>

	the information must appear prominently in the notice or report.

</dl></dl></dl>

Part 6A.3&#151;Completion of compulsory acquisition of securities
 666A  Completing the acquisition of securities

<center>Back to Top</center>

_Completion to be by private treaty or statutory procedure_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>A person entitled to acquire securities under section 661A or 664A must

either:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>pay, issue or transfer the consideration to the holder, take a transfer of

the securities from the holder and have the company that issued the securities

register the transfer; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>complete the procedure laid down in section 666B;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

by the end of the period referred to in subsection (2) or (3).

_Time for completing compulsory acquisition following takeover_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>For an acquisition under section 661A, the period ends 14 days after the

later of:
