</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the end of 1 month after the compulsory acquisition notice was lodged with

ASIC under section 661B; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the end of 14 days after the last statement under section 661D was given

if a request is made under that section; or</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>if an application to stop the acquisition is made to the Court under

section 661E&#151;the application is finally determined.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

_Time for completing compulsory acquisition under Part 6A.2_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>For an acquisition under section 664A or 664F, the period ends 14 days

after the later of:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the end of the objection period; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>if an application for approval of the acquisition is made to the Court

under section 664F in relation to the securities&#151;the application is finally

determined.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

666B  Statutory procedure for completion

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>Under this section, the person acquiring the securities must:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>give the company that issued the securities a copy of the compulsory

acquisition notice under section 661B or 664C together with a transfer of the

securities:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>signed as transferor by someone appointed by the person acquiring the

securities; and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>signed as transferee by the person acquiring the securities; and

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>pay, issue or transfer the consideration for the transfer to the company

that issued the securities.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

The person appointed under subparagraph (a)(i) has authority to sign the transfer on behalf of the holder of the securities.

<dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>If the person acquiring the securities complies with subsection (1), the

company that issued the securities must:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>register the person as the holder of the securities; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>hold the consideration received under subsection (1) in trust for the

person who held the securities immediately before registration; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>give written notice to the person referred to in paragraph (b) as soon as

practicable that the consideration has been received and is being held by the

company pending their instructions as to how it is to be dealt with.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>If the consideration held under subsection (2) consists of, or includes,

money, that money must be paid into a bank account opened and maintained for

that purpose only.

</dd> </dl>

Part 6A.4&#151;Experts' reports and valuations
 667A  Expert's report

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>An expert's report under section 663B, 664C or 665B must:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>be prepared by a person nominated by ASIC under section 667AA; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>state whether, in the expert's opinion, the terms proposed in the notice

give a fair value for the securities concerned; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>set out the reasons for forming that opinion.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	See section 667C on valuation.

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>If the person giving the compulsory acquisition notice is relying on

paragraph 664A(2)(c) to give the notice, the expert's report under section 664C

must also:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>state whether, in the expert's opinion, the person (either alone or

together with a related body corporate) has full beneficial ownership in at

least 90% by value of all the securities of the company that are shares or

convertible into shares; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>set out the reasons for forming that opinion.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>If the person giving the compulsory acquisition notice obtains 2 or more

reports, each of which were obtained for the purposes of that notice, a copy of

each report must be given to the holder of the securities.

</dd> </dl>

667AA  Expert to be nominated

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>A person who proposes to obtain an expert's report for the purposes of

section 663B, 664C or 665B must request ASIC in writing to nominate a person to

prepare the expert's report.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>Within 14 days after receiving a request under subsection (1), ASIC must nominate:</dd> <dt>(a)</dt><dd>an appropriate person to prepare the report; or</dd> <dt>(b)</dt><dd>up to 5 appropriate persons, one of whom the person making the request may choose to prepare the report.</dd> <dt>(3)</dt><dd>In determining whether a person is an appropriate person to prepare an expert's report, and without limiting the matters that ASIC may consider, ASIC must consider the nature of the company to be valued. </dd> </dl>

667B  Expert must not be an associate and must disclose prior dealings and relationships

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>The expert who provides the report must not be an associate of:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the person giving the notice; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the company that issued the securities.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>The report must set out details of:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>any relationship between the expert and:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>the person giving the notice or an associate of the person giving the

notice; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>the company that issued the securities or an associate of the company;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		including any circumstances in which the expert gives them advice, or acts on

their behalf, in the proper performance of the functions attaching to the

expert's professional capacity or business relationship with them; and

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>any financial or other interest of the expert that could reasonably be

regarded as being capable of affecting the expert's ability to give an unbiased

opinion in relation to the matter being reported on; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>any fee, payment or other benefit (whether direct or indirect) that the

expert has received or will or may receive in connection with the report.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

667C  Valuation of securities

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>To determine what is fair value for securities for the purposes of this

Chapter:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>first, assess the value of the company as a whole; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>then allocate that value among the classes of issued securities in the

company (taking into account the relative financial risk, and voting and

distribution rights, of the classes); and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>then allocate the value of each class pro rata among the securities in

that class (without allowing a premium or applying a discount for particular

securities in that class).

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>Without limiting subsection (1), in determining what is fair value for

securities for the purposes of this Chapter, the consideration (if any) paid

for securities in that class within the previous 6 months must be taken into

account.

</dd> </dl>

Part 6A.5&#151;Records of unclaimed consideration

668A  Company's power to deal with unclaimed consideration for compulsory acquisition

_Records of unclaimed compulsory acquisition consideration_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>If a company is paid consideration in respect of securities that are

compulsorily acquired under Part 6A.1 or 6A.3, the company must maintain

records of:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the consideration paid (including any benefit accruing from the

consideration and any property substituted for the whole or any part of that

consideration); and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the people who are entitled to that consideration; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>any transfers of the consideration to the people entitled to it.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>The company must keep the records at:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>its registered office; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>its principal place of business in Australia; or</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>another place in Australia approved by ASIC.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>A person may ask the company to let the person inspect all or any of the

records kept by the company under this section. The company must let the person

inspect the records:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>if the company requires payment of an amount not exceeding the prescribed

amount&#151;within 7 days after the day on which the company receives that amount;

or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>in any other case&#151;within 7 days after the day on which the request is

made.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>By the end of February each year, the company must publish in the

_Gazette_ a copy of the records kept under subsection (1) as at the end of

the previous December.

</dd> </dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

668B  Unclaimed consideration to be transferred to ASIC

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>If the company has not transferred the unclaimed consideration to the

person entitled to it within 12 months after the publication of a copy of the

records in the _Gazette_, the company must transfer the consideration to

ASIC within 1 month after the end of that 12 month period.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>The company is then discharged from liability to any person in respect of the consideration.</dd> <dt>(3)</dt><dd>ASIC must deal with the consideration under Part 9.7.</dd> <dt>(4)</dt><dd>Except as provided by subsection (2), this Part does not deprive a person of any right or remedy to which the person is entitled against a liquidator or company. </dd> </dl>

Part 6A.6&#151;ASIC powers

669  ASIC's power to exempt and modify

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>ASIC may:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>exempt a person from a provision of this Chapter; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>declare that this Chapter applies to a person as if specified provisions

were omitted, modified or varied as specified in the declaration.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>The exemption or declaration may:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>apply to all or specified provisions of this Chapter; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>apply to all persons, specified persons, or a specified class of persons;

and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>relate to all securities, specified securities or a specified class of

securities; and</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>relate to any other matter generally or as specified.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>An exemption may apply unconditionally or subject to specified conditions.

A person to whom a condition specified in an exemption applies must comply with

the condition. The Court may order the person to comply with the condition  in a specified way. Only ASIC may apply to the Court for the

order.</dd> <dt>(4)</dt><dd>The exemption or declaration must be in writing and ASIC must publish notice of it in the _Gazette_.</dd> <dt>(5)</dt><dd>For the purposes of this section, the _provisions of this Chapter_ include: </dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>regulations made for the purposes of this Chapter; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>definitions in this Law or the regulations as they apply to references in:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>this Chapter; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>regulations made for the purposes of this Chapter; and

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>Division 12 of Part 11.2.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

Chapter 6B&#151;Rights and liabilities in relation to Chapter 6 and 6A matters

670A  Misstatements in, or omissions from, takeover and compulsory acquisition and buy-out documents

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>A person must not give:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>a bidder's statement</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>a takeover offer document</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>a notice of variation of a takeover offer</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>a target's statement</dd>

<dt>(e)</dt><dd>a compulsory acquisition notice under section 661B or 664C</dd>

<dt>(f)</dt><dd>a compulsory buy-out notice under section 662B, 663B or 665B</dd>

<dt>(g)</dt><dd>a report that is included in, or accompanies, a statement or notice

referred to in paragraphs (a) to (f)

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<center>Back to Top</center>

if there is:

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(h)</dt><dd>for all documents&#151;a misleading or deceptive statement in the document;

or</dd>

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>for a bidder's statement or target's statement&#151;an omission from the

document of material required by section 636 or 638; or</dd>

<dt>(j)</dt><dd>for a bidder's statement or a target's statement&#151;a new circumstance that:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>has arisen since the document was lodged; and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>would have been required by section 636 or 638 to be included in the

document if it had arisen before the document was lodged; or

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(k)</dt><dd>for an expert's report under subsection 636(2) or section 640, 663B, 664C

or 665B&#151;an omission from the report of material required by subsection 648A(3)

or 667B(2).

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note 1:	See section 670D for defences. Note 2:	Section 995 imposes liabilities in respect of other conduct related to the dealings in securities.  </dl></dl>

_Forecasts and other forward-looking statement_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>A person is taken to make a misleading statement about a future matter

(including the doing of, or refusing to do, an act) if they do not have

reasonable grounds for making the statement. This subsection does not limit the

meaning of a reference to a misleading statement or a statement that is

misleading in a material particular.

</dd> </dl>

_Offence if statement, omission or new matter materially adverse_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>A person commits an offence if they contravene subsection (1) and:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the misleading or deceptive statement; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the omission or new circumstance;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

is materially adverse from the point of view of the holder of securities to whom the document is given.

670B  Right to recover for loss or damage resulting from contravention

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>A person who suffers loss or damage that results from a contravention of

subsection 670A(1) may recover the amount of the loss or damage from a person

referred to in the following table if the loss or damage is one that the table

makes the person liable for. This is so even if the person did not commit, and

was not involved in, the contravention.

</dd> </dl>

<table><tr align="left">
  <th colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>People liable on the document</div>

  </th>
  <th colspan="1" align="right">
    <div>\[operative table]</div>

  </th>
</tr>
<tr align="left">
  <th colspan="1" align="left">

  </th>
  <th colspan="1" align="left">
    <div><i>For these documents</i> 
these people...</div>

  </th>
  <th colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>
...are liable for loss or damages caused by</div>

  </th>
</tr>
<tr align="left">
  <td colspan="1" align="left">

  </td>
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div><i>bidder's statement or takeover offer document</i></div>

  </td>
</tr>
<tr align="left">
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>1</div>

  </td>
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>the bidder</div>

  </td>
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>any contravention of subsection 670A(1) in relation to the document</div>

  </td>
</tr>
<tr align="left">
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>2</div>

  </td>
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>each director of a bidder that is a body if the consideration offered under the bid is not a cash sum only</div>

  </td>
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>any contravention of subsection 670A(1) in relation to the document</div>

  </td>
</tr>
<tr align="left">
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>3</div>

  </td>
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>a director of a bidder that is a body unless the director proves that they:</div>
    <div>(a) were not present when the directors resolved to adopt the statement or offer document; or 
(b) voted against the resolution;</div>
    <div>if the consideration offered under the bid is a cash sum only</div>

  </td>
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>any contravention of subsection 670A(1) in relation to the document 
See also items 10 and 11.</div>

  </td>
</tr>
<tr align="left">
  <td colspan="1" align="left">

  </td>
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div><i>notice of variation of a takeover offer</i></div>

  </td>
</tr>

    <div>the bidder</div>

    <div>any contravention of subsection 670A(1) in relation to the document

  <td colspan="1" align="left">

    <div>(a) were not present when the directors resolved to give the notice; or

    <div><i>all documents</i></div>

  <td colspan="1" align="left">

  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>a person named in the document, with their consent, as having made a statement:</div>
    <div>(a) that is included in the document; or 
(b) on which a statement made in the document is based</div>

  </td>
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>the inclusion of the statement in the document</div>

  </td>
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>that contravention</div>

  </td>
</tr></table><dl compact="">

	(2)	An action under subsection (1) may begin at any time within 6 years after

<center>Back to Top</center>

the day on which the cause of action arose. 	(3)	This Part does not affect any liability that a person has under any other law. 

</dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Conduct that contravenes subsection 670A(1) is expressly

excluded from the operation of section 995.

 </dl></dl>

670C  People liable on takeover or compulsory acquisition statement to inform maker about deficiencies in the statement 

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>A person referred to in the table in subsection 670B(1) in relation to a

document must notify the issuer of the document in writing as soon as

practicable if they become aware during the bid period or objection period that:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>a material statement in the document is misleading or deceptive; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>there is a material omission from the document of information required by

section 636, 638 or 640; or</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>a material new circumstance that:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>has arisen since the document was lodged; and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>would have been required by section 636, 638 or 640 to be included in the

document if it had arisen before the document was lodged.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>An expert whose report accompanies, or is included in, a target's

statement under section 640 must notify the target in writing as soon as

practicable if they become aware during the takeover period that:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>a material statement in the report is misleading or deceptive; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>there has been a significant change affecting information included in the

report.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>An expert whose report accompanies, or is included in, a bidder's

statement under subsection 636(2) must notify the bidder in writing as soon as

practicable if they become aware during the takeover period that:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>a material statement in the report is misleading or deceptive; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>there has been a significant change affecting information included in the

report.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

670D  Defences against prosecutions under subsection 670A(3) and actions under section 670B

_Not knowing statement misleading or deceptive_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>A person does not commit an offence against subsection 670A(3), and is not

liable under section 670B for a contravention of subsection 670A(1), because of

a misleading or deceptive statement in a document if the person proves that

they did not know that the statement was misleading or deceptive.

</dd> </dl>

_Not knowing there was an omission_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>A person does not commit an offence against subsection 670A(3), and is not

liable under section 670B for a contravention of subsection 670A(1), because of

an omission from a document in relation to a particular matter if the person

proves that they did not know that there was an omission from the document in

relation to that matter.

</dd> </dl>

_Reasonable reliance on information given by someone elsestatements and omissions_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>A person does not commit an offence against subsection 670A(3), and is not

liable under section 670B for a contravention against subsection 670A(1),

because of a misleading or deceptive statement in, or an omission from, a

document if the person proves that they placed reasonable reliance on

<center>Back to Top</center>

information given to them by:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>if the person is a body&#151;someone other than a director, employee or agent

of the body; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>if the person is an individual&#151;someone other than an employee or agent of

the individual.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>For the purposes of subsection (3), a person is not the agent of a body or

individual merely because they perform a particular professional or advisory

function for the body or individual.

</dd> </dl>

_Withdrawal of consentstatements and omissions_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(5)</dt><dd>A person who is named in a document as:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>making a statement included in the document; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>making a statement on the basis of which a statement is included in the

document;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

does not commit an offence against subsection 670A(3), and is not liable under section 670B for a contravention against subsection 670A(1), because of a misleading or deceptive statement in, or an omission from, a document if the person proves that they publicly withdrew their consent to being named in the document in that way.

_Unawareness of new matter_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(6)</dt><dd>A person does not commit an offence against subsection 670A(3), and is not

liable under section 670B for a contravention of subsection 670A(1), because of

a new circumstance that has arisen since the document was lodged if the person

proves that they were not aware of the matter.

</dd> </dl>

670E  Liability for proposing a bid or not carrying through with bid

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>A person who:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>enters into a transaction relating to securities in reliance on:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>a public proposal for a takeover bid; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>an announcement of a market bid; and

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>suffers loss or damage that results from a contravention of section 631:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

may recover the amount of the loss or damage from:

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the person who contravened the section; or</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>any person involved in the contravention.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>To determine the amount of compensation payable under subsection (1),

deduct the price of the securities at which the transaction was entered into

from the price of the securities at which the transaction would have been

likely to be entered into if the proposal or announcement had not been made.

</dd> </dl>

670F  Defences

<dl compact="">

		A person does not commit an offence under subsection 631(1) or (2), and is

not liable under section 670E for a contravention of those subsections if the

person proves that they could not reasonably have been expected to comply with

those subsections because:

 </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>at the time of the proposal or announcement, circumstances existed that

the person did not know of and could not reasonably have been expected to know

of; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>after the proposal or announcement, a change in circumstances occurred

that was not caused, directly or indirectly, by the person.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

Chapter 6C&#151;Information about ownership of listed companies and managed investment schemes

671A  Chapter extends to some listed bodies that are not companies

<dl compact="">

		This Chapter applies to the acquisition of relevant interests in the

securities of listed bodies that are not companies but are incorporated or

formed in this jurisdiction in the same way as it applies to the acquisition of

relevant interests in the securities of companies.

 </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Section 9 defines _company_,

_jurisdiction_ and _listed_.

 </dl></dl>

Part 6C.1&#151;Substantial holding information

671B  Information about substantial holdings must be given to company, responsible entity and relevant securities exchange

_Requirement to give information_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>A person must give the information referred to in subsection (3) to a

listed company, or the responsible entity for a listed registered managed

investment scheme, if:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the person begins to have, or ceases to have, a substantial holding in the

company or scheme; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the person has a substantial holding in the company or scheme and there is

a movement of at least 1% in their holding; or</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the person makes a takeover bid for securities of the company or scheme.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

The person must also give the information to each relevant securities exchange.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note 1:	Section 9 defines _substantial holding_ and _associate_. Note 2:	The information must be given even if the situation changes by the time the information is to be given.  </dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>For the purposes of this section, there is a _movement of at least 1%_ in a person's holding if the percentage worked out using the following

formula increases or decreases by 1 or more percentage points from the

percentage they last disclosed under this Part in relation to the company or

scheme:

</dd> </dl>

<sub> ![A graphic exists here.](http://www.comlaw.gov.au/Details/C2004C01070/Html/AA356F7CD35B5DE2CA256F7100539BBD/$FILE/1205.gif)![A graphic exists here.](http://www.comlaw.gov.au/Details/C2004C01070/Html/AA356F7CD35B5DE2CA256F7100539BBD/$FILE/1206.gif)</sub>

where:

<def><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

_person&apos;s and associates&apos; votes_ is the total number of votes

attached to all the voting shares in the company or interests in the scheme (if

any) that the person or an associate has a relevant interest in. _total votes in company or scheme_ is the total number of votes attached to all voting shares in the company or interests in the scheme.  </dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Subsection (7) expands the normal concept of relevant

interest to take account of exchange traded options and conditional agreements.

 </dl></dl>

_Information that must be given_

<dl compact="">

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>The information to be given is:

</dd> 

</dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the person's name and address; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>details of their relevant interest in:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>voting shares in the company; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>interests in the scheme; and

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>details of any relevant agreement through which they would have a relevant

interest in:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>voting shares in the company; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>interests in the scheme; and

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>the name of each associate who has a relevant interest in voting shares in

the company or interests in the scheme, together with details of:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>the nature of their association with the associate; and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>the relevant interest of the associate; and</dd>

<dt>(iii)</dt><dd>any relevant agreement through which the associate has the relevant

interest; and

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(e)</dt><dd>if the information is being given because of a movement in their

holding&#151;the size and date of that movement; and</dd>

<dt>(f)</dt><dd>if the information is being given because a person has ceased to be an

associate&#151;the name of the person; and</dd>

<dt>(g)</dt><dd>any other particulars that are prescribed.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Subsection (7) expands the normal concept of relevant

interest to take account of exchange traded options and conditional agreements.

 </dl></dl>

_Information to be in prescribed form and accompanied by certain documents_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>The information must be given in the prescribed form and must be

accompanied by:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>a copy of any document setting out the terms of any relevant agreement

that:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>contributed to the situation giving rise to the person needing to provide

the information; and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>is in writing and readily available to the person; and

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>a statement by the person giving full and accurate details of any

contract, scheme or arrangement that:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>contributed to the situation giving rise to the person needing to provide

the information; and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>is not both in writing and readily available to the person.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

If the person is required to give a copy of a contract, scheme or arrangement, the copy must be endorsed with a statement that the copy is a true copy.

<dl compact="">

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dt>(5)</dt><dd>The information does not need to be accompanied by the documents referred

to in subsection (4) if the transaction that gives rise to the person needing

to provide the information takes place on a stock exchange approved under

section 769.

</dd> 

</dl>

_Deadline for giving information_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(6)</dt><dd>The person must give the information:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>within 2 business days after they become aware of the information; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>by 9.30 am on the next trading day of the relevant securities exchange

after they become aware of the information if:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>a takeover bid is made for voting shares in the company or voting

interests in the scheme; and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>the person becomes aware of the information during the bid period.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

_Relevant interestsexchange traded options and conditional agreements_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(7)</dt><dd>For the purposes of this section, a person has a relevant interest in

securities if the person would have a relevant interest in the securities but

for subsection 609(6) (exchange traded options) or 609(7) (conditional

agreements).

</dd> </dl>

671C  Civil liability

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>A person who contravenes section 671B is liable to compensate a person for

any loss or damage the person suffers because of the contravention.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>It is a defence in proceedings brought under this section if the person who contravenes section 671B proves that they contravened that section: </dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>because of inadvertence or mistake; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>because they were not aware of a relevant fact or occurrence.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

In determining whether the defence is available, disregard the person's ignorance of, or a mistake on the person's part concerning, a matter of law.

<dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>If 2 or more persons each contravene section 671B because of the same act

or omission, their liability under this section for the contravention is joint

and individual.

</dd> </dl>

Part 6C.2&#151;Tracing beneficial ownership of shares

672A  Disclosure notices

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>ASIC, a listed company or the responsible entity for a listed managed

investment scheme, may direct:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>a member of the company or scheme; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>a person named in a previous disclosure under section 672B as having a

relevant interest in, or having given instructions about, voting shares in the

company or interests in the scheme;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

to make the disclosure required by section 672B.

<dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>ASIC must exercise its powers under this section if requested to do so by

a member of the company or scheme unless it considers that it would be

unreasonable to do so in all the circumstances.

</dd> </dl>

672B  Disclosure by member of relevant interests and instructions

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>A person given a direction under section 672A must disclose to the person

giving the direction:

<center>Back to Top</center>

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>full details of their own relevant interest in the shares or interests in

the scheme and of the circumstances that give rise to that interest; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the name and address of each other person who has a relevant interest in

any of the shares or interests together with full details of:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>the nature and extent of the interest; and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>the circumstances that give rise to the other person's interest; and

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the name and address of each person who has given the person instructions

about:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>the acquisition or disposal of the shares or interests; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>the exercise of any voting or other rights attached to the shares or

interests; or</dd>

<dt>(iii)</dt><dd>any other matter relating to the shares or interests;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		together with full details of those instructions (including the date or dates

on which they were given).

</dl></dl></dl>

A matter referred to in paragraph (b) or (c) need only be disclosed to the extent to which it is known to the person required to make the disclosure.

<dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>The disclosure must be made within 2 business days after:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the person is given the direction; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>if the person applies for an exemption under section 673 from the

obligation to make the disclosure and ASIC refuses to grant the exemption&#151;ASIC

notifies the person of its decision on the application; or</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>if the direction is given by a company or responsible entity&#151;the company

or responsible entity pays any fee payable under the regulations made for the

purposes of section 672D.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>The person does not have to comply with a direction given by the company

or the responsible entity if the person proves that the giving of the direction

is vexatious.

</dd> </dl>

672C  ASIC may pass information on to person who made request

<dl compact="">

		If ASIC receives information in response to a direction under section 672A

about shares in a company or interests in a listed managed investment scheme,

ASIC:

 </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>may pass the information on to the company or the responsible entity for

the scheme; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>if ASIC gave the direction in response to a request under subsection

672A(2)&#151;must pass the information on to the person who made the request unless

ASIC considers it would be unreasonable in all the circumstances to do so.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

672D  Fee for complying with a direction given by a company or scheme under this Part

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>The regulations may prescribe fees that companies and responsible entities

are to pay to persons for complying with directions given under this Part.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>A person is liable to repay a fee paid to the person for complying with a direction under section 672A if the person does not comply with the direction on time even if the person does so later. The fee may be recovered as a debt due to the company or responsible entity that paid it to the person. </dd> </dl>

672E  No notice of rights

<dl compact="">

<center>Back to Top</center>

		A company or responsible entity is not, because of anything done under this

Part:

</dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>to be taken for any purpose to have notice of; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>put on inquiry as to;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

a person's right in relation to a share in the company or an interest in the listed managed investment scheme.

672F  Civil liability

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>A person who contravenes section 672B is liable to compensate a person for

any loss or damage the person suffers because of the contravention.</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>It is a defence in proceedings brought under this section if the person who contravenes section 672B proves that they contravened that section: </dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>because of inadvertence or mistake; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>because they were not aware of a relevant fact or occurrence.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

In determining whether the defence is available, disregard the person's ignorance of, or a mistake on the person's part concerning, a matter of law.

<dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>If 2 or more persons each contravene section 672B because of the same act

or omission, their liability under this section for the contravention is joint

and individual.

</dd> </dl>

Part 6C.3&#151;ASIC powers

673  ASIC's power to exempt and modify

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>ASIC may:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>exempt a person from a provision of this Chapter; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>declare that this Chapter applies to a person as if specified provisions

were omitted, modified or varied as specified in the declaration.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>In deciding whether to give the exemption or declaration, ASIC must

consider the purposes of this Chapter set out in section 602.</dd> <dt>(3)</dt><dd>The exemption or declaration may: </dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>apply to all or specified provisions of this Chapter; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>apply to all persons, specified persons, or a specified class of persons;

and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>relate to all securities, specified securities or a specified class of

securities; and</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>relate to any other matter generally or as specified.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>An exemption may apply unconditionally or subject to specified conditions.

A person to whom a condition specified in an exemption applies must comply with

the condition. The Court may order the person to comply with the condition in a

specified way _._ Only ASIC may apply to the Court for the order.</dd> <dt>(5)</dt><dd>The exemption or declaration must be in writing and ASIC must publish notice of it in the _Gazette_.</dd> <dt>(6)</dt><dd>For the purposes of this section, the _provisions of this Chapter_ include: </dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>regulations made for the purposes of this Chapter; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>definitions in this Law or the regulations as they apply to references in:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>this Chapter; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>regulations made for the purposes of this Chapter; and

<center>Back to Top</center>

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>Division 12 of Part 11.2.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

Chapter 6D&#151;Fundraising
 Part 6D.1&#151;Application of the fundraising provisions

700  Coverage of the fundraising rules

_Securities covered_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>Subsection 92(3) defines _securities_ for the purposes of this

Chapter.

</dd> </dl>

_Offers and invitations both covered_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>For the purposes of this Chapter:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>offering securities for issue includes inviting applications for the issue

of the securities; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>offering securities for sale includes inviting offers to purchase the

securities.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

_Person offering securities_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>For the purposes of this Chapter, the person who offers securities is the

person who has the capacity, or who agrees, to issue or transfer the securities

if the offer is accepted.

</dd> </dl>

_Geographical coverage of Chapter_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>This Chapter applies to offers of securities that are received in this

jurisdiction, regardless of where any resulting issue, sale or transfer occurs.

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	This Chapter in effect applies to all offers received

anywhere in Australia because the Corporations Law operates as a national law.

 </dl></dl>

701  Treatment of offers of interests in managed investment scheme

<dl compact="">

		This Chapter applies to offers of interests in managed investment schemes as

if:

 </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>making the interests available were issuing the interests; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the person making the interests available were the body whose securities

were issued; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the assets and liabilities, financial position and performance, profits

and losses and prospects of the scheme were those of the body; and</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>a person who has the capacity to determine the outcome of decisions about

the financial and operating policies governing the operation of the scheme were

able to control the body.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

702  Treatment of offers of options over securities

<dl compact="">

		For the purposes of this Chapter:

 </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>an offer of an option over securities is not to be taken to be an offer of

the underlying securities; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the grant of an option without an offer of the option is taken to be an

offer of the option; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>an offer to grant an option is taken to be an offer to issue the security

constituted by the option.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<center>Back to Top</center>

Note 1:	If a disclosure document is needed for the option and

there is no further offer involved in exercising the option, the issue or sale

of the underlying securities on the exercise of the option does not need a

disclosure document. Note 2:	Paragraph (b)&#151;the grant of the option will not require a disclosure document if no consideration is payable on the grant or the exercise of the option (see subsections 708(15) and (16)).  

</dl></dl>

703  Chapter may not be contracted out of

<dl compact="">

		A condition of a contract for the sale or issue of securities is void if it

provides that a party to the contract is:

 </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>required or bound to waive compliance with any requirement of this

Chapter; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>taken to have notice of any contract, document or matter not specifically

referred to in the disclosure document for the offer.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

Part 6D.2&#151;Disclosure to investors about securities
 Division 1&#151;Overview
 704  When disclosure to investors is needed

<dl compact="">

		Sections 706, 707 and 708 say when an offer of securities needs disclosure to

investors under this Part.

 </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note 1:	Section 727 prohibits offering securities without

disclosure. Note 2:	If the offer needs disclosure, section 734 applies advertising restrictions. These continue throughout the whole offer process. Different restrictions apply before and after the disclosure document is lodged. Note 3:	The way the offers are made to people must not breach the securities hawking prohibition in section 736\.  </dl></dl>

705  Types of disclosure document

<dl compact="">

		The following table shows what disclosure documents to use if an offer of

securities needs disclosure to investors under this Part.

 </dl>

<table><tr align="left">
  <th colspan="1" align="left">

  </th>
  <th colspan="1" align="left">

  </th>

  </td>
