defences \[732, 733]</div>

  </td>
</tr></table>Division 2&#151;Offers that need disclosure to investors
 706  Issue offers that need disclosure

<dl compact="">

		An offer of securities for issue needs disclosure to investors under this

Part unless section 708 says otherwise.

 </dl>

707  Sale offers that need disclosure

_Only some sales need disclosure_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>An offer of securities for sale needs disclosure to investors under this

Part only if disclosure is required by subsection (2), (3) or (5).

</dd> </dl>

_Off-market sale by controller_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>An offer of a body's securities for sale needs disclosure to investors

under this Part if:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the person making the offer controls the body; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>either:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>the securities are not quoted; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>although the securities are quoted, they are not offered for sale in the

ordinary course of trading on a stock market of a securities exchange;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

and section 708 does not say otherwise.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	See section 50AA for when a person controls a body.

 </dl></dl>

_Sale amounting to indirect issue_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>An offer of a body's securities for sale within 12 months after their

<center>Back to Top</center>

issue needs disclosure to investors under this Part if the body issued the

securities:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>without disclosure to investors under this Part; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>with the purpose of the person to whom they were issued:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>selling or transferring them; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>granting, issuing or transferring interests in, or options or warrants

over, them;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

and section 708 does not say otherwise.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note 1:	Section 706 normally requires disclosure for the issue of

securities. This subsection is intended to prevent avoidance of section 706.

However, to establish a contravention of this subsection, the only purpose that

needs to be shown is that referred to in paragraph (b). Note 2:	The issuer and the seller must both consent to the disclosure document (see section 720).  </dl></dl>

_Evidence of intentionindirect issue_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>Unless the contrary is proved, a body is taken to issue securities with

the purpose referred to in paragraph (3)(b) if any of the securities are

subsequently sold, or offered for sale, within 12 months after their issue.

</dd> </dl>

_Sale amounting to indirect off-market sale by controller_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(5)</dt><dd>An offer of a body's securities for sale within 12 months after their sale

by a person who controlled the body at the time of the sale needs disclosure to

investors under this Part if:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>at the time of the sale by the controller either:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>the securities were not quoted; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>although the securities were quoted, they were not offered for sale in

the ordinary course of trading on a stock market of a securities exchange; and

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the controller sold the securities without disclosure to investors under

this Part; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the controller sold the securities with the purpose of the person to whom

they were sold:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>selling or transferring them; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>granting, issuing or transferring interests in, or options or warrants

over, them;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

and section 708 does not say otherwise.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note 1:	Subsection (2) normally requires disclosure for a sale by

a controller. This subsection is intended to prevent avoidance of subsection

(2). However, to establish a contravention of this subsection, the only purpose

that needs to be shown is that referred to in paragraph (c). Note 2:	See section 50AA for when a person controls a body. Note 3:	The controller and the seller must both consent to the disclosure document (see section 720).  </dl></dl>

_Evidence of intentionindirect sale by controller_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(6)</dt><dd>Unless the contrary is proved, a person who controls a body is taken to

sell securities with the purpose referred to in paragraph (5)(c) if any of the

securities are subsequently sold, or offered for sale, within 12 months after

their sale by the controller.

</dd> 
<center>Back to Top</center>

</dl>

708  Offers that do not need disclosure

_Small scale offerings (20 issues or sales in 12 months)_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>Personal offers of a body's securities by a person do not need disclosure

to investors under this Part if:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>none of the offers results in a breach of the 20 investors ceiling (see

subsections (3) and (4)); and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>none of the offers results in a breach of the $2 million ceiling (see

subsections (3) and (4)).

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

This subsection does not apply to an offer for sale to which subsection 707(3) (sale amounting to indirect issue) or (5) (sale amounting to indirect sale by controller) applies.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note 1:	Subsection 727(4) makes it an offence to issue or

transfer securities without disclosure to investors once 20 issues or transfers

have occurred or $2 million has been raised. Note 2:	Under section 740 ASIC may make a determination aggregating the transactions of bodies that ASIC considers to be closely related.  </dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>For the purposes of subsection (1), a personal offer is one that:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>may only be accepted by the person to whom it is made; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>is made to a person who is likely to be interested in the offer, having

regard to:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>previous contact between the person making the offer and that person; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>some professional or other connection between the person making the offer

and that person; or</dd>

<dt>(iii)</dt><dd>statements or actions by that person that indicate that they are

interested in offers of that kind.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>An offer by a body to issue securities:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>results in a breach of the 20 investors ceiling if it results in the

number of people to whom securities of the body have been issued exceeding 20

in any 12 month period; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>results in a breach of the $2 million ceiling if it results in the amount

raised by the body by issuing securities exceeding $2 million in any 12 month

period.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>An offer by a person to transfer a body's securities:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>results in a breach of the 20 investors ceiling if it results in the

number of people to whom the person sells securities of the body exceeding 20

in any 12 month period; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>results in a breach of the $2 million ceiling if it results in the amount

raised by the person from selling the body's securities exceeding $2 million in

any 12 month period.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(5)</dt><dd>In counting issues and sales of the body's securities, and the amount

raised from issues and sales, for the purposes of subsection (1), disregard

issues and sales that result from offers that:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>do not need a disclosure document because of any other subsection of this

section; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>are not received in Australia; or</dd>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>are made under a disclosure document.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Also see provisions on restrictions on advertising (section

734) and securities hawking provisions (Part 6D.3).

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(6)</dt><dd>In counting issues and sales of the body's securities, and the amount

raised from issues and sales, for the purposes of subsection (1), disregard any

issues and sales made by a body if:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the body was a managed investment scheme (but not a registered managed

investment scheme) at the time that the offer of interests in the scheme that

resulted in the issues or sales was made; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the body became a registered managed investment scheme within 12 months

after that offer was made; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the offer would have been exempted under any other subsection of this

section if the managed investment scheme had been a registered managed

investment scheme at the time that the offer was made.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(7)</dt><dd>In working out the amount of money raised by the body by issuing

securities, include the following:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the amount payable for the securities at the time when they are issued</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>if the securities are shares issued partly-paid&#151;any amount payable at a

future time if a call is made</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>if the security is an option&#151;any amount payable on the exercise of the

option</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>if the securities carry a right to convert the securities into other

securities&#151;any amount payable on the exercise of that right.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

_Sophisticated investors_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(8)</dt><dd>An offer of a body's securities does not need disclosure to investors

under this Part if:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the minimum amount payable for the securities on acceptance of the offer

by the person to whom the offer is made is at least $500,000; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the amount payable for the securities on acceptance by the person to whom

the offer is made and the amounts previously paid by the person for the body's

securities of the same class that are held by the person add up to at least

$500,000; or</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>it appears from a certificate given by a qualified accountant no more than

6 months before the offer is made that the person to whom the offer is made:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>has net assets of at least $2.5 million; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>has a gross income for each of the last 2 financial years of at least

$250,000 a year.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note 1:	Section 9 defines _qualified accountant_. Note 2:	Paragraph (c)&#151;A dealer has obligations under Division 3 of Part 7.4 when making recommendations about securities and ASIC has power under section 826 to revoke a dealer's licence if the dealer contravenes paragraph 708(8)(c).  </dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(9)</dt><dd>In calculating the amount payable, or paid, for securities for the

purposes of paragraph (8)(a) or (b), disregard any amount payable, or paid, to

the extent to which it is to be paid, or was paid, out of money lent by the

person offering the securities or an associate.</dd> <dt>(10)</dt><dd>An offer of a body's securities does not need disclosure to investors under this Part if: </dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the offer is made through a licensed dealer; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the dealer is satisfied on reasonable grounds that the person to whom the

offer is made has previous experience in investing in securities that allows

them to assess:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>the merits of the offer; and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>the value of the securities; and</dd>

<dt>(iii)</dt><dd>the risks involved in accepting the offer; and</dd>

<dt>(iv)</dt><dd>their own information needs; and</dd>

<dt>(v)</dt><dd>the adequacy of the information given by the person making the offer; and

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the dealer gives the person before, or at the time when, the offer is made

a written statement of the dealer's reasons for being satisfied as to those

matters; and</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>the person to whom the offer is made signs a written acknowledgment

before, or at the time when, the offer is made that the dealer has not given

the person a disclosure document under this Part in relation to the offer.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

_Professional investors_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(11)</dt><dd>An offer of securities does not need disclosure to investors under this

Part if it is made to:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>a person who is a licensed or exempt dealer and is acting as principal; or

</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>a person who is a licensed or exempt investment adviser and is acting as

principal; or </dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>a body registered under the _Life Insurance Act 1995_; or</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>a body registered under the _Financial Corporations Act 1974_; or</dd>

<dt>(e)</dt><dd>a regulated superannuation fund, an approved deposit fund, a pooled

superannuation trust, or a public sector superannuation scheme within the

meaning of the _Superannuation Industry (Supervision) Act 1993_ if the

fund, trust or scheme has net assets of at least $10 million; or</dd>

<dt>(f)</dt><dd>a terminating building society within the meaning of the _Financial Corporations Act 1974_; or</dd>

<dt>(g)</dt><dd>a friendly society within the meaning of the _Life Insurance Act 1995_; or</dd>

<dt>(h)</dt><dd>a person who controls at least $10 million (including any amount held by

an associate or under a trust that the person manages) for the purpose of

investment in securities.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note 1:	Section 68 defines _exempt dealer_ and

_exempt investment adviser_. Note 2:	An underwriter to a securities issue or sale will generally be a licensed dealer.  </dl></dl>

_Offers of securities to people associated with the body_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(12)</dt><dd>An offer of a body's securities does not need disclosure to investors

under this Part if it is made to:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>an executive officer of the body or a related body or their spouse,

parent, child, brother or sister; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>a body corporate controlled by a person referred to in paragraph (a).

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

_Certain offers to present holder of securities_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(13)</dt><dd>An offer of securities for issue does not need disclosure to investors

under this Part if it is:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>an offer of fully-paid shares in a company to 1 or more existing holders

of shares in the company under a dividend reinvestment plan or bonus share

plan; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>an offer of interests in a managed investment scheme to 1 or more existing

holders of interests in the scheme if:

<center>Back to Top</center>

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>the offer is made under a distribution reinvestment plan or switching

facility; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>the scheme is of a kind commonly known as a cash common fund or cash

management trust.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(14)</dt><dd>An offer of a disclosing entity's debentures for issue does not need

disclosure to investors under this Part if the offer is made to 1 or more

existing debenture holders.

</dd> </dl>

_Issues or sales for no consideration_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(15)</dt><dd>An offer of securities (other than options) does not need disclosure to

investors under this Part if no consideration is to be provided for the issue

or transfer of the securities.</dd> <dt>(16)</dt><dd>An offer of options does not need disclosure to investors under this Part if: </dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>no consideration is to be provided for the issue or transfer of the

options; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>no consideration is to be provided for the underlying securities on the

exercise of the option.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

_Compromise or arrangement under Part 5.1_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(17)</dt><dd>An offer of securities does not need disclosure to investors under this

Part if it is made under a compromise or arrangement under Part 5.1 approved at

a meeting held as a result of an order under subsection 411(1) or (1A).

</dd> </dl>

_Takeovers_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(18)</dt><dd>An offer of securities does not need disclosure to investors under this

Part if it is:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>made as consideration for an offer to acquire securities under a takeover

bid under Chapter 6; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>accompanied by a bidder's statement.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Although this offer does not need a disclosure document,

similar disclosures must be made about the securities in the bidder's statement

under section 636.

 </dl></dl>

_Debentures of certain bodies_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(19)</dt><dd>An offer of a body's debentures for issue or sale does not need

disclosure to investors under this Part if the body is:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>an Australian ADI; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>registered under the _Life Insurance Act 1995._

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

_Offers by exempt bodies_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(20)</dt><dd>An offer of a body's securities does not need disclosure to investors

under this Part if the body is an exempt body of this jurisdiction.

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Section 66A defines _exempt body__._

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(21)</dt><dd>An offer of a body's securities for issue does not need disclosure to

investors under this Part if the body is an exempt public authority of a State

<center>Back to Top</center>

or Territory.

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Debentures, stock or bonds issued by a government are not

securities for the purposes of this Chapter (see subsection 92(3)).

 </dl></dl>

Division 3&#151;Types of disclosure documents
 709  Prospectuses, short-form prospectuses, profile statements and offer information statements

_Prospectus or short-form prospectus_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>If an offer of securities needs disclosure to investors under this Part, a

prospectus must be prepared for the offer unless subsection (4) allows an offer

information statement to be used instead. Under section 712, the prospectus may

simply refer to material already lodged with ASIC instead of including it.

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	See sections 710 to 713 for the contents of a prospectus.

 </dl></dl>

_Profile statement_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>A profile statement for an offer may be prepared in addition to the

prospectus if ASIC has approved the making of offers of that kind with a

profile statement instead of a disclosure document.

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note 1:	See section 714 for the contents of a profile

statement. Note 2:	Subsection 729(2) provides that there is still liability to investors on the prospectus when a profile statement is used.  </dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>ASIC may approve the use of profile statements for offers of securities of

a particular kind. The approval may specify information to be included in the

profile statement (including information about a matter referred to in

paragraphs 714(1)(a) to (d)).

</dd> </dl>

_Offer information statement_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>A body offering to issue securities may use an offer information statement

for the offer instead of a prospectus if the amount of money to be raised by

the body by issuing the securities, when added to all amounts previously raised

by:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the body; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>a related body corporate; or</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>an entity controlled by:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>a person who controls the body; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>an associate of that person;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

by issuing securities under an offer information statement is $5 million or less.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note 1:	See section 715 for the contents of an offer information

statement. The statement must include financial statements that are less that 6

months old. Note 2:	Under section 740, ASIC may make a determination aggregating the transactions of bodies that ASIC considers to be closely related.  </dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(5)</dt><dd>In working out the amount of money to be raised by a body or entity by

issuing securities, include the following:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the amount payable for the securities at the time when they are issued</dd>

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>if the securities are issued partly-paid&#151;any amount payable at a future

time if a call is made</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>if the securities are options&#151;any amount payable on the exercise of the

options</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>if the securities carry a right to convert the securities into other

securities&#151;any amount payable on the exercise of that right.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

Division 4&#151;Disclosure requirements
 710  Prospectus content&#151;general disclosure test

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>A prospectus for a body's securities must contain all the information that

investors and their professional advisers would reasonably require to make an

informed assessment of the matters set out in the table below. The prospectus

must contain this information:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>only to the extent to which it is reasonable for investors and their

professional advisers to expect to find the information in the prospectus;

and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>only if a person whose knowledge is relevant (see subsection (3)):

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>actually knows the information; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>in the circumstances ought reasonably to have obtained the information by

making enquiries.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<table><tr align="left">
  <th colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>Disclosures</div>

  </th>
  <th colspan="1" align="right">
    <div>\[operative]</div>

  </th>
</tr>
<tr align="left">
  <th colspan="1" align="left">

  </th>
  <th colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>Offer</div>

  </th>
  <th colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>Matters</div>

  </th>
</tr>
<tr align="left">
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>1</div>

  </td>
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>offer to issue (or transfer) shares, debentures or interests in a managed investment scheme</div>

  </td>
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>* the rights and liabilities attaching to the securities offered</div>
    <div>* the assets and liabilities, financial position and performance, profits and losses and prospects of the body that is to issue (or issued) the shares, debentures or interests</div>

  </td>
</tr>
<tr align="left">
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>2</div>

  </td>
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>offer to grant (or transfer) a legal or equitable interest in securities or grant (or transfer) an option over securities</div>

  </td>
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>* the rights and liabilities attaching to:</div>
    <div>- the interest or option 
- the underlying securities</div>
    <div>* for an option&#151;the capacity of the person making the offer to issue or deliver the underlying securities</div>
    <div>* if the person making the offer is:</div>
    <div>- the body that issued or is to issue the underlying securities; or 
- a person who controls that body;</div>
    <div>the assets and liabilities, financial position and performance, profits and losses and prospects of that body</div>
    <div>* if subsection 707(3) or (5) applies to the offer&#151;the assets and liabilities, financial position and performance, profits and losses and prospects of the body whose securities are offered</div>

  </td>
</tr></table><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Section 713 makes special provision for prospectuses for

<center>Back to Top</center>

continuously quoted securities.

</dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>In deciding what information should be included under subsection (1), have

regard to:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the nature of the securities and of the body; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>if the securities are investments in a managed investment scheme&#151;the

nature of the scheme; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the matters that likely investors may reasonably be expected to know;

and</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>the fact that certain matters may reasonably be expected to be known to

their professional advisers.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>For the purposes of this section, a person's knowledge is relevant only if

they are one of the following:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the person offering the securities</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>if the person offering the securities is a body&#151;a director of the body</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>a proposed director of the body whose securities will be issued under the

offer</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>a person named in the prospectus as an underwriter of the issue or sale</dd>

<dt>(e)</dt><dd>a person named in the prospectus as a stockbroker to the issue or sale if

they participate in any way in the preparation of the prospectus</dd>

<dt>(f)</dt><dd>a person named in the prospectus with their consent as having made a

statement:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>that is included in the prospectus; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>on which a statement made in the prospectus is based

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(g)</dt><dd>a person named in the prospectus with their consent as having performed a

particular professional or advisory function.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Section 729 says who is liable for misstatements in, and

omissions from, a disclosure document.

 </dl></dl>

711  Prospectus content&#151;specific disclosures

_Terms and conditions of offer_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>The prospectus must set out the terms and conditions of the offer.

</dd> </dl>

_Disclosure of interests and fees of certain people involved in the offer_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>The prospectus must set out the nature and extent of the interests (if

any) that each person referred to in subsection (4) holds, or held at any time

during the last 2 years, in:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the formation or promotion of the body; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>property acquired or proposed to be acquired by the body in connection

with:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>its formation or promotion; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>the offer of the securities; or

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the offer of the securities.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>The prospectus must set out the amount that anyone has paid or agreed to

pay, or the nature and value of any benefit anyone has given or agreed to give:

</dd> 

</dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>to a director, or proposed director, to induce them to become, or to

qualify as, a director of the body; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>for services provided by a person referred to in subsection (4) in

connection with:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>the formation or promotion of the body; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>the offer of the securities; and

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>if the prospectus is for interests in a managed investment scheme&#151;to the

responsible entity:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>to procure acquisitions of interests in the scheme; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>for services provided under the constitution of the scheme.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

To comply with this subsection it is not sufficient merely to state in the prospectus that a person has been paid or will be paid normal, usual or standard fees.

<dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>Disclosures need to be made under subsections (2) and (3) in relation to:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>any directors and proposed directors of the body</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>a person named in the prospectus as performing a function in a

professional, advisory or other capacity in connection with the preparation or

distribution of the prospectus</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>if the securities are interests in a managed investment scheme&#151;the person

making the interests available and, if the person is a body, its directors</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>a promoter of the body</dd>

<dt>(e)</dt><dd>a stockbroker or underwriter (but not a sub-underwriter) to the issue or

sale.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

_Quotation of securities_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(5)</dt><dd>If the prospectus for an offer of securities states or implies that the

securities are to be quoted on a stock market of a securities exchange (whether

in Australia or elsewhere), the prospectus must state that:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the securities have been admitted to quotation on that stock market; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>an application for admission of the securities to quotation on that stock

market has been made to that securities exchange; or</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>an application for admission of the securities to quotation on that stock

market will be made to that securities exchange within 7 days after the date of

the prospectus.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note 1:	Paragraph 724(1)(b) gives times within which the person

should seek and obtain admission to quotation. Note 2:	Subsection 716(1) requires the prospectus to be dated.  </dl></dl>

_Expiry date_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(6)</dt><dd>The prospectus must state that no securities will be issued on the basis

of the prospectus after the expiry date specified in the prospectus. The expiry

date must not be later than 13 months after the date of the prospectus. The

expiry date of a replacement prospectus must be the same as that of the

original prospectus it replaces.

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note 1:	Subsection 716(1) requires the prospectus to be dated. Note 2:	Section 719 deals with replacement prospectuses.  
<center>Back to Top</center>

</dl></dl>

_Lodgment with ASIC_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(7)</dt><dd>The prospectus must state that:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>a copy of the prospectus has been lodged with ASIC; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>ASIC takes no responsibility for the content of the prospectus.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

_Prescribed information_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(8)</dt><dd>The prospectus must set out the information required by the regulations.

</dd> </dl>

712  Prospectus content&#151;short form prospectuses

_Prospectus may simply refer to material lodged with ASIC_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>Instead of setting out information that is contained in a document that

has been lodged with ASIC, a prospectus may simply refer to the document. The

reference must:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>identify the document or the part of the document that contains the

information; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>inform people of their right to obtain a copy of the document (or part)

under subsection (5).

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>The reference must also include:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>if the information is primarily of interest to professional analysts or

advisers or investors with similar specialist information needs:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>a description of the contents of the document (or part); and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>a statement to the effect that the information in the document (or part)

is primarily of interest to those people; or

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>in any other case&#151;sufficient information about the contents of the

document to allow a person to whom the offer is made to decide whether to

obtain a copy of the document (or part).

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>The document (or part) referred to under subsection (1) is taken to be

included in the prospectus.</dd> <dt>(4)</dt><dd>A person who wishes to take advantage of subsection (1) may lodge a document with ASIC even if this Law does not require the document to be lodged.</dd> <dt>(5)</dt><dd>If the prospectus is taken to include a document, or part of a document, under subsection (1), the person making the offer must give a copy of the document (or part) free of charge to anyone who asks for it during the application period of the prospectus. </dd> </dl>

713  Special prospectus content rules for continuously quoted securities

_Alternative general disclosure test_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>A prospectus for an offer of:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>continuously quoted securities of a body; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>options to acquire continuously quoted securities of a body;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

satisfies section 710 if it complies with subsections (2), (3) and (4) of this section.

<dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>The prospectus must contain all the information investors and their

<center>Back to Top</center>

professional advisers would reasonably require to make an informed assessment

of:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the effect of the offer on the body; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>if the securities are interests in a managed investment scheme&#151;the effect

of the offer on the scheme; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the rights and liabilities attaching to the securities offered; and</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>if the securities are options&#151;the rights and liabilities attaching to:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>the options themselves; and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>the underlying securities.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

The prospectus must contain this information only to the extent to which it is reasonable for investors and their professional advisers to expect to find the information in the prospectus.

<dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>The prospectus must state that:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>as a disclosing entity, the body or scheme is subject to regular reporting

and disclosure obligations; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>copies of documents lodged with ASIC in relation to the body may be

obtained from, or inspected at, an ASIC office.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>The prospectus must either:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>inform people of their right to obtain a copy of any of the following

documents:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>the annual financial report most recently lodged with ASIC by the body or

scheme</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>any half-year financial report lodged with ASIC by the body or scheme

after the lodgment of that annual financial report and before the lodgment of

the copy of the prospectus with ASIC</dd>

<dt>(iii)</dt><dd>any continuous disclosure notices given by the body or scheme after the

lodgment of that annual financial report and before the lodgment of the copy of

the prospectus with ASIC; or

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>include, or be accompanied by, a copy of the document.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

If the prospectus informs people of their right to obtain a copy of the document, the person making the offer must give a copy of the document free of charge to anyone who asks for it during the application period for the prospectus.

_Information excluded from continuous disclosure notice_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(5)</dt><dd>Information about the offer must also be set out in the prospectus if the

information:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>has been excluded from a continuous disclosure notice in accordance with

the listing rules of the securities exchange to which the notice was given;

and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>is information that investors and their professional advisers would

reasonably require for the purpose of making an informed assessment of:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>the assets and liabilities, financial position and performance, profits

and losses and prospects of the body; and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>the rights and liabilities attaching to the securities being offered.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

The prospectus must contain this information only to the extent to which it is reasonable for investors and their professional advisers to expect to find the information in the prospectus.

_ASIC power to exclude entity from this section_

<dl compact="">

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dt>(6)</dt><dd>ASIC may determine in writing that a body or scheme may not rely on this

section if it is satisfied that, in the previous 12 months, any of the

following provisions were contravened in relation to the body or scheme:

</dd> 

</dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the provisions of Chapter 2M</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>section 1001A</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>section 724</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>section 728.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

ASIC must publish a copy of the determination in the _Gazette_. While the determination is in force, section 710 and not this section applies to securities of the body or scheme.

714  Contents of profile statement

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>A profile statement must:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>identify the body and the nature of the securities; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>state the nature of the risks involved in investing in the securities;

and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>give details of all amounts payable in respect of the securities

(including any amounts by way of fee, commission or charge); and</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>state that the person given the profile statement is entitled to a copy of

the prospectus free of charge; and</dd>

<dt>(e)</dt><dd>state that:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>a copy of the statement has been lodged with ASIC; and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>ASIC takes no responsibility for the content of the statement; and

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(f)</dt><dd>give any other information required by the regulations or by ASIC approval

under subsection 709(3).

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>The profile statement must state that no securities will be issued on the

basis of the statement after the expiry date specified in the statement. The

expiry date must not be later than 13 months after the date of the prospectus.

The expiry date of a replacement statement must be the same as that of the

original statement it replaces.

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note 1:	Subsection 716(1) requires the profile statement to be

dated. Note 2:	Section 719 deals with supplementary and replacement profile statements.  </dl></dl>

715  Contents of offer information statement 

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>An offer information statement for the issue of a body's securities must:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>identify the body and the nature of the securities; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>describe the body's business; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>describe what the funds raised by the offers are to be used for; and</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>state the nature of the risks involved in investing in the securities;

and</dd>

<dt>(e)</dt><dd>give details of all amounts payable in respect of the securities

(including any amounts by way of fee, commission or charge); and</dd>

<dt>(f)</dt><dd>state that:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>a copy of the statement has been lodged with ASIC; and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>ASIC takes no responsibility for the content of the statement; and

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(g)</dt><dd>state that the statement is not a prospectus and that it has a lower level

of disclosure requirements than a prospectus; and</dd>

<dt>(h)</dt><dd>state that investors should obtain professional investment advice before

<center>Back to Top</center>

accepting the offer; and

</dd>

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>include a copy of a financial report for the body; and</dd>

<dt>(j)</dt><dd>include any other information that the regulations require to be included

in the statement.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>The financial report included under paragraph (1)(i) must:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>be a report for a 12 month period and have a balance date that occurs

within the last 6 months before the securities are first offered under the

statement; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>be prepared in accordance with the accounting standards; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>be audited.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>The statement must state that no securities will be issued on the basis of

the statement after the expiry date specified in the statement. The expiry date

must not be later than 13 months after the date of the statement. The expiry

date of a replacement statement must be the same as that of the original

statement it replaces.

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note 1:	Subsection 716(1) requires the statement to be dated. Note 2:	Section 719 deals with replacement statements.  </dl></dl>

716  Disclosure document date and consents

_Date of disclosure document_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>A disclosure document must be dated. The date is the date on which it is

lodged with ASIC.

</dd> </dl>

_Consent of person to whom statement attributed_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>A disclosure document may only include a statement by a person, or a

statement said in the document to be based on a statement by a person, if:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the person has consented to the statement being included in the document

in the form and context in which it is included; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the document states that the person has given this consent; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the person has not withdrawn this consent before the document is lodged

with ASIC.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

Division 5&#151;Procedure for offering securities
 717  Overview of procedure for offering securities

<dl compact="">

		The following table summarises what a person who wants to offer securities

must do to make an offer of securities that needs disclosure to investors under

this Part and gives signposts to relevant sections:

 </dl>

<table><tr align="left">
  <th colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>Offering securities (disclosure documents and procedure)</div>

* does not contain any misleading or deceptive statements 
* is dated</div>

  </td>

    <div>* the investor used an application form distributed with the disclosure document; and

    <div>* securities are issued in response to an improper application form; or 
* the disclosure document is not current or is materially deficient.</div>
    <div>Sections 731, 732 and 733 provide defences for the contraventions. 
Section 737 provides remedies for an investor.</div>

  </td>
</tr></table>718  Lodging of disclosure document

<dl compact="">

		A disclosure document to be used for an offer of securities must be lodged

with ASIC.

 </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note 1:	Subsection 727(3) makes it an offence to process

applications for non-quoted securities under an offer that needs a disclosure

document until 7 days after the disclosure document is lodged. Note 2:	See section 720 for the consents that need to be obtained before lodgment. Note 3:	Section 351 says what signatures are necessary for documents that are to be lodged with ASIC.  </dl></dl>

719  Lodging supplementary or replacement document

_Need for a supplementary or replacement document_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>If the person making the offer becomes aware of:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>a misleading or deceptive statement in the disclosure document; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>an omission from the disclosure document of information required by

section 710, 711, 712, 713, 714 or 715; or</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>a new circumstance that:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>has arisen since the disclosure document was lodged; and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>would have been required by section 710, 711, 712, 713, 714 or 715 to be

included in the disclosure document if it had arisen before the disclosure

document was lodged;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

that is materially adverse from the point of view of an investor, the person may lodge a supplementary or replacement document with ASIC.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note 1:	Section 728 makes it an offence to continue making offers

after the person has become aware of a misleading or deceptive statement,

omission or new circumstance that is materially adverse from the point of view

of an investor unless the deficiency is corrected. Note 2:	Because of section 712, a prospectus may be taken to include information in another document. This should be taken into account when 
<center>Back to Top</center>
 considering whether the prospectus is deficient. Note 3:	The power to issue a supplementary or replacement document is not limited to the situations dealt with in this section. Note 4:	This section applies to a document that has already been previously supplemented or replaced. Note 5:	See section 720 for the consents that need to be obtained before lodgment.  

</dl></dl>

_Form of supplementary document_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>At the beginning of a supplementary document, there must be:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>a statement that it is a supplementary document; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>an identification of the disclosure document it supplements; and</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>an identification of any previous supplementary documents lodged with ASIC

in relation to the offer; and</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>a statement that it is to be read together with the disclosure document it

supplements and any previous supplementary documents.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

The supplementary document must be dated. The date is the date on which it is lodged with ASIC.

_Form of replacement document_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>At the beginning of a replacement document, there must be:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>a statement that it is a replacement document; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>an identification of the disclosure document it replaces.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

The replacement document must be dated. The date is the date on which it is lodged with ASIC.

_Consequences of lodging a supplementary document_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>If a supplementary document is lodged with ASIC, the disclosure document

is taken to be the disclosure document together with the supplementary document

for the purposes of the application of this Chapter to events that occur after

the lodgment.

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	This subsection means, for example, that offers made after

lodgment of the supplementary document must be accompanied by copies of both

the original disclosure document and the supplementary document.

 </dl></dl>

_Consequences of lodging a replacement document_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(5)</dt><dd>If a replacement document is lodged with ASIC, the disclosure document is

taken to be the replacement document for the purposes of the application of

this Chapter to events that occur after the lodgment.

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	This subsection means, for example, that offers made after

lodgment of the replacement document must be accompanied by copies of the

replacement document and not the original disclosure document.

 </dl></dl>

720  Consents needed for lodgment

_Consents for issue offers_

<dl compact="">

		The lodgment of a disclosure document, or a supplementary or replacement

document, for the offer of a body's securities requires the consent of:

 </dl>

<table><tr align="left">
  <th colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>Consents required for lodgment</div>

  </th>
  <th colspan="1" align="right">
    <div>\[operative]</div>

  </th>

  <center>Back to Top</center>

  <th colspan="1" align="left">

  </th>

  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>

every director of the body

if securities interests in a managed investment scheme made available by a body&#151;every director of that body

    <div>

offer of securities for sale that needs a disclosure document because of subsection 707(5)</div>

  </td>
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>

if seller an individual&#151;that individual 
if seller a body&#151;every director of the body 
if individual controls the body whose securities are offered for sale&#151;that individual 
if body controls the body whose securities are offered for sale&#151;every director of the controlling body</div>

  </td>
</tr></table>721  Offer must be made in, or accompanied by, the disclosure document

_Offers using prospectus alone_

<dl compact="">

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>Offers of securities for which a prospectus is being used must be made in,

or accompanied by, the prospectus unless subsection (2) allows a profile

statement to be used instead.

</dd> 

</dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note 1:	Subsection 727(1) makes it an offence to make an offer of

securities unless the offer is made in or accompanied by the disclosure

document and subsection 723(1) makes it an offence to issue securities unless

they are applied for on a form that was issued in or together with the

disclosure document. Note 2:	Section 736 makes it an offence to make unsolicited offers in a way that amounts to securities hawking. Note 3:	Section 728 makes it an offence for a person to offer securities if the disclosure document is deficient in a way that is material from the point of view of an investor.  </dl></dl>

_Offers using prospectus and profile statement_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>An offer of securities may be made in, or accompanied by, a profile

statement if:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>under subsection 709(3), ASIC has approved the making of offers of that

kind with a profile statement instead of a prospectus; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the profile statement complies with the requirements specified in ASIC

approval.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>If the offer that is made to a person is made in or accompanied by a

profile statement, the person making the offer must give the person a copy of

the prospectus free of charge if the person asks for it.

</dd> </dl>

_Offers using offer information statement_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>Offers for which an offer information statement is being used must be made

in, or accompanied by, the offer information statement.

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note 1:	Subsection 727(1) makes it an offence to make an offer of

securities unless the offer is made in or accompanied by the disclosure

document and subsection 723(1) makes it an offence to issue securities unless

they are applied for on a form that was issued in or together with the

disclosure document. Note 2:	Section 736 makes it an offence to make unsolicited offers in a way that amounts to securities hawking. Note 3:	Section 728 makes it an offence for a person to offer securities if the disclosure document is deficient in a way that is material from the point of view of an investor.  </dl></dl>

722  Application money to be held on trust

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>If a person offers securities for issue or sale under a disclosure

document, the person must hold:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>all application money received from people applying for securities under

the disclosure document; and</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>all other money paid by them on account of the securities before they are

issued or transferred;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

in trust under this section for the applicants until:

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the securities are issued or transferred; or</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>the money is returned to the applicants.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>If the application money needs to be returned to an applicant, the person

must return the money as soon as practicable.

</dd> </dl>

723  Issuing or transferring the securities under a disclosure document

_Applications must be made on form included in, or accompanied by, disclosure document_

<dl compact="">

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>If an offer of securities needs a disclosure document, the securities may

only be issued or transferred in response to an application form. The

securities may only be issued or transferred if the person issuing or

transferring them has reasonable grounds to believe that:

</dd> 

</dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the form was included in, or accompanied by:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>the disclosure document; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>if subsection 721(2) allows a profile statement to be used&#151;the

prospectus or the profile statement;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		when the form was distributed by the person issuing or transferring the

securities; or

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the form was copied, or directly derived, by the person making the

application from a form referred to in paragraph (a).

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

_Minimum subscription condition must be fulfilled before issue or transfer_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>If a disclosure document for an offer of securities states that the

securities will not be issued or transferred unless:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>applications for a minimum number of the securities are received; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>a minimum amount is raised;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

the person making the offer must not issue or transfer any of the securities until that condition is satisfied. For the purpose of working out whether the condition has been satisfied, a person who has agreed to take securities as underwriter is taken to have applied for those securities.

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note 1:	Under section 722, the application money must be held in

trust until the issue or transfer of the securities. Note 2:	This subsection prevents the issue or transfer of the securities not only to those who apply for them in response to the disclosure document but also to those who do not need to apply for them (for example, because they are to take the securities under an underwriting agreement).  </dl></dl>

_Issue or transfer void if quotation condition not fulfilled_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>If a disclosure document for an offer of securities states or implies that

the securities are to be quoted on a stock market of a securities exchange

(whether in Australia or elsewhere) and:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>an application for the admission of the securities to quotation is not

made within 7 days after the date of the disclosure document; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the securities are not admitted to quotation within 3 months after the

date of the disclosure document;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

then:

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>an issue or transfer of securities in response to an application made

under the disclosure document is void; and</dd>

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>the person offering the securities must return the money received by the

person from the applicants as soon as practicable.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

724  Choices open to person making the offer if disclosure document condition not met or disclosure document defective

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>If a person offers securities under a disclosure document and:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the disclosure document states that the securities will not be issued or

transferred unless:

</dd>

<center>Back to Top</center>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>applications for a minimum number of the securities are received; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>a minimum amount raised;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		and that condition is not satisfied within 4 months after the date of the

disclosure document; or

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the disclosure document states or implies that the securities are to be

quoted on a stock market of a securities exchange (whether in Australia or

elsewhere) and:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>an application for the admission to quotation is not made within 7 days

after the date of the disclosure document; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>the securities are not admitted to quotation within 3 months after the

date of the disclosure document; or

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>the person becomes aware that:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>the disclosure document contains a misleading or deceptive statement; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>there is an omission from the disclosure document of information required

by section 710, 711, 712, 713, 714 or 715;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

		that is materially adverse from the point of view of an investor; or

<dt>(d)</dt><dd>the person becomes aware of a new circumstance that:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>has arisen since the disclosure document was lodged; and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>would have been required by section 710, 711, 712, 713, 714 or 715 to be

included in the disclosure document if it had arisen before the disclosure

document was lodged; and</dd>

<dt>(iii)</dt><dd>is materially adverse from the point of view of an investor;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

the person must deal under subsection (2) with any applications for the securities made under the disclosure document that have not resulted in an issue or transfer of the securities. For the purpose of working out whether a condition referred to in paragraph (a) has been satisfied, a person who has agreed to take securities as underwriter is taken to have applied for those securities.

<dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>The person must either:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>repay the money received by the person from the applicants; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>give the applicants:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>the documents required by subsection (3); and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>1 month to withdraw their application and be repaid; or

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>issue or transfer the securities to the applicants and give them:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>the documents required by subsection (3); and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>1 month to withdraw their application and be repaid.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Section 719 deals with lodging supplementary and

replacement documents. Section 728 makes it an offence for a person to offer

securities if the disclosure document is deficient in a way that is material

from the point of view of an investor.

 </dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>The documents to be given are set out in the following table:

</dd> 

</dl>

<table><tr align="left">
  <th colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>Documents to be given</div>

  </th>
  <th colspan="1" align="right">
    <div>\[operative]</div>

  </th>
</tr>
<tr align="left">
  <th colspan="1" align="left">

  </th>
  <th colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>Circumstances</div>

  </th>
  <th colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>Documents</div>

  </th>
</tr>
<tr align="left">
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>1</div>

  </td>
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>the sole disclosure document is a prospectus</div>

  </td>
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>a supplementary or replacement prospectus that corrects the deficiency or changes the terms of the offer</div>

  </td>
</tr>
<tr align="left">
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>2</div>

  </td>
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>the disclosure documents are a prospectus and a profile statement and subsection (1) applies to the prospectus</div>

  </td>
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>a statement that sets out the changes needed to the prospectus to correct the deficiency or change the terms of offer; and 
a statement that the person is entitled to a copy of the prospectus free of charge</div>

  </td>
</tr>
<tr align="left">
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>3</div>

  </td>
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>the disclosure documents are a prospectus and a profile statement and subsection (1) applies to the profile statement 
 <i>Note that item 2 and this item may both apply to the offer.</i></div>

  </td>
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>a supplementary or replacement profile statement that corrects the deficiency or changes the terms of the offer</div>

  </td>
</tr>
<tr align="left">
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>4</div>

  </td>
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>the disclosure document is an offer information statement</div>

  </td>
  <td colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>a supplementary or replacement offer information statement that corrects the deficiency or changes the terms of the offer</div>

  </td>
</tr></table>725  Expiration of disclosure document

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>If a person offers securities under a disclosure document and the

disclosure document passes its expiry date, the person must deal with

applications for the securities under the document in accordance with

subsections (2) and (3).</dd> <dt>(2)</dt><dd>If an application is received on or before the expiry date, the person may issue or transfer securities to the applicant. </dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Subsection 723(1) (when read with subsections 719(4) and

(5)) requires the person issuing or transferring the securities to have

reasonable grounds to believe that the application form was included in, or

<center>Back to Top</center>

accompanied by, a disclosure document that was current at the time.

</dl></dl>

<dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>If an application is received after the expiry date, the person must

either:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>return any money received by the person from the applicant; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>give the applicant:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>a new disclosure document; and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>1 month to withdraw their application and be repaid; or

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>issue or transfer the securities to the applicant and give them:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>a new disclosure document; and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>1 month to withdraw their application and be repaid.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

Part 6D.3&#151;Prohibitions, liabilities and remedies
 Division 1&#151;Prohibitions and liabilities
 726  Offering securities in a body that does not exist

<dl compact="">

		A person must not offer securities of:

 </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>a body that has not been formed or does not exist; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>a managed investment scheme that needs to be, or will need to be,

registered and that has not been registered;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

if the offer would need disclosure to investors under Part 6D.2 if the body or scheme did exist or had been registered. This is so even if it is proposed to form, incorporate or register the body or scheme.

727  Offering securities without a current disclosure document

_Offer of securities needs lodged disclosure document_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>A person must not make an offer of securities, or distribute an

application form for an offer of securities, that needs disclosure to investors

under Part 6D.2 unless a disclosure document for the offer has been lodged with

ASIC.

</dd> </dl>

_Offer form to be included in or accompanied by disclosure document_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>A person must not make an offer of securities, or distribute an

application form for an offer of securities, that needs disclosure to investors

under Part 6D.2 unless:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>if a prospectus is used for the offer&#151;the offer or form is:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>included in the prospectus; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>accompanied by a copy of the prospectus; or

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>if both a prospectus and a profile statement are used for the offer&#151;the

offer or form is:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>included in the prospectus or profile statement; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>accompanied by a copy of the prospectus or profile statement; or

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<center>Back to Top</center>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>if an offer information statement is used for the offer&#151;the offer or form

is:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>included in the statement; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>accompanied by a copy of the statement.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note:	Sections 706, 707 and 708 say when the offer needs

disclosure to investors under Part 6D.2.

 </dl></dl>

_Non-quoted securitieswaiting period after lodgment before processing applications for securities_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>A person must not accept an application for, or issue or transfer,

non-quoted securities offered under a disclosure document until the period of 7

days after lodgment of the disclosure document has ended. ASIC may extend the

period by notice in writing to the person offering the securities. The period

as extended must end no more than 14 days after lodgment.

</dd> </dl>

_Issue or transfer not to breach section 708 ceiling_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(4)</dt><dd>If a person relies on subsection 708(1) to make offers of securities

without disclosure to investors under Part 6D.2, the person must not issue or

transfer securities without disclosure to investors under that Part if the

issue or transfer would result in a breach of the 20 investors ceiling or the

$2 million ceiling (see subsections 708(3), (4), (5), (6) and (7)).

</dd> </dl>

728  Misstatement in, or omission from, disclosure document

_Misleading or deceptive statements, omissions and new matters_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>A person must not offer securities under a disclosure document if there is:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>a misleading or deceptive statement in:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>the disclosure document; or</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>any application form that accompanies the disclosure document; or</dd>

<dt>(iii)</dt><dd>any document that contains the offer if the offer is not in the

disclosure document or the application form; or

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>an omission from the disclosure document of material required by section

710, 711, 712, 713, 714 or 715; or</dd>

<dt>(c)</dt><dd>a new circumstance that:

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(i)</dt><dd>has arisen since the disclosure document was lodged; and</dd>

<dt>(ii)</dt><dd>would have been required by section 710, 711, 712, 713, 714 or 715 to be

included in the disclosure document if it had arisen before the disclosure

document was lodged.

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl></dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact="">

Note 1:	The person may make further offers after making up the

deficiency in the current disclosure document by lodging a supplementary or

replacement document. Note 2:	See sections 731, 732 and 733 for defences. Note 3:	Section 995 imposes liabilities in respect of other conduct related to the offering of the securities.  </dl></dl>

_Forecasts and other forward-looking statements_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(2)</dt><dd>A person is taken to make a misleading statement about a future matter

(including the doing of, or refusing to do, an act) if they do not have

reasonable grounds for making the statement. This subsection does not limit the

meaning of a reference to a misleading statement or a statement that is

misleading in a material particular.

</dd> 
<center>Back to Top</center>

</dl>

_Offence if statement, omission or new matter materially adverse_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(3)</dt><dd>A person commits an offence if they contravene subsection (1) and:

</dd> </dl>

<dl compact=""><dl compact=""><dl compact="">

<dt>(a)</dt><dd>the misleading or deceptive statement; or</dd>

<dt>(b)</dt><dd>the omission or new circumstance;

</dd>

</dl></dl></dl>

is materially adverse from the point of view of an investor.

729  Right to recover for loss or damage resulting from contravention

_Right to compensation_

<dl compact="">

<dt>(1)</dt><dd>A person who suffers loss or damage because an offer of securities under a

disclosure document contravenes subsection 728(1) may recover the amount of the

loss or damage from a person referred to in the following table if the loss or

damage is one that the table makes the person liable for. This is so even if

the person did not commit, and was not involved in, the contravention.

</dd> </dl>

<table><tr align="left">
  <th colspan="1" align="left">
    <div>People liable on disclosure document</div>

  </th>
  <th colspan="1" align="right">
    <div>\[operative]</div>

  </th>
